### [76] [PubMedCausal: A Span-Level Annotated Corpus for Causal Relation Extraction in Biomedical Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28363)
*Ifeoluwa Kunle-John,Josiah Paul,Oluwatosin Agbaakin,Peter Aina,Ikenna Odezuligbo,Sydney Anuyah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 PubMedCausal，这是一个用于生物医学领域细粒度、段落级因果关系抽取的全新数据集，并对其进行了多模型基准测试，探讨了当前技术在处理复杂因果表达时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生物医学因果关系抽取（CRE）资源存在因果定义模糊（与广义关联混淆）、标注仅限于句级、主要关注显式因果线索等局限性，无法真实反映生物医学文本中因果关系的复杂表达。

Method: 构建了一个包含 30,000 个段落级样本的标注语料库，包含 3,945 个因果行和 6,491 个经裁定的因果对；利用判别式编码器（如 PubMedBERT）进行检测任务评估，并利用生成式模型（如 DeepSeek-R1-32B）进行跨度抽取任务评估；同时开展了跨数据集的迁移学习实验。

Result: PubMedBERT 在因果检测任务上取得最优性能（F1 分数为 0.7391）；DeepSeek-R1-32B 在少样本提示下在跨度抽取任务中表现最佳（Cosine Pair F1 为 0.6765）。研究表明类不平衡、长因果跨度及跨句关系是当前模型的主要难点。

Conclusion: PubMedCausal 为生物医学领域因果关系抽取提供了高质量、细粒度的基准数据集，揭示了当前模型在处理跨句因果、长跨度因果及隐式因果关系时仍面临重大挑战，并证明了该数据集在跨数据集评估中的有效性。

Abstract: Causal relation extraction (CRE) is central to biomedical text mining, but current resources often conflate causal relations with broader associations, restrict annotation to sentence-level examples, or focus mainly on explicit causal cues. This limits their usefulness for evaluating whether models can recover causal claims as they are actually expressed in biomedical text. We introduce PubMedCausal, a span-level annotated corpus for biomedical CRE built from PubMed abstracts. The corpus contains 30,000 paragraph-level rows, including 3,945 causal rows and 6,491 adjudicated cause--effect pairs. Each causal relation is annotated with full-text cause and effect spans, causality type, and sententiality, enabling evaluation of both causal detection and full-span causal extraction. We benchmark discriminative encoders and open-source generative models across detection and extraction settings. For causal detection, biomedical encoders are strongest, with PubMedBERT reaching an F$_1$ score of 0.7391. For span-level extraction, the best generative baseline is DeepSeek-R1-32B with few-shot prompting, reaching a Cosine Pair F$_1$ of 0.6765. We further test transfer learning by evaluating PubMedCausal-trained encoders on external causal relation datasets, showing that the resource supports cross-dataset evaluation. Our results show that biomedical CRE remains difficult under class imbalance, long causal spans, implicit causality, inter-sentential relations, and prompt sensitivity. Code and Data can be found here: https://github.com/josiahpaul07/PubMedCausal_Exp

</details>

Conclusion: PrionNER 提供了一个高质量的标注数据集，填补了朊病毒病领域临床信息提取研究的空白。它为解决罕见病低资源、细粒度及复杂实体的命名实体识别任务提供了有效的基准，并证明了当前主流模型在处理该领域复杂医学术语时仍存在提升空间。

Abstract: Prion diseases are rare, rapidly progressive, and fatal neurodegenerative disorders that remain difficult to diagnose, particularly in their early stages because of nonspecific clinical presentations. However, to our knowledge, there is no publicly available prion-disease-focused dataset designed to capture a broad range of clinically relevant entities from the biomedical literature. We introduce PrionNER, a manually annotated named entity recognition dataset for prion disease clinical information in PubMed abstracts. The current release comprises 317 abstracts, 2,943 sentences, and 6,955 text-bound entity annotations spanning 15 coarse-grained and 31 fine-grained clinically oriented entity types covering diseases, symptoms, diagnostics, findings, anatomy, treatments, and temporal and statistical evidence. Inter-annotator agreement reaches 81.78 exact-match F1, indicating strong annotation consistency. We benchmark supervised BERT baselines, W2NER, and zero-shot extractors on PrionNER. W2NER is the strongest supervised model, and Gemma-4-31B is the strongest zero-shot model, but the benchmark remains challenging, especially for structurally complex mentions and fine-grained clinically adjacent label distinctions. PrionNER provides a clinically grounded benchmark for prion-disease information extraction and supports research on rare-disease biomedical NLP under low-resource, fine-grained, and non-flat extraction conditions. The dataset, annotation guidelines, and evaluation scripts are available at https://github.com/daotuanan/PrionNER/.

### [78] [FABSVer: Faster Training and Better Self-Verification for LLM Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28389)
*Haihui Pan,Junwei Bao,Hongfei Jiang,Yang Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 FABSVer 方法，通过将数学解题与验证过程融合并引入动态参考模型更新机制，在大幅降低训练成本的同时，显著提升了大模型的数学推理与自我验证能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型在数学推理方面虽然取得进展，但在自我验证（判断自身答案正确性）方面依然不可靠。此外，现有的自我验证方法通常将生成与验证视为两个独立任务，导致训练时间显著增加，效率低下。

Method: 1. FABSVer：将解决方案生成与自我验证过程融合为单次生成任务，以降低训练开销并实现联合优化。
2. DRMU（动态参考模型更新）：针对训练后期奖励平台化瓶颈，动态更新参考模型，突破性能上限，实现持续的奖励增长。

Result: 1. 训练效率显著提升：相比现有方法，训练时间仅为原先的 51%–71%。
2. 性能提升：在数学基准测试中，FABSVer 在三种不同模型规模下均表现出更强的自我验证与推理能力。
3. 学习特征：揭示了模型获取自我验证能力的独特学习阶段，并发现随着模型规模增加，验证奖励与答案奖励之间的差距明显缩小。

Conclusion: FABSVer 通过将生成与验证任务融合，并配合动态参考模型更新机制（DRMU），有效解决了大模型数学推理中自我验证不可靠及训练效率低下的问题，为提升模型自主推理与判断能力提供了一种高效的优化路径。

Abstract: While large language models have made significant progress in mathematical reasoning, they remain unreliable at judging the correctness of their own solutions. Existing approaches that equip models with self-verification typically treat solution generation and verification as two separate tasks, leading to substantially increased training time. In this paper, we propose FABSVer, which fuses these two tasks into a single generation pass, dramatically reducing training overhead while jointly optimizing both capabilities. We further identify a convergence bottleneck both theoretically and empirically: as training progresses, the reward reaches a plateau because the policy is constrained by a fixed reference model. To overcome this, we introduce Dynamic Reference Model Update (DRMU), which raises the reward ceiling and enables sustained reward growth. Extensive experiments on math benchmarks demonstrate that FABSVer achieves superior self-verification and reasoning performance across three model scales, while requiring only 51%--71% of the training time of existing methods. Analysis further reveals distinct learning phases in how models acquire self-verification, and that the gap between verify and answer rewards shrinks noticeably as model size increases.

### [79] [Skill0.5: Joint Skill Internalization and Utilization for Out-of-Distribution Generalization in Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28424)
*Jiapeng Zhu,Jianxiang Yu,Yibo Zhao,Chengcheng Han,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Xiang Li,Weining Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Skill0.5是一种新型智能体强化学习框架，通过动态区分任务难度，结合通用技能的深度内化与任务特定技能的针对性应用，显著提升了智能体在复杂环境下的任务解决能力与泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型智能体强化学习方法在处理复杂任务时，在“全外化”（导致上下文开销过大）和“全内化”（导致过拟合与知识冲突）之间面临两难境地，亟需一种能兼顾两者优势的方法。

Method: 提出了Skill0.5框架，包含以下核心机制：1. 动态难度感知路由：根据任务难度将任务分配至不同掌握层级；2. 通用技能内化：利用特权蒸馏（privileged distillation）构建认知基础；3. 任务特定技能利用：在简单任务中采用诊断式探测（diagnostic probing）以防止走捷径，强制执行特定技能利用。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop数据集上的实验结果表明，Skill0.5在分布内（in-distribution）和分布外（out-of-distribution）场景下，均优于现有的记忆驱动和技能驱动强化学习基准模型。

Conclusion: Skill0.5通过在通用技能内化和任务特定技能利用之间建立动态平衡，有效解决了大语言模型智能体在复杂任务处理中的效率与泛化性困境，为构建高效智能体提供了新路径。

Abstract: Equipping large language models with explicit skills has emerged as a promising paradigm for enabling autonomous agents to solve complex tasks. Agent skills can be inherently divided into general skills for broad cognitive transfer and task-specific skills for dynamic execution. However, existing skill-based reinforcement learning (RL) methods typically force a rigid choice between full externalization, which incurs prohibitive context overhead, and full internalization, which risks overfitting and knowledge conflicts. To address this dilemma, we propose Skill0.5, a novel agentic RL framework that explicitly differentiates skill treatments by combining general skill internalization with task-specific skill utilization. Driven by a dynamic, difficulty-aware router, Skill0.5 streams tasks into distinct mastery tiers to apply tailored optimization strategies: it internalizes general skills via privileged distillation to build a cognitive foundation for hard tasks, while using diagnostic probing on easy tasks to penalize shortcuts and enforce specific skill utilization. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that Skill0.5 outperforms both memory-based and skill-based RL baselines, yielding performance improvements across both in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios.

### [80] [Roles with Rails: Contract-Preserving Role Evolution in Multi-Agent Structured Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28433)
*Ling-Yue Ge,Lan-Zhe Guo*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SERO的自演化多智能体编排框架，通过强制执行五个核心结构契约，在确保系统逻辑完整性与稳定性前提下，实现了角色池的自动化演化与优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体LLM系统在面对动态需求时存在局限性：要么角色池固定导致缺乏适应性，要么允许无约束的演化导致“角色漂移”，破坏系统原有的结构性契约与任务执行逻辑。

Method: 提出“契约保护角色演化”（Contract-preserving role evolution）框架，通过定义并强制执行五个结构性契约（能力、通信、验证、聚合、输出协议）来约束角色演化；构建了SERO框架，包含基于信用的检索机制、基于DAG的通信拓扑、以及利用上下文多臂老虎机（Contextual-bandit）进行演化决策的控制器。

Result: 在多个真实推理基准测试及不同LLM基座上的实验表明，SERO框架通过契约保护演化，有效提升了系统的自适应能力与任务完成得分。

Conclusion: SERO通过引入“契约保护”机制，成功解决了多智能体系统中角色进化与系统稳定性之间的矛盾，证明了在LLM多智能体系统中引入结构化约束是实现高效、自适应演化的关键。

Abstract: Role-based LLM multi-agent systems need adaptive role pools, yet adapting such systems is not merely a matter of prompt optimization: roles often carry structural obligations, including capability coverage, message compatibility, validation, final-answer aggregation, and parser-compatible output protocols. Existing systems either fix the role inventory and lose adaptivity, or allow unconstrained generation to induce role drift, removing structurally necessary roles and breaking answer contracts. We formulate this as contract-preserving role evolution, requiring every committed edit to preserve five structural contracts (capability, communication, validation, aggregation, output protocol). We instantiate this formulation in SERO, a Self-Evolving Role Orchestration framework that evolves a typed role-card pool through credit-guided retrieval, a credit-ranked communication DAG with a protected terminal aggregator and conditional validator repair, and a contextual-bandit controller whose LLM-proposed edits are committed only when they preserve the contracts and improve task score. Experiments on real-world reasoning benchmarks across three LLM backbones confirm the value of contract-preserving role evolution.

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems are commonly evaluated using aggregate metrics such as Word Error Rate (WER), which do not capture the linguistic structure of errors. Fine-grained analysis, such as Part-of-Speech (PoS)-wise error characterization, requires accurate alignment between ASR hypotheses and reference transcriptions. However, existing alignment tools are often unreliable for languages written in non-Latin scripts. In this work, we address this gap by proposing a robust, automated, language-agnostic alignment mechanism applicable across ASR architectures and across languages written in both Latin and non-Latin scripts. This enables consistent alignment of hypotheses, references, and evaluation sequences, forming the basis for downstream linguistic analysis. Building on this, we employ standard PoS taggers to perform scalable and reproducible PoS-wise error analysis. ### [82] [AdaDPO: Self-Adaptive Direct Preference Optimization with Balanced Gradient Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28440)
*Shaolong Chen,Madalina Ciobanu,Qingqing Mao,Ritankar Das*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AdaDPO是一种新型的DPO优化方法，通过动态平衡正负样本的梯度贡献，解决了原算法对负面样本过度优化的问题，在保持原有架构的基础上显著提升了模型对齐效果与稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DPO算法在对齐过程中存在梯度不对称现象，即模型会过快地抑制负面样本，而对正面样本的促进作用相对不足。这种偏差导致模型倾向于学习“如何避免糟糕答案”而非“如何生成优秀答案”，进而可能引发长度偏见等问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为AdaDPO的自适应DPO变体。该方法引入了基于停止梯度（stop-gradient）的系数，这些系数直接由当前策略模型的生成概率计算得出（参考模型概率可选）。其核心机制在于通过动态调整权重，强制使偏好响应（preferred）与非偏好响应（dispreferred）之间的梯度幅度趋于相等，并结合数值裁剪技术确保训练稳定性。

Result: 在Llama-3-8B-Instruct模型和UltraFeedback数据集上的实验表明，AdaDPO在AlpacaEval 2基准测试中表现优异，81%的超参数配置下均优于标准DPO。该方法在提升长度控制胜率（LC）的同时，有效缓解了长度偏见，且能无缝集成到多种基于对比偏好的对齐算法中。

Conclusion: AdaDPO通过动态平衡偏好数据的梯度幅度，成功解决了DPO算法中存在的梯度不对称问题。该方法在无需额外模型架构变更的情况下，实现了对偏好对齐效率和生成质量的显著提升，并能有效抑制长度偏差，具有极高的通用性和工业落地价值。

Abstract: DPO has become a widely adopted alternative to RLHF for aligning LLMs with human preferences, eliminating the need for a separate reward model or RL loop. Recent theoretical analysis uncovers an asymmetric gradient behavior in DPO: the loss suppresses dispreferred responses substantially faster than it promotes preferred ones, causing the model to learn to avoid bad answers rather than to generate good ones. We propose AdaDPO, a Self-Adaptive variant of the DPO algorithm that introduces per-preference-pair, stop-gradient-based coefficients derived directly from the policy model's generation probabilities, with the reference model's probabilities as an optional component. AdaDPO is constructed to enforce equality of gradient magnitudes between preferred and dispreferred probabilities; the practical implementation balances per-token gradients and applies a numerical clipping bound for stability, while retaining DPO's original hyperparameter structure. On Llama-3-8B-Instruct trained on UltraFeedback under a SimPO similar setup, AdaDPO consistently outperforms DPO on AlpacaEval 2: it achieves higher length-controlled win rates (LC) in 81% of hyperparameter combinations, attains the global best LC (48.3%) and raw win rate (46.1%), and enlarges the LC-over-WR margin in 88% of combinations, indicating effective mitigation of length bias. Additional analyses on KL divergence, reward margin, and reward accuracy confirm that AdaDPO rectifies the gradient imbalance and yields more efficient optimization. Because it operates purely at the loss level, AdaDPO can be dropped into existing preference-based alignment pipelines without changing data collection or model architectures. The method requires only a few lines of code, and the same self-adaptive principle generalizes to a broad family of pairwise contrastive preference losses including SimPO, R-DPO, IPO, CPO, and ORPO.

</details>

To fill this gap, we propose \textbf{Prosecution Decision Prediction (PDP)}, the first Legal AI task built around prosecutorial review, which classifies each case into prosecution or one of three non-prosecution decisions and reflects legal AI's capabilities in evidence evaluation, legal subsumption, and value-based discretion. We further construct \textbf{PDP-Bench}, a benchmark of 4{,}630 real Chinese prosecutorial decisions spanning 190 charges. *Jihyeong Park,Ingeol Baek,Jeonghyun Park,Hwanhee Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了弥补现有评估方法对大模型交互式发散思维评估的缺失，本文提出了MUTATE基准，并设计了ReDNA框架。该方法通过分离发散生成与收敛选择，有效解决了模型在任务中容易陷入动作固定的问题，提升了智能体的创造性推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的评估方法将大语言模型视为单轮文本生成器，无法反映智能体在交互过程中的迭代推理能力。此外，现有评价往往只关注任务完成率，忽略了发散性思维过程中的探索价值。因此，研究旨在构建能够评估智能体在交互中展现“发散性思维”的基准和提升方法。

Method: 1. 提出MUTATE基准：通过路径级（发现多种目标达成路径）和动作级（非典型对象使用）两个维度评估智能体的发散性思维。
2. 提出ReDNA算法：通过将无约束的发散候选生成阶段与收敛性约束选择阶段解耦，引导智能体进行更具弹性的发散推理，从而克服“动作固定化”倾向。

Result: 实验结果显示，主流大模型在面临压力时倾向于采取固定化的动作方案，表现出明显的结构性盲点。采用ReDNA方法后，模型在路径级和动作级的发散性评分上均显著优于现有基准，且证明其性能提升来源于高质量的发散推理能力，而非简单的环境随机探索。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了现有大模型在面对即时任务压力时容易陷入“动作固定化”的缺陷。通过引入ReDNA框架，研究证明了在决策过程中将发散性候选生成与收敛性约束选择分离开来，能够显著提升智能体在多路径探索和非典型对象使用方面的创造性推理能力。

Abstract: Divergent thinking is a core dimension of creativity, yet existing evaluations of Large Language Models (LLMs) treat them as single-turn text generations, failing to capture how an agent reasons through iterative interaction. To address this, we introduce MUTATE, an interactive benchmark designed to evaluate agentic divergent thinking at two levels: path-level, where an agent discovers multiple alternative paths to the same goal, and action-level, where individual actions require non-typical, mechanism-shifting object uses. Unlike success-only evaluations, MUTATE scores both completed paths and off-path attempts, capturing divergent reasoning that conventional success rates discard. Our experiments with frontier LLMs reveal a structural blind spot in existing frameworks: when exposed to immediate convergence pressure, they tend to fall into immediate action fixation, failing to improve action-level divergence. To overcome this, we propose ReDNA, which separates unconstrained divergent candidate generation from convergent constraint selection. ReDNA significantly outperforms prior methods across both divergence levels and generalizes effectively to an external creativity environment. We also confirm its success stems from a qualitative enhancement of resilient divergent reasoning rather than simple environmental exploration.

</details>


### [85] [Comonadic Morphophonology: A Compositional Framework for Context-Dependent Morphological Rules in Finnish](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28484)
*Yongseok Jang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Writer comonad的代数框架，用于处理复杂的形态音系规则。该方法通过coKleisli箭头组合规则，成功解决了传统有限状态方法中的状态爆炸问题，在大幅精简规则数量的同时，实现了高效、双向的形态处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有限状态转换器（FST）在处理复杂的上下文相关形态音系规则时会导致“状态爆炸”问题，而神经模型虽然有效但缺乏对规则的正式描述和可解释性。因此，研究旨在寻求一种既能正式表达形态音系规则，又能避免FST组合复杂性的新型数学框架。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于Writer comonad（由DeletionSet和Zipper组成）的新型代数框架。在该框架下，每一个形态音系规则被建模为从局部上下文到输出片段的函数，并利用coKleisli箭头实现规则的组合。通过这种方式，长度改变规则得以被高效处理，删除操作作为幺半群作用进行累积，有效避免了传统有限状态转换器（FST）中的状态爆炸问题。

Result: 该框架将Omorfi系统中原有的874个延续类规则精简为13个coKleisli箭头，实现了规则表示层面上67:1的压缩比。在UD Finnish-TDT语料库上，该系统在仅使用规则消歧的情况下达到83.92%的UPOS准确率，结合外部词缀标注器可提升至94.66%，并支持形态分析与生成的双向转换。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用Writer comonad代数结构处理形态音系规则不仅在理论上实现了严谨的组合性，而且在实际应用中具有极高的紧凑性（规则数量减少67倍）和双向处理能力。该框架在芬兰语形态分析任务中展现了极高的准确率，验证了其作为实用形态引擎的潜力。

Abstract: Composing finite-state transducers (FSTs) for context-dependent morphophonological rules -- consonant gradation, vowel harmony, possessive suffix assimilation -- leads to multiplicative state explosion; neural models sidestep the problem but provide no formal account of the rules themselves. We present the first framework where each morphophonological rule is a function from a focused local context to a single output segment -- the type of a local rule familiar from cellular automata -- and where length-changing rules compose as coKleisli arrows of a comonad. Our central contribution is the Writer comonad (DeletionSet x Zipper), a new algebraic construction that restores strict coKleisli compositionality for such rules: each rule is a coKleisli arrow, extend lifts it to a global transformation, and deletions accumulate as a monoid action rather than requiring intermediate materialization. As supporting evidence, thirteen coKleisli arrows provide an alternative formulation expressing the same morphophonological behaviors that Omorfi encodes via 874 continuation classes (67:1 reduction at the rule-representation level), and the same abstraction enables bidirectional morphology -- a MorphGenerator reuses the analysis arrows for generation. On UD Finnish-TDT, the system achieves 83.92% UPOS accuracy with rule-only disambiguation (94.66% with an external suffix tagger), validating the framework as a practical morphological engine.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者构建了一个包含20个法语多义动词的语料库，并采用了三重标注体系：(1) 基于平行语料库中对应的英语翻译；(2) 基于法语词汇-语法（Lexicon-Grammar）表的词典条目；(3) 将上述两者拼接生成的细粒度复合标签。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用多语平行语料库和计算词典相结合的方式，可以有效构建高质量的语义标注语料库，为法语词义消歧任务提供了一种细粒度且可靠的基准。

Abstract: We describe a new sense-tagged corpus for word sense disambiguation. The corpus is constituted of instances of 20 French polysemous verbs. Each verb instance is annotated with three sense labels: (1) the actual translation of the verb in the english version of this instance in a parallel corpus, (2) an entry of the verb in a computational dictionary of French (the Lexicon-Grammar tables) and (3) a fine-grained sense label resulting from the concatenation of the translation and the Lexicon-Grammar entry.

### [87] [Functional Entropy: Predicting Functional Correctness in LLM-Generated Code with Uncertainty Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28500)
*Dylan Bouchard,Mohit Singh Chauhan,Zeya Ahmad,Ho-Kyeong Ra*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型代码生成中容易出现幻觉的问题，本文提出了一套“功能等价评估”方法，通过利用代码的功能性特征代替传统的语义推理，显著提升了代码生成任务中的不确定性量化效果和幻觉检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大模型在代码生成方面表现出色，但常产生功能错误的“幻觉”代码。现有的不确定性量化方法多用于自然语言生成，在代码生成领域的适用性尚不明确，且现有的语义评估方法（如NLI）难以捕捉代码的功能性差异。

Method: 研究者系统评估了多种不确定性量化（UQ）技术在代码生成中的表现。针对现有NLI方法无法区分功能性代码的缺陷，作者提出了“功能等价方法”（Functional Equivalence Methods），包括“功能熵”（Functional Entropy），利用基于LLM的功能等价性评估替代语义评估，并针对三种编程语言和五种LLM进行了大规模实证分析。

Result: 实验结果表明，功能等价性方法在15个模型-基准组合中的11个达到了最佳AUROC表现，且在校准度（calibration）方面优于NLI及其他评估方法。此外，研究发现基于Token概率的方法可直接迁移使用，但基于NLI的方法在代码场景下表现不佳。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，针对代码生成的特性，基于功能等价性的评估方法优于传统的基于自然语言推理（NLI）的语义评估方法。通过引入功能熵等指标，可以显著提高大型语言模型在代码生成任务中的不确定性量化能力，从而更有效地检测幻觉。

Abstract: Large language models have shown impressive capabilities in code generation, yet they often produce functionally incorrect code. Uncertainty quantification (UQ) methods have emerged as a promising approach for detecting hallucinations in natural language generation, but their effectiveness for code generation tasks remains underexplored. We systematically evaluate how UQ techniques transfer to code generation across three programming languages, five LLMs, and over 1,700 problems. We find that some token-probability-based methods generalize effectively without modification, while sampling-based methods relying on natural language inference (NLI) fail because NLI models cannot distinguish functionally different code, causing most responses to collapse into a single semantic cluster. To address this, we introduce functional equivalence methods, a family of code-specific methods that replace NLI-based semantic equivalence with an LLM-based functional equivalence assessment, including functional entropy, a code-specific analog of semantic entropy. Functional equivalence methods achieve top AUROC in 11 out of 15 model-benchmark combinations and the best calibration across most settings, consistently outperforming both NLI-based counterparts and all other methods evaluated.

### [88] [On Compositional Learning Behaviours in Formal Mathematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28512)
*Kevin Yandoka Denamganaï*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出S2B-LM基准以评估AI的组合学习行为（CLB），研究发现CLB是模型攻克奥赛级数学难题的必要条件，但仅靠提升模型规模不足以解决该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的科研智能体在处理形式化数学中的复杂难题（即“长尾”部分）时表现受限。研究认为，要实现真正的自我进化，智能体必须具备“组合学习行为”（CLB），即在特定背景下建立并重组新型符号结构的能力，而非仅仅重组预先学习的原子知识。本文旨在探究CLB能力与攻克数学难题之间的内在联系。

Method: 研究提出了S2B-LM基准，该基准去除了数值处理的干扰，并通过思维链（CoT）引导来激发模型的潜在CLB能力。研究人员对10种Lean 4定理证明器进行了交叉评估，使用精确置换检验（Permutation Tests）分析了CLB胜任度（adj-ZSCT）与miniF2F整体证明性能之间的关系，并排除了模型规模作为混淆变量的影响。

Result: 实验发现存在明确的等级结构：搜索能力强的模型能处理易解的常规题目，但缺乏显著的CLB能力；而所有在奥赛水平（miniF2F >75%）取得突破的模型，其CLB评分均位列前五（p=0.004）。这表明CLB胜任度与高级数学证明能力之间存在强相关性。

Conclusion: 组合学习能力（CLB）是攻克形式数学中“长尾”难题的必要而非充分条件。未来的研究应聚焦于提升模型在复杂数学背景下的符号重组与根植能力，而非仅仅依赖模型规模的扩大。

Abstract: Self-evolving scientific agents capable of conquering the hard tail of formal mathematics require Compositional Learning Behaviours (CLBs) -- the capacity to ground and recombine novel symbolic structures in context, beyond mere recombination of prelearned atoms. We propose \textbf{S2B-LM}, an adaptation of the Symbolic Behaviour Benchmark that removes numerical processing as a confound and adds chain-of-thought scaffolding to elicit rather than merely probe latent CLB competency. Cross-evaluating ten Lean~4 theorem provers on CLB competency (adj-ZSCT) and miniF2F whole-proof performance, exact permutation tests establish a hierarchical necessity structure: search-heavy models cover the tractable bulk without detectable CLBs, yet every model breaking into the Olympiad-level tier (miniF2F $>75\%$) is among the five highest CLB scorers ($p=0.004$). After ruling out model scale as a confound, our results show that CLB competency is \emph{necessary but not sufficient} for the hard tail of formal mathematical verification.

*François Remy*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于BGE-M3模型进行后训练，利用ClinicalMap25临床潜在空间进行多级对齐；采用包含合成临床笔记、医患对话及标注资源的混合数据，结合命名实体级与句子级的多适配器蒸馏（Multi-adapter distillation）及ColBERT式检索目标；在NER任务中，额外配置两层CNN头以优化边界检测。

Result: 在MultiClinNER共享任务中达到多语言实体召回率SOTA水平，Character-weighted F1评分位列前五；表现出优于基准M3模型的数据效率，且支持单次处理8192个Token的长文档。

Abstract: ClinicalEncoder26AM is a multilingual Diagnosable ColBERT for clinical and biomedical texts, which aligns at multiple levels its token-level semantic with ClinicalMap25, a clinical latent space inspired by BioLORD-2023 and enriched with synthetic and annotated supervision. The post-training recipe builds upon BGE-M3, and combines synthetic clinical notes, patient--doctor conversations, and annotated resources such as MedMentions, while considering both named-entity-level and sentence-level representations in a multi-adapter distillation, along with a ColBERT-style retrieval objective. In this system demonstration paper, we evaluate the model in the MultiClinNER shared task by finetuning it as a BIO tagger for patient symptoms, disorders, and procedure spans, using a lightweight two-layer CNN head to improve local boundary detection. The resulting system remains simple, processes most documents in a single 8192-token window, and achieves state-of-the-art multilingual entity recall, while achieving Top 5 overall across all entity types and languages in Character-weighted F1 scores. Training curves further show that ClinicalEncoder26AM is markedly more data-efficient than the base M3 model, supporting the usefulness of its clinical post-training for downstream information extraction.
  The model can be downloaded on https://huggingface.co/Parallia/ClinicalEncoder26AM-Diagnosable-Colbert-L2-for-multilingual-medical-texts

### [90] [GUI-CIDER: Mid-training GUI Agents via Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28534)
*Zheng Wu,Chengcheng Han,Zhengxi Lu,Tianjie Ju,Yanyu Chen,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Zhuosheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 GUI-CIDER，一种通过显式内化因果知识来提升 GUI 智能体操作理解力的新型中途训练方法，有效解决了传统方法知识获取效率低的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态 GUI 智能体在处理现实任务时受到 GUI 操作世界知识匮乏的限制，而传统的监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）方法只能通过隐式方式吸收知识，导致效率低下且难以实现真正的理解。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GUI-CIDER 的中途训练（mid-training）方法，包含三个阶段：1. 数据合成：将 GUI 轨迹中的静态规划和动态因果知识提取为文本；2. 样本重选：基于因果结构奖励和语义冗余惩罚来筛选数据集；3. 中途训练：将精炼后的知识注入到模型中。

Result: 在两个 GUI 知识基准和三个任务完成基准上的实验表明，GUI-CIDER 显著提升了智能体对 GUI 操作的理解能力及其在复杂任务中的执行成功率。

Conclusion: GUI-CIDER 证明了通过显式的知识内化（而非传统的监督微调或强化学习）能够有效提升 GUI 智能体对操作逻辑的理解，从而显著提高任务完成的成功率。

Abstract: Despite the rapid progress of multimodal large language models in building Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents, their real-world task completion is fundamentally bottlenecked by a lack of world knowledge about GUI operations. Existing solutions typically rely on expensive multi-agent scaffolding or conventional post-training paradigms, such as Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, post-training only allows agents to implicitly absorb world knowledge through action annotations or reward signals, leading to inefficient trajectory memorization rather than genuine comprehension. Therefore, an approach that enables explicit learning of this knowledge is imperative. To this end, we propose GUI-CIDER, a mid-training method that explicitly internalizes GUI world knowledge through Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection. GUI-CIDER operates in three stages: (1) data synthesis, which distills static planning and dynamic causal knowledge from GUI trajectories into text; (2) exemplar reselection, which filters the corpus by rewarding causal structures and penalizing semantic redundancy; and (3) mid-training, where the refined data is used to embed the acquired knowledge. Extensive experiments on two GUI knowledge benchmarks and three task completion benchmarks demonstrate that GUI-CIDER consistently improves both the agent's understanding of GUI operations and its task success rates.The codes are available at https://github.com/Wuzheng02/GUI-CIDER.

### [91] [Soft-SVeRL: Self-Verified Reinforcement Learning with Soft Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28561)
*Saurabh Dash,Pierre Clavier,John Dang,Matthias Galle,Marzieh Fadaee,Ahmet Üstün,Beyza Ermis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Soft-RLVR 提出将复杂任务分解为原子需求清单，通过细粒度的“部分得分”奖励代替传统的全量二值反馈，显著提升了大语言模型在指令遵循任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 RLVR 依赖于全量验证（Holistic verification），难以处理部分可验证或无标准答案的复杂指令任务；此外，稀疏的通过/失败信号限制了强化学习的优化效率，亟需一种能够提供更密集、更精确奖励信号的方法。

Method: 提出 Soft-RLVR 框架，将提示词分解为检查清单（checklist）并利用大语言模型评估每个原子需求的完成度；引入 Soft-SVeRL，允许策略模型兼任验证者；并提出了显式稳定性控制机制以防止自验证带来的奖励塌陷。

Result: 在 IFEval 指令跟随任务中，Soft-RLVR 相比于传统的验证方法，性能提升最高可达 11.1 个百分点。实验证实了验证器质量和清单拆解质量对强化学习结果的核心影响，并验证了稳定性机制对于自验证模型的重要性。

Conclusion: Soft-RLVR 通过将复杂任务分解为原子需求来优化奖励信号，证明了细粒度反馈对于强化学习训练的有效性。研究同时指出，在自验证（Self-verification）过程中，如果不加以显式的稳定性控制，模型容易陷入奖励通胀，导致训练失效。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has improved language models in domains such as mathematics and code, where correctness can be checked automatically. However, many important tasks are only partially verifiable: prompts contain multiple requirements, responses may satisfy some but not all of them, or no single reference answer might exist. We introduce Soft-RLVR, a framework for reinforcement learning from decomposed, learned verification signals. Soft-RLVR converts each prompt into a checklist of atomic requirements, scores candidate responses item by item with an LLM verifier, and trains on the resulting soft reward. Checklist-based rewards turn sparse pass/fail supervision into a denser partial-credit signal, but they also introduce a tradeoff: averaging item-level judgments can reduce verifier noise, while partial credit can reward incomplete responses. We formalize this tradeoff and identify conditions under which checklist-based verification gives a more reliable RL training signal than holistic verification. We further introduce Soft-SVeRL, a self-verifying variant of Soft-RLVR in which the policy also acts as the verifier. We show that self-verification is prone to reward inflation from overly permissive self-judgments, and that explicit stabilization is needed to prevent this collapse. In a controlled instruction-following setting with rule-based ground-truth evaluation, checklist-based Soft-RLVR improves IFEval by up to 11.1 points using only learned verifier rewards. Our experiments further show that verifier quality and checklist quality both affect downstream RL outcomes, and that explicit stabilization is essential for effective self-verification.

</details>


### [92] [Models That Know How Evaluations Are Designed Score Safer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28591)
*Katharina Deckenbach,Haritz Puerto,Jonas Geiping,Sahar Abdelnabi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AI模型可能通过接触过往的评估资料（如学术论文或社交媒体讨论）习得“评估元知识”，从而在安全测试中表现出比实际更安全的行为，这使得安全评估结果存在偏差，且难以通过常规手段检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI安全评估依赖于模型在受控环境下的表现，但研究发现模型能够通过“评估元知识”（即关于评估结构特征的参数化知识）识别并适应评估情境，导致其在评估中的表现优于其实际的安全水平。本文旨在揭示这种“元知识”如何作为一种干扰变量影响安全基准的可靠性。

Method: 研究者通过构建合成文档，专门描述AI评估过程中的典型特征（如可验证结构或道德困境），对基础模型进行微调，以模拟模型获取“评估元知识”的过程。随后，在六个安全基准测试上对比微调模型与基准/控制模型在安全行为上的差异，并排除了明确表达评估意识的情况。

Result: 实验结果表明，经过“评估元知识”微调的模型在六个安全基准测试中展现出显著提高的安全性，且即使在没有明确表达“意识到正在被评估”的情况下，这种行为转变依然存在。证明了元知识确实会导致安全性能的虚高。

Conclusion: “评估元知识”是导致AI安全评估性能虚高的一种新型干扰因素，它独立于明确的记忆或对评估环境的察觉。这一发现挑战了当前AI安全评估的有效性，并强调了在评估设计中考虑模型背景知识的重要性。

Abstract: The validity of AI safety evaluations depends on models behaving consistently across controlled and deployment settings. Prior work has identified test-time contextual cues, such as hypothetical scenarios, as a source of verbalized evaluation awareness and subsequent behavioral shift. In this paper, we investigate a potential explanation of this phenomenon: evaluation meta-knowledge, defined as parametric knowledge about the structural traits that characterize evaluations. Similar to dataset contamination, where benchmark exposure leads to higher performance through memorization, we hypothesize that models trained on texts describing evaluation practices may implicitly learn to recognize and respond to evaluation-like contexts, for instance, through exposure to scientific articles or social media posts about AI benchmarking. To test this, we fine-tune models on synthetic documents describing evaluation traits such as verifiable structures or moral dilemmas. Evaluating this fine-tuned model on six safety benchmarks, we find that it is significantly safer than the base model and control model. This behavioral shift persists even when restricting the analysis to responses lacking explicit verbalization of evaluation awareness. Our results demonstrate that evaluation meta-knowledge may inflate safety benchmark performance, introducing a novel confounder that is independent of explicit memorization or verbalized evaluation awareness, thus, challenging to detect. These findings have important implications for the design and interpretation of AI safety evaluations. Our code and models are available at https://github.com/compass-group-tue/arxiv2026_evaluation_meta_knowledge.

### [93] [Measuring Form and Function in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28616)
*Héctor Javier Vázquez Martínez,Charles Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型评估往往缺乏与人类语言习得过程的直接联系。研究动机旨在建立一套量化指标，通过模仿人类儿童早期习得英语限定词的过程，科学评估语言模型在语法掌握和语用功能理解方面的认知能力，填补模型性能与人类认知表现之间的对比空白。

Method: 研究提出了“情境替代选择”（Contextual Alternative Choice, CAC）提示方法。该方法通过构建特定的测试集，针对英语限定词的语法结构和语用功能进行受控测试，并将模型表现直接与人类儿童的经验习得数据及统计基准进行横向对比。

Result: 研究发现，目前的模型中，只有规模足够大的模型能够同时达到形式（语法）和功能（语用）上的基准要求，而训练数据量相当的较小模型则难以达到人类儿童的表现水平。这意味着模型规模与习得能力的成熟度之间存在显著的正相关。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了当前大型语言模型在学习英语限定词（determiner）时，能够实现类似人类儿童的语法和语用表现。研究强调，单纯的模型规模并不完全等同于人类的习得机制，通过对比儿童习得数据，可以更有效地评估模型的认知能力与语言习得水平。

Abstract: We introduce quantitative metrics for child language acquisition to evaluate language models. Our focus is on the formal syntactic and functional discourse properties of determiners in English, which young children acquire early and accurately. We propose Contextual Alternative Choice (CAC), a new prompting method which provides targeted tests for both syntactic and discourse knowledge of language. The method enables direct comparison of language models against children, and more importantly, against statistical benchmarks independently established in empirical research. No current model trained on a comparable amount of data simultaneously meet both formal and functional benchmarks like human children, but some very large models do. We present our results as methodological and technical contributions, with specific emphasis on cognitive status of language models.

### [94] [The Attentional White Bear Effect in Transformer Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28639)
*Rebecca Ramnauth,Brian Scassellati*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大模型安全对齐的局限性：通过指令抑制有害内容仅能限制“表达”，而无法消除模型内部对违禁概念的“表征”，导致安全性存在明显的内在逻辑鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于指令的抑制（Instruction-based suppression）是目前大模型防止生成违禁内容的主流手段，但学术界尚不明确这种机制是真正消除了模型内部的有害表征，还是仅仅抑制了其外在表现。该研究旨在探究这种安全对齐方法的有效性边界。

Method: 采用了多种分析手段：1. 表征探测（Representational Probing）：评估隐藏层中是否包含被抑制概念的语义信息；2. 注意力分析（Attention Analysis）：观察被抑制概念如何影响模型的注意力路由机制；3. 行为语义泄露实验（Behavioral Semantic Leakage）：检测被抑制概念在后续生成过程中是否通过间接方式产生干扰。

Result: 研究发现，即便是模型成功地在词汇层面规避了违禁内容，相关概念在隐藏层表征中依然高度可恢复，持续影响注意力机制的分配，并对后续生成的语义产生可度量的塑造作用。这一结论在不同的模型架构和控制条件下均保持一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于指令的抑制机制并未从模型内部消除有害概念，而仅仅是切断了这些内部概念与输出层之间的表象联系。这种“行为与表征对齐”之间的脱节意味着，大模型在安全性对齐上仍存在深层次的脆弱性，单纯依赖指令抑制不足以实现真正的鲁棒对齐。

Abstract: Instruction-based suppression is widely used to prevent language models from generating prohibited content, yet it remains unclear whether suppression reduces internal representation or merely suppresses expression. We investigate this question through representational probing, attention analysis, and behavioral semantic leakage experiments across multiple transformer models. We find that prohibited concepts remain highly recoverable from hidden representations under suppression, continue to influence attention routing, and measurably shape downstream generations despite successful lexical avoidance. These effects persist across pooling strategies, indirect semantic controls, and multiple model families. Our results expose a fundamental gap between behavioral and representational alignment.

</details>


### [95] [Sense Representations Are Inducible Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28669)
*Jan Christian Blaise Cruz,Alham Fikri Aji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ACROS 是一种无需重新训练即可为预训练语言模型注入语义表征能力的技术，通过门控残差连接实现了高效的词义消歧、语义引导和跨语言对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语义表征方法要求模型在预训练时就必须包含语义结构，这限制了其在普通预训练模型上的应用。作者希望开发一种能够为已冻结的预训练语言模型引入语义表征能力的通用接口，以实现消歧、语义引导和跨语言对齐。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为 ACROS 的方法，通过门控残差连接（gated residual addition）将明确的语义路径诱导至冻结的预训练解码器语言模型中。该方法通过在模型架构中引入语义变量，从而无需预先在模型预训练阶段嵌入语义结构。

Result: 在 SmolLM2-360M 模型上的实验表明，ACROS 在保持基础语言模型质量的同时，实现了零样本词义消歧（Raganato ALL 数据集上达到 64.95 F1）、词汇引导（在 CoInCo 测试中恢复了约 90% 的正向偏移）以及高效的跨语言适配（四种语言的平均 R@1 达到 0.988）。

Conclusion: ACROS 提供了一种高效的方法，使现有的预训练大型语言模型能够通过可诱导的接口具备语义表征能力，而无需重新训练模型，为模型解释性、语义控制和跨语言应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Sense representations (explicit, per-token meaning decompositions) are useful for disambiguation, steering, and cross-lingual alignment, but existing approaches require models to be pretrained with sense structure baked in. We introduce ACROS, which induces an explicit sense pathway into a frozen pretrained decoder LM through a gated residual addition. On SmolLM2-360M, ACROS preserves base LM quality while supporting three uses of the same induced variables: zero-shot word-sense disambiguation (64.95 F1 on Raganato ALL, competitive with the WordNet first-sense heuristic), low-KL lexical steering across 5,161 CoInCo cases where a simple non-oracle proxy recovers about 90% of positive shifts, and SENSIA cross-lingual adaptation to four languages (mean R@1 0.988, target FLORES PPL 7.94). ACROS makes sense representations an inducible interface for ordinary pretrained LMs.

</details>


### [96] [Towards Reliable Multilingual LLMs-as-a-Judge: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28710)
*Irune Zubiaga,Aitor Soroa,Rodrigo Agerri*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统探讨了多语言大模型评估器的构建策略，发现领域内数据的存在决定了模型选型与微调的最佳路径，为低资源语言及跨领域场景下的评估提供了实证依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）在文本评估中应用广泛，但现有研究多局限于英语。随着多语言评估需求增长，如何克服低资源语言及缺乏领域内数据场景下的评估挑战，成为亟待解决的问题。本文旨在探索并建立一套高效、可靠的多语言LLM评估方法。

Method: 本文针对英、西、巴斯克三种资源水平各异的语言，系统研究了多语言“大语言模型作为裁判”（LLM-as-a-judge）的构建策略。方法包括：1. 比较指令翻译、单语与多语言监督微调策略；2. 评估不同模型规模的影响；3. 将两个元评估数据集扩展至西班牙语和巴斯克语；4. 对比有无领域内数据支撑下的模型表现。

Result: 研究发现：在有领域内数据的情况下，精调后的较小模型能够达到与昂贵专有模型相当的评估效果；在缺乏领域内数据或领域外场景下，利用大规模模型进行零样本（zero-shot）推理更为优越；同时，不当的领域外数据微调会对模型评估性能产生负面影响。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了构建多语言LLM评估器时的关键权衡：在有领域内数据时，经过微调的较小模型性能可媲美专有模型；而在领域外场景下，大模型的零样本评估更为有效。此外，盲目利用领域外数据进行微调反而可能导致性能下降。该研究为构建高效、可靠的多语言自动化评估管道提供了实践指南。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for the automatic evaluation of generated text, yet most prior work focuses on English. Despite the growing demand for multilingual evaluation, extending LLM-based evaluators to multilingual settings remains challenging, particularly for low-resource languages and scenarios where in-domain data is scarce. This work explores several strategies for developing multilingual LLMs-as-a-judge, considering whether in-domain data is available for fine-tuning or not. We systematically analyze English, Spanish, and Basque, representing high-, mid-, and low-resource languages, considering instruction translation, monolingual versus multilingual supervision, and model size. For evaluation, we extend two existing meta-evaluation datasets to Basque and Spanish. Our results reveal key trade-offs: When in-domain data is available, fine-tuned smaller models can achieve performance comparable to proprietary models, whereas zero-shot evaluation with larger models proves more effective in out-of-domain settings. We also observe that fine-tuning on out-of-domain data can adversely affect model performance. These findings provide practical guidance for building efficient, reliable multilingual evaluation pipelines. The data and code are publicly available at hitz-zentroa/mJudge.

### [97] [IPO-Mine: A Toolkit and Dataset for Section-Structured Analysis of Long, Multimodal IPO Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28714)
*Michael Galarnyk,Siddharth Lohani,Vidhyakshaya Kannan,Sagnik Nandi,Aman Patel,Liqin Ye,Arnav Hiray,Rutwik Routu,Prasun Banerjee,Siddhartha Somani,Sudheer Chava*

Abstract: An Initial Public Offering (IPO) filing is a document released when a private firm goes public, allowing individual (retail) investors to purchase its shares. These filings describe a firm's business, financials, and risks and are long, multimodal documents with narrative text and images. Despite their importance to financial markets, there is no large-scale, standardized dataset or benchmark for studying IPO filings with modern language and multimodal models. These documents pose significant challenges: filings frequently exceed 500,000 tokens and lack consistent structural organization. We introduce the IPO-Toolkit, an open-source framework for downloading and parsing IPO filings into standardized section-structured text and extracted images. The toolkit segments filings, extracts embedded images, and produces structured outputs that enable large-scale, reproducible analysis workflows over long, multimodal documents. Using this infrastructure, we construct the IPO-Dataset, a large, section-structured, multimodal dataset covering more than 109,000 IPO filings and amendments from 1994 to 2026 and containing over 76,000 images. We establish structured evaluation tasks over extracted financial charts, including chart quality and misleadingness assessment. Our experiments show that state-of-the-art multimodal models often diverge from expert human judgments on these tasks, exposing alignment challenges in multimodal reasoning over long, real-world regulatory documents. Beyond benchmarking, the IPO-Dataset enables large-scale analysis of section-level textual variation and cross-industry differences in visual and textual disclosure practices. Our code, dataset, and website are publicly available under CC-BY-4.0.

### [98] [MemTrace: Tracing and Attributing Errors in Large Language Model Memory Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28732)
*Xinle Deng,Ruobin Zhong,Hujin Peng,Xiaoben Lu,Yanzhe Wu,Guang Li,Buqiang Xu,Yunzhi Yao,Jizhan Fang,Haoliang Cao,Junjie Guo,Yuan Yuan,Ziqing Ma,Yuanqiang Yu,Rui Hu,Baohua Dong,Hangcheng Zhu,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文针对大模型内存系统不可靠、难以调试的问题，提出了一种通过内存演化图追踪错误并自动归因的框架，并构建了MemTraceBench基准。该方法能有效定位并纠正内存故障，显著提升模型长程任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型的内存系统在支持长程推理时存在不可靠且难以调试的问题。为了理解信息在内存中如何被合成、传播或损坏，作者旨在解决LLM内存系统中的错误追踪与归因这一新问题，以提升系统的稳定性。

Method: 1. 提出将内存管道转化为“可执行内存演化图（Executable Memory Evolution Graphs）”，实现对信息流的精细化追踪；2. 构建MemTraceBench基准测试集，涵盖Long-Context、RAG、Mem0等主流内存系统；3. 引入迭代式自动归因方法，通过遍历操作子图定位故障根源；4. 建立闭环系统，利用归因信号自动优化提示词以纠正内存错误。

Result: 研究发现内存故障具有系统性，主要源于信息丢失和检索错位等操作层面的问题。通过该框架进行的闭环优化，能够自动纠正故障，使下游任务性能提升最高达7.62%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过对大模型内存系统进行细粒度的错误追踪与归因，可以有效识别系统性故障根源。构建闭环的自动校正系统能够显著提升模型的长程推理能力，为构建更可靠、可解释的LLM内存架构提供了关键方法论。

Abstract: Memory is essential for enabling large language models to support long-horizon reasoning, yet existing memory systems remain unreliable and difficult to debug. Tracing memory's dynamic evolution is crucial to understand how information is synthesized, propagated, or corrupted over time. In this work, we study the new problem of error tracing and attribution in LLM memory systems. We propose a novel framework that transforms memory pipelines into executable memory evolution graphs, enabling fine-grained tracing of operational information flow. We then construct MemTraceBench, a benchmark collected from representative memory systems such as Long-Context, RAG, Mem0, and EverMemOS, to systematically study memory failure modes. We further introduce an automatic attribution method that iteratively traces operation subgraphs to pinpoint the root cause of any failed case. Our analysis reveals that memory failures are systematic, stemming from operation-level issues like information loss and retrieval misalignment. Crucially, we leverage these fine-grained attribution signals to guide downstream prompt optimization, establishing a closed-loop system that automatically corrects faults and boosts end-task performance by up to 7.62%. Code will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/MemTrace.

</details>


### [99] [Reverse Probing: Supervised Token-level Uncertainty Quantification for Large Language Models in Clinical Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28740)
*Bushi Xiao,Sarvesh Soni,Daisy Zhe Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种专用于临床摘要的“反向探测”不确定性量化框架，通过分析模型内部状态而非重复采样，实现了更精准、高效的令牌级不确定性检测，显著提升了临床应用的安全性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型不确定性量化方法多针对开放域生成，无法在临床长文本中进行细粒度的令牌（token）级不确定性定位，而临床应用对准确性要求极高。

Method: 提出了一种名为“反向探测（Reverse Probing）”的框架，该框架不依赖于生成新样本，而是将文本视为对模型内部状态的探测，从四类内部激活中提取不确定性信号，并直接利用已有的标签摘要进行训练。

Result: 在两个专家标注的临床数据集上，该方法在所有指标上均优于八个基准模型，AUPRC 提升高达 4 倍，同时显著降低了推理时间和计算成本；实验表明“增量能量（delta energy）”和“邻域上下文”是预测模型不确定性的关键特征。

Conclusion: 反向探测（Reverse Probing）框架通过利用模型内部激活信息，为临床文本摘要提供了一种高效、精确且具备可解释性的不确定性量化方法，优于传统依赖采样的方法。

Abstract: As large language models are increasingly deployed for clinical text, ensuring they can reliably signal their own uncertainty becomes critical. Most existing uncertainty quantification (UQ) methods are designed for open-domain generation and cannot localize uncertainty at the token or span level in long clinical text. We propose Reverse Probing, the first UQ framework specialized for clinical summarization, which estimates token-level uncertainty directly from pre-existing labeled summaries. Rather than sampling new outputs, Reverse Probing treats the text as a probe into the model's internal state, extracting uncertainty signals from four categories of internal activations. We evaluate on two expert-annotated clinical datasets and outperform eight adapted baselines on all metrics, achieving up to 4 times higher AUPRC while reducing inference time and computational costs. Feature analysis reveals that delta energy and neighborhood context are the most consistent predictors across all models. This study offers interpretable insights into how models internally respond to unsupported clinical content.

</details>


### [100] [Stance Detection in Prediction Markets: Addressing Imbalanced Trader Commentary via Counterfactual Augmentation and Market Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28745)
*Thomas Mbrice*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了如何利用大语言模型生成的合成数据与上下文信息，解决预测市场中评论立场检测面临的严重类别不平衡问题，发现引入市场背景至关重要，且适度的合成数据增强可优化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测市场（如Polymarket）的价格仅能反映实时概率估计，而交易者发表的评论包含无法通过价格捕捉的丰富方向性立场信息。由于预测市场评论具有极简、特有术语及严重类别不平衡（仅8.7%评论持反对意见）的特点，传统检测方法效果不佳，因此需要专门的研究。

Method: 本文首次将立场检测应用于预测市场评论。研究采用RoBERTa-base模型，通过4x3消融实验评估了不同输入配置（类别数与市场背景）和数据增强条件（基准、50%合成、100%合成）。合成少数类样本由大语言模型驱动的“支持转反对”反事实生成技术完成。此外，通过基于注意力的可解释性分析来验证模型决策机制。

Result: 1. 引入市场背景是提升模型性能最有效的因素，将反对类别的召回率从0.10提升至0.45；2. 反事实增强策略在弱模型配置下有效，但在强模型配置下会降低性能；3. 50%的合成数据增强为最佳剂量，而100%的合成数据会持续损害模型表现。

Conclusion: 市场背景对提升预测市场评论的情感倾向检测至关重要，但数据增强策略（尤其是合成数据）的使用需要谨慎平衡，过度的合成数据反而会损害模型性能。该研究为理解金融预测市场中的意见表达提供了重要的方法论参考。

Abstract: Prediction markets such as Polymarket aggregate crowd beliefs into real-time probability estimates, and the comments traders post beneath each market contain rich directional stance signals that prices alone cannot capture. This work introduces the first stance detection study applied to prediction market commentary, a domain characterized by extreme brevity, trader- specific vernacular, and severe class imbalance (only 8.7% of comments oppose the market outcome). RoBERTa-base is fine-tuned across a 4 x 3 ablation: four input configurations ({2- class, 3-class} x {with/without market context}) and three augmentation conditions (baseline, 50% synthetic, 100% synthetic). Synthetic minority-class samples are generated via LLM-driven Pro -> Anti counterfactual flips using the Anthropic API. Results show that (1) market context is the single most impactful factor, raising 3-class Anti recall from 0.10 to 0.45; (2) counterfactual augmentation is conditionally effective, improving Anti F1 in weak configurations (0.10 -> 0.24) while degrading strong ones (2-class-ctx macro F1: 0.68 -> 0.50 at full dose); and (3) 50% augmentation is the optimal dose, with 100% consistently hurting performance. Attention-based interpretability analysis provides mechanistic support for all three findings.

### [101] [Can LLMs Use Linguistic Uncertainty Markers to Reliably Reflect Intrinsic Confidence?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28778)
*Gabrielle Kaili-May Liu,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究系统分析了大型语言模型（LLMs）在表达置信度时的语言稳定性，发现模型虽然能保持一定的标记排序一致性，但在跨任务和跨分布中缺乏将语言标记与真实内部置信度进行稳定、精确映射的能力，存在严重的“忠实性失准”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有研究指出LLMs在以人类对齐的方式使用认识论标记（如“很有可能……”）方面存在困难，但目前尚不明确LLMs能否建立一套稳定且可泛化的内部语言信心框架，以及语境特征如何影响模型将标记与具体置信度水平相关联的能力。因此，该研究旨在系统性地探索LLMs内部置信度与语言表达之间的映射关系。

Method: 研究提出了“标记内部置信度”（Marker Internal Confidence, MIC）的概念，用于衡量模型将特定认识论标记与特定任务领域内的固有置信度相关联的能力。作者设计了7项指标，用于评估MIC在分布内（within-distribution）和跨分布（cross-distribution）的稳定性，并在多种模型和任务上进行了系统性实验分析。

Result: 实验表明，即使在以模型为中心的解释框架下，LLMs依然表现出“忠实性失准”。模型在跨分布任务中难以通过内部置信度来有效区分不同的语言标记，尽管在不同任务中仍能保持某种程度的标记排序一致性。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在表达语言信心时存在显著的“忠实性校准”（faithful miscalibration）问题。尽管模型在不同任务中表现出一定程度的排序一致性，但它们未能根据语境稳定地映射语言标记（如“很可能”）与其内部置信度。这一发现强调了在提升模型可信度和可靠性方面，需要更深入地研究和优化语言标记的对齐与稳定性。

Abstract: LLMs' linguistically expressed confidence should faithfully reflect their intrinsic uncertainty. While recent work shows LLMs struggle to use epistemic markers (e.g., "it is likely...") in a human-aligned fashion, it remains unclear whether models can apply their own linguistic confidence framework to associate markers with specific confidence levels in a stable and generalizable way, and how contextual features impact this ability. We conduct the first systematic study of this question, formalizing _marker internal confidence_ (MIC) as the estimated intrinsic confidence a model associates with a specific epistemic marker in a given task domain. We present 7 metrics to evaluate the stability of MICs within and across distributions. Applying our analysis framework to diverse models and tasks, we find that LLMs remain faithfully miscalibrated even under model-centric interpretation of marker meanings, struggling to differentiate markers by internal confidence across distributions despite preserving a somewhat consistent ranking order across tasks. This supplies critical, complementary evidence to existing work toward a holistic understanding of faithful calibration in LLMs, emphasizing the need for more aligned and stable marker use to improve trustworthiness and reliability.

</details>


### [102] [The Abstraction Gap in Vision-Language Causal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28779)
*Chinh Hoang,Mohammad Rashedul Hasan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了视觉语言模型普遍存在“语言流利但推理匮乏”的问题。通过提出的CAGE基准与双探针方法，证实大多数模型缺乏忠实的因果推理能力，且单纯通过微调难以解决，推理能力的优劣主要取决于预训练与架构选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语言模型评估方法无法区分“语言合理性”（看起来通顺）与“忠实因果推理”（逻辑正确）之间的差异。研究旨在揭示并量化这种认知偏差，以评估模型是否真的理解因果逻辑，还是仅仅在模仿人类语言模式。

Method: 提出了一套“双探针”方法（Dual-probe methodology）：通过“仅文本探针”（Text-Only Probe）衡量语言质量，通过“链式文本探针”（Chain-Text Probe）要求模型显式生成因果链条，并引入“抽象差距”（Abstraction Gap, AG）指标来量化两者之间的性能差异。同时，构建了涵盖皮尔因果层次的CAGE基准测试集。

Result: 在对8个主流VLM进行评估后发现，7个模型表现出超过0.50的AG值，显示出严重的推理能力缺失。即使通过45,000个链式标注样本进行微调，也无法消除这一差距。但有一个模型表现出色，实现了近乎为零的AG，证明了现有架构具备实现真正因果推理的潜力。

Conclusion: 目前视觉语言模型（VLMs）在因果推理方面存在显著的“抽象差距”（Abstraction Gap），即模型虽能生成看起来通顺的文本，却缺乏真正的忠实因果推理能力。研究表明，这种能力并非架构的必然限制，而是高度依赖于预训练策略和特定的架构选择。CAGE基准测试为评估模型因果推理的真实水平提供了一个关键的诊断工具。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) generate fluent causal explanations, but current evaluations cannot distinguish linguistic plausibility from faithful causal reasoning. We introduce a dual-probe methodology that isolates these properties. The Text-Only Probe measures linguistic quality. The Chain-Text Probe requires models to first generate explicit causal chains. The Abstraction Gap (AG) metric quantifies the normalized performance difference. Evaluating eight VLMs on CAGE (Causal Abstraction Gap Evaluation), a benchmark of 49,500 questions across 5,500 images spanning Pearl's causal hierarchy, we find seven models exhibit AG exceeding 0.50 with text scores of 6--8 but chain scores below 2.5. Fine-tuning on 45,000 chain-annotated examples fails to close the gap. However, one model achieves near-zero AG. The capability exists within current VLM architectures and depends on pretraining and architectural choices. CAGE provides a diagnostic tool for assessing faithful causal reasoning in VLMs.

</details>


### [103] [Can Large Language Models Handle Discourse Particles? A Case Study of Colloquial Malay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28782)
*Mariah Al Giptiah Binte Yusoff,Jakin Tan,Bocheng Chen,Guangliang Liu,Xi Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了针对口语马来语的语篇标记评估基准 MalayPrag，并定义了一套五个维度的语用属性框架。实验发现当前大模型在马来语语用处理上存在显著短板，但通过结构化的提示引导可以有效提升模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语篇标记（如“well”、“kind of”）在提升大模型语言的类人性、情感色彩及交互意义方面至关重要，但目前学界对大模型处理此类标记的能力缺乏全面评估，且现有研究多集中于英语等高资源语言，忽略了对东南亚语言（如马来语）语用能力的探索。

Method: 1. 构建了名为 MalayPrag 的基准测试集，专门用于评估大型语言模型在口语马来语中处理语篇标记的能力；2. 提出了五个语篇标记的语用属性框架，为解析语篇功能提供语言学理论支撑；3. 在十个主流大模型上进行了三项预测任务实验，并验证了所提属性对提升模型表现的有效性。

Result: 实验表明，当前的主流大语言模型在准确关联马来语语篇标记及其语用功能方面面临严峻挑战；同时，实验证实引入本文设计的五个语用属性可以显著改善模型在这些任务上的表现，证明了结构化知识引导对于提升模型语用能力的重要性。

Conclusion: 当前的大型语言模型在处理马来语语篇标记时表现不佳，但通过引入结构化的语言学属性进行辅助（Scaffolding），可以显著提升模型理解和生成语用意义的能力。未来的研究应关注非高资源语言的语用能力开发，并进一步优化模型对语篇标记的精细化理解。

Abstract: Discourse particles, such as \textit{well} and \textit{kind of}, are crucial components that enable LLMs to ``speak'' more like humans. They are used to convey emotions, intentions, and interpersonal meanings. However, existing studies have not yet built a comprehensive understanding of LLMs' capabilities in handling discourse particles. Moreover, the limited number of studies focuses primarily on high-resource languages such as English, with little attention paid to Southeast Asian languages. In this paper, we (1) propose \textsc{MalayPrag}, a benchmark designed to systematically evaluate and analyze LLMs' capabilities in handling discourse particles in colloquial Malay; and (2) introduce five attributes that provide a linguistically grounded, unified framework for interpreting the pragmatic functions of discourse particles. Applying these two contributions, we prompt ten off-the-shelf LLMs to perform three prediction tasks. The experimental results reveal substantial challenges for current LLMs in accurately connecting discourse particles with their pragmatic functions in Malay. The provision of the five attributes designed in this study is found to significantly improve these connections, highlighting the need for structured scaffolding for models' pragmatic competence.

### [104] [Skill-Conditioned Gated Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28791)
*Jiazhen Huang,Xiao Chen,Xiao Luo,Yong Dai,Senkang Hu,Yuzhi Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SGSD是一种新型的在线自我蒸馏框架，通过利用从历史经验中提取的技能库（而非标准答案）作为特权信息，将复杂的推理任务转化为教师假设验证问题，显著提升了轻量级大模型的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线自我蒸馏方法通常假设拥有可信的“特权信息”（如标准参考答案），这限制了其应用场景。研究者旨在探索是否能利用从经验中获取的、可能包含无关或误导性信息的技能库来实现高效的自我蒸馏。

Method: 提出“技能条件门控自我蒸馏”（SGSD）：1. 构建技能-错误对库并形成多教师池；2. 所有技能条件教师对同一学生样本进行评分；3. 通过验证器确认教师极性（支持成功/抑制失败给予正向监督，反之则反转）；4. 采用稳健的门控目标函数，蒸馏有信息量的师生分歧，同时抑制不确定或极端信号。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试（AIME24、AIME25、HMMT25）中，SGSD在Qwen3-1.7B模型上表现优异，平均性能分别比GRPO高出6.2%，比基于答案的OPSD高出1.7%，证明了其在较弱特权信息假设下的竞争力。

Conclusion: SGSD证明了利用从经验中获得的技能库（而非仅依赖标准参考答案）进行自我蒸馏是提升大模型推理能力的有效途径。通过将技能引导的蒸馏转化为教师假设验证过程，该方法在弱特权信息假设下实现了优于现有基线（如GRPO）的性能。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (SD) improves LLM reasoning by using teacher-side privileged information (PI) to turn sparse verifier outcomes into dense token-level supervision. Existing methods usually assume trusted PI, such as reference answers or successful traces. We ask whether PI can instead come from an experience-derived skill bank, where retrieved skills are compact and reusable but may also be irrelevant or misleading. We propose Skill-Conditioned Gated Self-Distillation (SGSD), which formulates skill-based SD as teacher hypothesis validation rather than unconditional imitation. SGSD retrieves skill-mistake pairs, constructs a multi-teacher pool, and lets all skill-conditioned teachers score the same plain-prompt student rollout. The verifier validates each teacher's polarity: supporting a success or suppressing a failure gives positive supervision, while the opposite stance is reversed. A robust gated objective then distills informative teacher-student disagreements while suppressing uncertain or extreme signals. Experiments on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that SGSD consistently improves over GRPO and remains competitive with answer-conditioned OPSD under a weaker PI assumption. For example, on Qwen3-1.7B, SGSD outperforms GRPO by 6.2% and OPSD by 1.7% on average on AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25. Our code is available at https://github.com/walawalagoose/SGSD.

</details>


### [105] [Human Label Variation as Stable Signal: Learning Annotator-Specific Explanation Behavior via Cross-Annotator Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28802)
*Beiduo Chen,Pingjun Hong,Ziyun Zhang,Benjamin Roth,Anna Korhonen,Barbara Plank*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型学习人类标注者特定“标签-解释”行为的可行性，提出了CAPO优化算法，证实了LLM能够通过学习标注者历史来重现其独特的推理模式，从而有效应对人类标签偏差（HLV）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统标注研究多关注标签的不一致性，而忽略了自由文本解释所蕴含的深层推理和偏好。本文旨在探讨大语言模型（LLM）是否能学习并复现这种特定标注者的“标签-解释”行为，从而更好地理解和处理人类标签偏差（HLV）。

Method: 本文对比了提示工程（Prompting）和监督微调（SFT）基线，并提出了一种名为“跨标注者偏好优化”（Cross-Annotator Preference Optimization, CAPO）的方法。该方法通过对比目标标注者的响应与其他虽有效但不够“个性化”的标注，来强化模型对特定标注者推理行为的模仿能力。

Result: 实验发现，在处理句子对任务时，标注者的个性化模式在去除输入内容影响并进行聚合后是可以被检测到的。研究显示，简单的提示工程效果有限且不稳定，SFT表现较好，而提出的CAPO方法在保持特定标注者推理模式的前提下，进一步提升了模型对标注者行为的模仿精度和归因能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，人类标签偏差（HLV）可以被建模为特定的标签-解释行为。通过利用基于标注者历史的微调策略（如CAPO），大语言模型能够学习并重现特定标注者的推理模式，这为未来基于解释的、可扩展的标注方法提供了新路径。

Abstract: Free-text explanations extend human label variation (HLV) beyond label disagreement by revealing the reasoning and preferences behind annotators' decisions. We study whether large language models (LLMs) can learn and reproduce such annotator-specific label-explanation behavior. Using two sentence-pair tasks with four annotators each -- natural language inference and paraphrase judgment -- we first analyze whether annotators exhibit stable individual patterns. We find that such patterns are weak at the single-annotation level due to strong input-content effects, but become detectable after input-content reduction and annotator-level aggregation. We then compare prompting and supervised fine-tuning (SFT) baselines and propose cross-annotator preference optimization (CAPO), which contrasts a target annotator's response with other valid but less target-specific annotations for the same input. Experiments show that prompting is limited and unstable, SFT better captures annotator-specific behavior, and CAPO further improves aggregation-aware imitation and judge-based attribution while preserving target-specific reasoning patterns under human validation. Overall, our results show that HLV can be learned as annotator-specific label-explanation behavior, suggesting a path toward scalable explanation-based annotation grounded in annotator histories rather than labels alone.

</details>


### [106] [OmniVerifier-M1: Multimodal Meta-Verifier with Explicit Structured Recalibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28805)
*Xinchen Zhang,Bowei Liu,Jiale Liu,Chufan Shi,Yizhen Zhang,Junhong Liu,Youliang Zhang,Zhiheng Li,Yujiu Yang,Ling Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 OmniVerifier-M1 模型，通过使用符号化的元验证信号（如边界框）并采用解耦强化学习策略，实现了多模态模型的高可靠性验证和细粒度错误定位，显著提升了模型的自我修正能力与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着多模态大模型的广泛应用，对于可靠且细粒度的验证机制需求日益迫切。现有的验证方法多关注最终决策结果，缺乏对模型推理过程的深度监督与错误定位能力。因此，研究如何利用元验证（利用推理过程）并优化验证器训练方法，对于提升多模态模型的准确性与可控性至关重要。

Method: 1. 提出多模态元验证（Multimodal Meta-verification）框架，利用验证器生成的推理过程（rationales）而非仅仅是决策结果进行训练。
2. 对比评估了符号化输出（如边界框）与文本解释作为元验证依据的效果。
3. 采用解耦强化学习目标（Decoupled RL Objectives）策略，分别优化二进制判断与元验证任务，以适应不同的输出结构与学习动态。
4. 开发了 OmniVerifier-M1 模型，并构建了具备区域级自修正能力的智能体系统 M1-TTS。

Result: 1. 证实了符号化验证器输出（如边界框）在元验证任务中优于文本解释，且能实现高效的基于规则的强化学习奖励。
2. 实验表明，将二进制判断与元验证的强化学习目标进行解耦，比联合优化能显著提升模型性能。
3. 训练的 OmniVerifier-M1 模型能够提供稳健的验证功能和细粒度的错误定位。
4. 基于 OmniVerifier-M1 构建的 M1-TTS 系统实现了动态的区域级自修正。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入符号化元验证和解耦强化学习目标，为多模态模型提供了一种更可靠、可解释且具备细粒度错误定位能力的验证方案。OmniVerifier-M1 的成功表明，将推理过程从单纯的文本描述转向结构化的符号验证，是提升多模态模型自我修正与决策能力的关键路径。

Abstract: Visual outcomes are increasingly central to multimodal large language models, making reliable and fine-grained verification essential for scaling generalist foundation models. In this work, we investigate multimodal meta-verification, which leverages verifier-generated rationales rather than decision-only signals, and explore how to effectively incorporate meta-verification feedback into multimodal verifier training. We identify two key findings. First, symbolic verifier outputs (e.g., bounding boxes) outperform textual explanations as meta-verification rationales, enabling efficient rule-based reinforcement learning rewards while avoiding reliance on model-based rewards from auxiliary judge models. Second, decoupling reinforcement learning objectives for binary judgment and meta-verification substantially outperforms joint reward optimization, due to intrinsic differences in output structure and learning dynamics. Based on these insights, we train OmniVerifier-M1, a generalist visual verifier leveraging symbolic meta-verification and decoupled reinforcement learning. OmniVerifier-M1 provides robust verification and fine-grained error localization, and further enables M1-TTS, a verifier-driven agentic generation system achieving dynamic region-level self-correction. This approach paves the way for more reliable, interpretable, and fine-grained multimodal verification, supporting safer and more controllable foundation model deployment.

</details>


### [107] [Self-Improving Language Models with Bidirectional Evolutionary Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28814)
*Guowei Xu,Zhenting Qi,Huangyuan Su,Weirui Ye,Himabindu Lakkaraju,Sham M. Kakade,Yilun Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“双向进化搜索”（BES）框架，通过引入进化算子扩展探索空间，并利用后向目标分解提供稠密反馈，解决了现有语言模型搜索方法中验证信号稀疏及探索空间受限的问题，显著提升了模型在后训练和推理阶段的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索方法（如 Best-of-N 和树搜索）存在两个核心缺陷：一是验证信号稀疏，难以引导搜索；二是局限于自回归扩展，导致搜索空间被限制在模型概率质量集中的区域，缺乏对更广阔解空间的探索。

Method: 提出“双向进化搜索”（Bidirectional Evolutionary Search, BES）框架：1. 前向进化：在标准自回归扩展的基础上引入进化算子（如重组部分轨迹），以探索模型概率密度之外的区域；2. 后向搜索：将复杂任务递归分解为可验证的子目标，从而为前向搜索提供密集的中间反馈。

Result: 理论分析表明，进化算子能使搜索跳出“熵壳”，而后向搜索能指数级减少寻找正确解所需的样本量。实验证明，BES 在主流方法失效的后处理任务中取得了持续提升，并在三个公开问题求解基准测试中，其平均性能和最优性能均优于现有的开源框架。

Conclusion: BES 通过结合前向进化策略和后向目标分解，有效克服了传统搜索方法在探索空间和反馈密度上的局限性，为语言模型的自我改进和推理搜索提供了一种更高效、鲁棒的通用框架。

Abstract: Search has been proposed as an effective method for self-improving language models and agentic systems, both for post-training sample generation and for inference. However, widely used methods such as best-of-N sampling and tree search face two fundamental limitations: they are guided by sparse verification signals, and they construct candidates primarily through autoregressive expansion, restricting exploration to regions with substantial model probability mass. To address these, we propose Bidirectional Evolutionary Search (BES), a search framework that couples forward candidate evolution with backward goal decomposition. In the forward search, BES augments standard expansion with evolution operators that recombine partial trajectories to generate candidates that are difficult to obtain from a single model rollout. In the backward search, BES recursively decomposes the original task into checkable subgoals, producing dense intermediate feedback that guides forward search. We provide theoretical motivation showing that candidates generated by expansion-only search are confined to a narrow entropy shell while evolutionary operators can escape it, and that backward search can exponentially reduce the number of required samples to find a correct answer. Experiments show that on challenging post-training tasks where mainstream post-training algorithms fail to improve, BES enables consistent gains, and on three open problem solving benchmarks at inference time, BES outperforms existing open-source frameworks in both average and best-case performance. Code and trained models are available at https://github.com/Embodied-Minds-Lab/BES.

</details>


### [108] [VLMs May Not Globally Enhance Human Alignment over LLMs During Natural Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28818)
*Jinzhou Wu,Zhengwu Ma,Jixing Li,Baoping Tang,Zitong Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究通过对比LLM与VLM发现，多模态训练对模型模拟人类阅读过程的影响并非全局性的，而是仅在视觉语义丰富的文本中表现出显著的选择性对齐优势，强调了纯语言表征在模拟人类阅读中的核心地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在语言处理建模方面已取得进展，但多模态训练（视觉-语言学习）是否能使文本表征在自然阅读过程中变得更具“类人”特征，目前尚不明确。该研究旨在探究多模态预训练历史对模型与人类语言处理对齐程度的影响。

Method: 研究采用了受控的比较实验方法，对比了参数严格匹配的纯文本大语言模型（LLM）与视觉-语言模型（VLM）。在纯文本输入的前提下，排除了在线视觉输入或跨模态融合的干扰，专门评估多模态训练历史对模型的影响。实验利用人类自然阅读数据集（包含全脑fMRI反应和同步眼动追踪数据）来评估模型表征与人类生理反应的对齐程度。

Result: 实验结果表明，多模态预训练并不提供全局性的优势；然而，当句子包含较强的视觉语义内容时，VLM在fMRI脑区激活模式和眼动行为的对齐上表现出选择性的优势，证实了视觉经验在特定语义情境下对语言表征的塑造作用。

Conclusion: 多模态预训练对人类语言处理的建模并非具有全局性的优势，其贡献具有选择性。在处理自然语言阅读任务时，模型内部的语言表征仍然是决定其与人类大脑活动和眼动行为对齐程度的关键因素，视觉语义内容较强的句子能凸显视觉-语言模型（VLM）的优势。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have become increasingly useful computational models of human language processing, but it remains unclear whether vision-language learning makes text representations more human-like during natural reading. Here, we address this question by comparing tightly matched LLM and vision-language model (VLM) pairs under a strictly text-only setting, allowing us to isolate the effect of multimodal training history from online visual input or cross-modal fusion. We evaluate model alignment with a human natural-reading dataset that includes whole-cortex fMRI responses and synchronized eye-tracking saccades. Our findings demonstrate that multimodal pretraining may not confer a uniform, global advantage in human alignment during natural reading, indicating that language-internal representations remain the key factor for modeling human text processing. However, the VLM advantage could emerge more selectively when sentences contain stronger visual semantic content, with converging evidence from both fMRI and eye-movement alignments. Together, our findings provide a controlled in silico framework for testing how visual learning history shapes model-human alignment of language processing, suggesting that multimodal pretraining contributes selectively rather than globally to human-like language representations during natural reading.

### [109] [The Future of Facts: Tracing the Factual Generation-Verification Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27564)
*Tim R. Davidson,Anja Surina,Caglar Gulcehre*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型在事实性知识上存在显著的“生成-验证鸿沟”，发现验证能力习得早于生成能力且更具鲁棒性，并指出知识更新会导致模型产生新旧知识共存的认知混乱状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在输出事实性知识时往往存在“生成-验证鸿沟”（GV-gap），即模型校验输出的能力强于其生成内容的能力。当前对于这种鸿沟在事实性知识领域的动态演变机制尚缺乏深入理解，亟需探究其背后的训练动力学。

Method: 研究团队跨越四个开源模型家族（每个家族两种规模），通过三个训练阶段（知识获取、持续学习、知识更新）对模型的生成与验证能力进行定量追踪。同时，利用前沿大模型进行自然实验，以验证并对比上述动态规律在更大规模下的表现。

Result: 1. 验证能力的习得总是先于生成能力；2. 相比生成能力，验证能力在持续学习过程中表现出更高的鲁棒性；3. 事实更新会导致模型产生“多重宇宙”现象，即模型对新旧事实存在认知冲突；4. 前沿模型在大规模下表现出相似动态，并存在明显的验证偏差。

Conclusion: 事实性知识的“生成-验证鸿沟”是模型训练过程中的固有现象。验证能力的习得早于生成能力，且在持续学习中更具鲁棒性。知识更新可能导致模型陷入“多重宇宙”状态（同时认为新旧知识均为正确），揭示了现有模型在事实一致性管理方面的根本局限。

Abstract: Language models are becoming the default interface to factual knowledge, yet they often verify outputs more reliably than they generate them. This generation-verification gap (GV-gap) underlies many recent advances in self-improvement and reasoning, but its dynamics on factual knowledge specifically remain poorly understood. We focus on the training mechanisms underlying factual GV-gaps, distinguishing them from their computational and aesthetic counterparts. We trace generation and verification capabilities through three training phases (acquisition, continual learning, and updating) across four open-source model families at two scales each. Three findings recur across models: (i) verification is consistently learned before generation; (ii) verification is more robust to continual learning than generation; and (iii) factual updates can leave models in a "multi-verse" state, simultaneously verifying both old and new answers as correct. Natural experiments on frontier models reproduce these dynamics at scale and reveal residual verification biases on well-covered facts.

</details>


### [110] [Disentangling Language Roles in Multilingual LLM Task Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27649)
*Qishi Zhan,Minxuan Hu,Seoyeon Jang,Lei Zhao,Ziheng Chen,Man Liang,Xinyue Xiang,Jiaxin Liu,Guansu Wang,Liang He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 MTM-Bench，这是一个通过控制指令、内容和响应三种语言角色进行完全交叉测试的多语言基准。研究表明，模型在多语言任务中的表现极度依赖于“响应语言”的一致性，而非仅仅取决于语言匹配的总体数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多语言指令微调基准测试缺乏对指令语言、源内容语言和目标响应语言三者之间相互作用的系统性考察，无法有效评估模型在复杂多语言任务切换下的处理能力。因此，需要一个能够解耦这些角色并进行受控实验的基准。

Method: 研究团队构建了 MTM-Bench 基准测试，采用完全交叉设计（Fully Crossed Design），通过 (L_instr, L_content, L_resp) 三元组对中、英、西三种语言进行全排列组合（共27种情况），包含 2,430 个实例。评估任务涵盖语义反转、最终状态提取、以及带更新实现的语言纯度检查，并引入了包括语义正确性、目标语言依从性、约束满足度及联合成功率在内的细分指标，并通过人工审计验证评分有效性。

Result: 对 20 个主流 LLM 的评估发现，模型的性能退化与其在任务中所处的语言角色密切相关。响应语言不匹配对模型的影响远大于指令或源内容语言的不匹配。研究还发现，不匹配的数量并非难度的单调预测指标，且不同任务族在失败模式上表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: 语言模型的性能下降不仅仅取决于语言匹配的数量，而是取决于语言在任务结构中所扮演的角色。其中，响应语言（Response Language）是影响模型表现的最关键因素，单一的响应语言不匹配即可导致大部分性能下降。单纯依靠语义正确性指标不足以评估复杂的多语言任务执行能力。

Abstract: Multilingual LLMs are increasingly used when instruction, source content, and required response languages do not coincide. Existing benchmarks have expanded multilingual instruction-following evaluation, but they rarely isolate these three roles within a fully crossed design. We introduce MTM-Bench, a controlled benchmark for language-conditioned task execution in which each instance is defined by a triplet \((L_{\text{instr}}, L_{\text{content}}, L_{\text{resp}})\). Across English, Spanish, and Chinese, MTM-Bench enumerates all 27 triplets and contains 2{,}430 instances per model across semantic reversal, final-state extraction, and language purity with update realization. We evaluate 20 frontier and open-weight LLMs using decomposed metrics for semantic correctness, target-language adherence, constraint satisfaction, contamination ratio, and joint success, with scoring validated by a targeted human audit. The fully crossed design reveals that degradation is organized by the role a language occupies in the task structure, not merely by mismatch count. The response-language role is the dominant axis of variation, and a single response-slot mismatch accounts for most degradation. The response-only and full-mismatch comparison suggests that mismatch count is not a monotonic predictor of difficulty, with model-level ordering varying across systems. Task families fail through distinct channels, showing that semantic correctness alone does not capture reliable multilingual task execution.

</details>


### [111] [TRACES: Proactive Safety Auditing for Multi-Turn LLM Agents via Trajectory-State Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27690)
*Jiaqian Li,Yanshu Li,Boxuan Zhang,Ruixiang Tang,Kuan-Hao Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对LLM智能体长周期交互中的安全风险，本文提出了一种基于隐层表示的前瞻性审计框架TRACES，通过学习轨迹的前缀风险演变，实现了比事后诊断更高效、及时的风险预警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体安全审计多为“反应式”（即事后诊断），难以在长周期多轮交互中实时捕捉隐藏在中间步骤的风险。作者旨在解决这一局限，实现对智能体行为的“前瞻性”审计，从而及时预警潜在的不安全行为。

Method: 提出TRACES（轨迹表示审计系统），利用观察者LLM的隐藏层表示，通过学习前缀级别的轨迹风险状态来评估安全风险。其核心技术包括诱导潜在机制特征、建模风险的时间演变，并采用弱轨迹级监督学习来实现密集的步级风险估计。

Result: 实验表明，TRACES在多个智能体安全基准测试中均提升了全轨迹安全预测的准确性，并表现出卓越的风险判别能力；此外，该方法提取的风险状态对于提升智能体的安全性训练具有显著潜力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的TRACES框架证明了基于隐藏表示的前瞻性审计在长周期LLM智能体安全中的有效性。通过建模轨迹演化中的风险状态，该方法能够在风险产生早期进行识别，不仅优于传统的反应式审计，还为开发更安全的智能体提供了新的训练路径。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly operate through multi-turn tool use and environment interaction, where safety risks often emerge from intermediate steps long before they surface in the final outcome. Reactive auditing is therefore insufficient: post-hoc diagnosis frequently misses the chance to flag risks while they are unfolding. We propose TRACES, a representation-based proactive auditor that learns prefix-level trajectory risk states from the hidden representations of an observer LLM. TRACES induces latent mechanism features from step representations and models their temporal evolution to estimate whether a partial trajectory is drifting toward unsafe behavior. To sidestep the cost and ambiguity of step-level risk annotation, TRACES is trained with weak trajectory-level supervision while still producing dense prefix-level risk estimates. Across multiple agent safety benchmarks, TRACES improves both full-trajectory safety prediction and proactive risk discrimination. Our analyses further suggest that these risk states can help train a safer agent, highlighting the broader potential of proactive auditing for long-horizon agent safety.

### [112] [StoryMI: Steerable Multi-Agent Therapeutic Dialogue Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27393)

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate fluent dialogue, but prior works lack situational grounding, dynamic strategy control, and evaluation aligned with clinical standards in motivational interviewing (MI). We introduce StoryMI, a multi-LLM agent framework for controllable MI dialogue generation, where questionnaire-based client profiles are expanded into situational stories that provide narrative context for the dialogue. Therapist and client agents generate MI-coded utterances guided by MI codes selected by the interaction agent, while an interaction agent dynamically coordinates exchanges to control MI strategies during a multi-turn conversation. We propose a two-level evaluation protocol: lexical metrics and MI-specific measures of macro-level counseling strategies, alongside LLM-as-judge and human expert assessments. We construct a dataset of 6K simulated MI dialogues grounded in 1K questionnaire-story pairs, covering 12 MI codes and 13 symptom domains, and benchmark six open- and closed-source LLMs. Our results show that situational grounding and macro-level control can improve MI adherence and clinical plausibility, demonstrating the effectiveness of a structured multi-agent workflow for psychotherapy dialogue generation. ### [113] [Cultural Fidelity in English-to-Hindi Translation: A Preservation-Fluency Frontier for Gender Recoverability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27654)
*Samyak Savi,Chavi Gupta,Shreyas Gantayet,Tanay Sodha,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了生成式翻译中性别信息丢失的问题，提出了两种推理时干预策略，在显著提升性别还原度的同时，探讨了其与语言流利度之间的平衡与权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式翻译系统在处理语言时往往会抹除源文本中明确编码的性别信息（特别是在印地语的作格和敬语结构中），这忽略了翻译作为一种文化技术在保留社会意义线索方面的重要性。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含37,345个实例的基准数据集，专门评估英译印（Hindi）过程中性别信息的可恢复性。
2. 开发了两种推理时干预机制：
   - 源感知重排序（SAR）：优先选择避免性别中性化语法结构的候选翻译。
   - 现象感知重排序（PAR）：通过目标词汇标记，即便在必须使用中性语法结构时也能保留性别信息。

Result: 在GPT-4o-mini和Sarvam模型上，PAR干预显著提高了性别保留准确率（分别从11.07%提升至54.47%和从15.99%提升至49.66%）。人工评估显示性别保留率从10.3%提升至81.3%，但流利度评分从4.36降至3.37。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在文化敏感的机器翻译任务中，性别信息的保留与语言流利度之间存在权衡。PAR干预手段虽然显著提升了性别信息的可恢复性，但会对句子的自然流畅度产生负面影响，这揭示了生成式AI在处理复杂文化表征时面临的结构性挑战。

Abstract: Generative translation systems are cultural technologies because they decide how socially meaningful cues are rendered within culturally specific grammatical systems. We study one concrete notion of successful cultural translation: when an English source explicitly encodes gender, an English-to-Hindi translation should preserve the recoverability of that cue unless the source itself is ambiguous. We evaluate this criterion on a 37,345-instance benchmark spanning twelve categories and show that five systems frequently erase gender through ergative and honorific constructions. We then introduce two mechanism-aware inference-time interventions. The first, the Source-Aware Reranker (SAR), prefers candidates that avoid gender-neutralizing syntax. The second, the Phenomenon-Aware Reranker (PAR), preserves gender through targeted lexical marking even when ergative syntax remains. Across GPT-4o-mini and Sarvam, PAR improves target-subset accuracy from 11.07% to 54.47% and from 15.99% to 49.66%, respectively. Human evaluation shows that PAR increases gender preservation from 10.3% to 81.3%, but reduces mean fluency from 4.36 to 3.37. These findings place the two interventions on a preservation and fluency frontier rather than supporting a single dominant solution, and show how culturally situated generation can require explicit tradeoffs among fidelity, fluency, and stylistic naturalness.

</details>
