### [191] [Mechanistically Interpreting the Role of Sample Difficulty in RLVR for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28388)
*Yue Cheng,Jiajun Zhang,Xiaohui Gao,Weiwei Xing,Zheng Wang,Zhanxing Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了样本难度对大模型RLVR推理能力的影响，发现难度呈非单调效应，并利用时间稀疏自编码器揭示了不同难度下的特征演化机制，进而提出了自适应策略以优化困难样本的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管强化学习（RLVR）在提升大模型数学和编程推理能力方面表现出色，但样本难度在这一过程中的具体机制尚不明确，且盲目训练困难样本可能导致模型能力退化，因此需要深入探究样本难度对训练动态的影响。

Method: 1. 难度分层与单样本分析：评估不同难度问题对RLVR推理性能的影响；2. 机制分析：利用时间稀疏自编码器（T-SAE）监测模型内部特征动态；3. 优化策略：提出难度自适应策略，包括“逆向推理重构”和“T-SAE引导的训练信号”，以增强RLVR过程中的奖励密度与信用分配。

Result: 1. 样本难度对RLVR存在非单调影响：简单和中等难度问题能带来最稳定提升，而过难问题会导致退化行为（如重复、跳步）；2. 特征动态差异：简单问题强化基础计算，中等难度问题平衡计算与推理，困难问题需成功轨迹引导方能产生有效信号；3. 改进效果：提出的难度自适应策略有效提升了困难样本下的奖励密度与学习效果。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了样本难度是决定RLVR优化动态和表征演化的关键因素。通过针对难度差异采取自适应策略，可以显著提升RLVR在处理复杂问题时的训练效率与模型性能，避免了模型因盲目训练困难样本而导致的退化。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) is empirically shown to notably enhance the reasoning performance of large language models (LLMs), particularly in mathematics and programming. However, the mechanistic role of Sample Difficulty in RLVR remains poorly understood. In this paper, we investigate RLVR through the lens of difficulty-wise and one-sample analysis. We find that sample difficulty has a non-monotonic effect on RLVR: easy and medium-difficulty problems yield the strongest and most stable reasoning improvements, whereas overly hard problems often provide weak learning signals, induce degenerate behaviors such as answer repetition or skipping necessary computation, and can ultimately degrade the model's pre-existing capabilities. Beyond the obverse of response, we further analyze the model's internal feature dynamics using Temporal Sparse Autoencoders (T-SAE). Easy problems mainly reinforce direct-answer and basic-computation features while suppressing deliberative-reasoning features; hard problems activate reasoning-related features but become useful only when successful trajectories are sampled; medium-difficulty problems provide a more balanced signal, strengthening both computation and multi-step reasoning features. Motivated by these findings, we propose difficulty-adaptive strategies for hard-sample utilization, using backward-reasoning reformulation and T-SAE-guided training signals to improve reward density and credit assignment during RLVR. Overall, our results identify sample difficulty as a key factor governing both the optimization dynamics and representation evolution of RLVR.

### [192] [HRBench: Benchmarking and Understanding Thinking-Mode Switch Strategies in Hybrid-Reasoning LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28398)
*Yansong Ning,Mianpeng Liu,Jingwen Ye,Weidong Zhang,Hao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 HRBench，这是一个用于评估混合推理大语言模型思维模式切换能力的统一框架。通过对比多种策略与训练范式，该研究揭示了不同策略在成本与准确率之间的权衡规律，为高效推理的研究提供了标准化参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合推理大语言模型（LLMs）允许用户在回答质量与推理成本之间进行权衡，但现有研究缺乏统一的评估标准和实验环境，导致不同方法在模型、数据集和假设条件各异的情况下难以进行公平比较，限制了对思维模式切换机制的深入理解。

Method: 作者提出了 HRBench 评估框架，将混合推理的设计空间划分为“切换策略”（基于提示的选择、外部路由、投机执行）和“训练范式”（无需训练、监督微调 SFT、离线与在线强化学习）两个维度，形成 12 种受控实验设置。此外，研究涵盖了 6 种不同规模的模型（从 2B 到 1.1T 参数）和 5 个涵盖数学、科学及代码的推理基准，并重现了超过 12 种既有方法进行横向对比。

Result: 研究发现，不同的切换策略占据了不同的效率-效果权衡空间：基于提示的方法在权衡通证（token）与准确率方面表现出色；路由方法能够实现更稳定的成本降低；投机执行则倾向于以更高的通证消耗为代价提升准确率。此外，模型规模和任务类型对策略的选择具有显著影响。

Conclusion: HRBench 作为一个统一的评估框架，成功量化了混合推理大语言模型中不同思维模式切换策略的有效性与效率权衡。研究表明，没有单一的最优策略，策略的选择应根据模型规模、任务领域及预算约束进行动态调整。该框架为高效推理研究提供了标准化的基准和参考实现。

Abstract: Hybrid-reasoning large language models (LLMs) expose explicit controls over reasoning effort, allowing users or systems to trade off answer quality against inference cost. However, existing methods for adaptive thinking-mode selection are typically evaluated under different models, datasets, and implementation assumptions, making it difficult to compare their practical behavior. We introduce HRBench, a unified evaluation framework for studying thinking-mode switching in hybrid-reasoning LLMs. HRBench organizes the design space along two axes: three switching strategy families, prompt-based selection, external routing, and speculative execution, and four training regimes, training-free, SFT, offline and online RL, yielding 12 controlled evaluation settings. We evaluate these settings across 6 LLMs, from Qwen3.5-2B to Kimi-K2.5-1.1T, and 5 reasoning benchmarks covering mathematics, science, and code, while reimplementing 12+ representative prior methods within the same pipeline. Our analysis characterizes how different switching strategies occupy distinct effectiveness-efficiency trade-off regions: prompt-based methods often provide favorable token-accuracy trade-offs, routing methods offer more stable cost reduction, and speculative methods tend to improve accuracy at higher token cost. We further find that training affects strategies differently, and that the preferred strategy varies with model scale and task domain. HRBench provides reference implementations and a unified evaluation platform to support more controlled research on efficient reasoning in hybrid-reasoning LLMs. Our data, code and repository are available at https://github.com/usail-hkust/HRBench.

Drawing from decades of research in psychology, neuroscience, and cognitive science, we introduce a Cognitive Taxonomy that deconstructs general intelligence into 10 key cognitive faculties. We then propose a rigorous evaluation protocol in which a system's performance is measured across a suite of targeted, held-out cognitive tasks, generating a 'cognitive profile' that can be used to understand a system's strengths and weaknesses. We hope this framework will provide a practical roadmap and an initial step toward more rigorous, empirical evaluation of AGI.

### [195] [DenoiseRL: Bootstrapping Reasoning Models to Recover from Noisy Prefixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28421)
*Caijun Xu,Changyi Xiao,Zhongyuan Peng,Yixin Cao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DenoiseRL 是一种无需外部强监督的强化学习框架，它通过让大语言模型直接从自身的错误推理轨迹中进行“恢复导向”的学习，实现了比传统方法更高效、更具可扩展性的推理能力提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习方法大多依赖强教师模型或高质量的人工标注数据集，这限制了模型能力的扩展性。作者旨在探索一种能减少对外部资源依赖、能够利用模型自身失败经验进行自我进化的训练框架。

Method: 提出了 DenoiseRL 框架，其核心思想是“恢复导向的优化”（recovery-oriented optimization）。该方法不依赖外部强监督，而是让模型直接从自身的错误推理轨迹中学习，通过将错误的推理过程转化为改进的机会，从而实现高效的强化学习训练。

Result: 在多个数学和通用推理基准测试中，DenoiseRL 的表现一致优于强策略内（on-policy）强化学习基线模型。实验表明，该方法在提升推理性能的同时，显著提高了训练效率，并增强了模型在面对困难问题时的自我纠错能力。

Conclusion: DenoiseRL 证明了一种无需依赖强教师模型或精选数据的创新训练范式。通过将模型自身的错误转化为学习信号，不仅提升了推理能力，还增强了模型的自我纠错能力，为大语言模型的推理能力提升提供了一条更具可扩展性的路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a central paradigm for advancing reasoning in large language models, yet most existing methods still depend on stronger teacher models or heavily curated difficult datasets, limiting scalable capability improvement. In this paper, we introduce DenoiseRL, a reinforcement learning framework that substitutes external supervision with recovery-oriented optimization over failures from weak models. Instead of relying on stronger supervision or carefully engineered data, DenoiseRL learns directly from incorrect reasoning traces by converting them into opportunities for improvement, making training more scalable and less dependent on external resources. This yields a richer and more diverse learning signal, improving exploration efficiency from imperfect model behavior. As a result, DenoiseRL improves reasoning performance and overall training efficiency while reducing the need for expensive data curation or stronger teacher models. Empirically, DenoiseRL consistently outperforms strong on-policy RL baselines across competitive mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks and promotes stronger self-corrective behavior as training difficulty increases, highlighting an effective and scalable alternative pathway for improving reasoning in large language models.

</details>


### [196] [GONDOR to the Rescue: Satisficing Planning with Low Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28454)
*Yonatan Vernik,Alexander Tuisov,Alexander Shleyfman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对内存受限场景下的规划问题，本文提出了一种改进型 GBFS 算法 GONDOR，通过周期性压缩搜索树和重搜索机制，显著提升了在严苛内存限制下的任务求解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贪婪最佳优先搜索（GBFS）是规划与路径规划领域的主流方法，但在内存受限的环境（如边缘设备）中，该算法往往因内存溢出而无法完成搜索，亟需一种能在严格内存约束下持续运行的高效搜索扩展方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GONDOR 的算法：1. 通过定期压缩搜索树并保留一组稀疏的“锚点状态（outpost states）”来减少内存占用；2. 在达到目标后，通过在这些锚点之间进行重新搜索来重建完整路径；3. 引入了多种锚点选择策略；4. 利用布隆过滤器（Bloom filters）实现闭表（closed list）的紧凑重复检测。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多个数值规划领域及不同启发式配置下，与标准 GBFS 相比，GONDOR 在低内存预算限制下显著提高了任务完成的覆盖率（coverage）。

Conclusion: GONDOR 成功地在内存受限环境下扩展了贪婪最佳优先搜索（GBFS）的适用性。通过结合树压缩、锚点状态重搜索以及布隆过滤器等技术，该算法有效地在有限内存资源与搜索性能之间取得了平衡，为资源受限设备上的规划任务提供了一种高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Greedy Best-First Search (GBFS) is the dominant approach for solving search problems where the goal can be estimated with a heuristic, such as planning, route finding, navigation, and pathfinding. This is especially true when the memory is tightly constrained, such as planning on edge devices. To alleviate that, we present GONDOR (Greedy Online Navigation with Dynamic Outpost-based Re-search), a memory-efficient extension of GBFS that allows search to continue under strict memory limits by periodically compressing the search tree while retaining a sparse set of anchor states, then upon reaching the goal reconstructs the path by re-searching between the sparse states. We analyze the algorithm and discuss several variants defined by different outpost selection policies. In addition, we explore using Bloom filters for compact duplicate detection in the closed list. Experiments across numeric planning domains and heuristic configurations show that GONDOR consistently improves coverage under low memory budgets compared to standard GBFS. We release the implementation of GONDOR and the Bloom-filter variant to facilitate further research on memory-efficient heuristic search.

</details>


### [197] [Diffusion Large Language Models for Visual Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28456)
*Jeong Hun Yeo,Chae Won Kim,Hyeongseop Rha,Yong Man Ro*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语音识别（VSR）系统多采用从左至右的自回归解码，容易在上下文信息不足时对视觉上模糊的词元做出过早且错误的决定，限制了识别准确率。

Method: 1. 提出了 DLLM-VSR 框架，将转录过程建模为迭代式掩码去噪任务；2. 采用基于置信度的非自回归解码，利用双向上下文细化模糊 token；3. 设计了两阶段掩码去噪训练策略，以分离视觉-文本内容对齐与长度建模；4. 开发了长度引导的候选解码与重排序策略，以缓解目标长度不确定性带来的性能损失。

Abstract: Existing Visual Speech Recognition (VSR) systems commonly rely on left-to-right autoregressive decoding, which can force premature decisions on visually ambiguous tokens before sufficient context is available. We propose DLLM-VSR, to the best of our knowledge, the first Diffusion Large Language Model (DLLM)-based VSR framework, formulating transcription as iterative masked denoising with flexible-order decoding. With confidence-based unmasking, DLLM-VSR commits high-confidence positions early and uses the committed tokens as bidirectional context to refine ambiguous ones. To adapt DLLMs to VSR, we introduce a two-stage masked-denoising training strategy that separates visual-to-text content alignment from length modeling. We further observe a performance gap with oracle-length decoding, which assumes access to the true transcript length, indicating that reducing target-length uncertainty can improve DLLM-based VSR. To reduce this gap, we develop length-guided candidate decoding, which uses video duration to construct plausible transcript-length hypotheses, decodes under multiple hypotheses, and reranks candidates using length plausibility and decoding confidence. The proposed method achieves a state-of-the-art WER of 19.5\% on LRS3 using only its labeled training data.

Abstract: Materials process optimization requires reasoning over routes, conditions, tools and causal dependencies, yet most computational formulations flatten synthesis procedures into text or ordered steps. We introduce MatProcBench, a provenance-grounded benchmark constructed from literature-mined MatPROV graphs, to evaluate seven process-reasoning tasks spanning route continuity, step-level variable inference and global causal consistency under both same-split and shift-aware evaluation, including a strict dual-OOD split that combines temporal and material-class shift. We further introduce ProvMind, a process-memory reasoning framework that retrieves analogous training processes, converts them into provenance-aware option-level compatibility scores, and uses a language model for constrained final decision making. ProvMind achieves 52.84\% accuracy on the dual-OOD split, outperforming prompting, retrieval-augmented and supervised fine-tuning baselines.

Abstract: Accurately forecasting the impact of salient financial events on markets is critical for investors and policymakers. In this work, we propose GS-Fuse, a multimodal event-based forecasting framework that employs (i) a Granger-supervised, causal-aware gated fusion module, which learns to open toward event text only when it provides incremental predictive value beyond historical prices, and (ii) a multi-granularity alignment mechanism that jointly aligns high-level event representations and fine-grained textual cues with future market trajectories. Built as a flexible, plug-and-play adapter on top of off-the-shelf large language models and time-series foundation models, GS-Fuse can be instantiated across diverse backbones and market settings. Abstract: Masked language modeling has become a standard pretraining objective for training encoder-based language models. Conventionally, the tokens selected for masking are chosen at random, which may not always yield the most effective learning signals. In this work, we examine a token masking strategy based on entropy distribution. We use the model's entropy over token predictions to identify which tokens should be masked. This method aims to target tokens that are more informative and uncertain to improve the training efficacy. Method: 提出FeasiGen自动化框架，通过提取成功执行的工具调用轨迹，识别并屏蔽核心工具，从而构建不可行任务数据集；同时引入可行性感知评估指标来衡量智能体识别并及时终止任务的能力。

Abstract: Tool-using agents often incur substantial computational cost due to long reasoning chains and iterative tool usage. In practical scenarios, many tasks become infeasible under constrained tool environments, where the capabilities required for successful task completion are unavailable. Detecting infeasible tasks and stopping execution early can significantly reduce unnecessary execution cost. In this work, we propose FeasiGen, an automatic pipeline for constructing infeasible agent tasks by identifying the critical tools required for successful task completion. Our approach extracts tool-calling traces from successful executions across multiple agent systems, identifies critical tools consistently shared across diverse execution strategies, and masks these tools to automatically transform solvable tasks into infeasible ones. Human verification confirms that the infeasibility annotations for our constructed tasks achieve over 94% accuracy. We further introduce feasibility-aware evaluation metrics for measuring whether agents can recognize infeasible tasks and stop execution appropriately. ### [202] [Cultural Binding Heads in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28543)
*Avrile Floro,Luca Benedetto*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过机械可解释性技术揭示了大语言模型中存在“文化绑定”机制的特定注意力头，发现模型对文化差异的处理不足归因于内部路由瓶颈而非知识缺失，并提出了一种通过微调特定注意力权重来提升模型文化差异感知能力的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在处理跨文化场景时往往倾向于“一视同仁”，缺乏对文化背景差异的敏锐度（即差异意识缺失），导致模型在处理文化相关任务时表现不佳。该研究旨在探究模型内部如何实现“文化绑定”，以及能否通过干预特定结构来提升模型的文化差异识别能力。

Method: 利用机械可解释性方法（Mechanistic Interpretability）和析因设计，在N4文化挪用基准上对8个不同架构的模型进行分析；通过因果干预技术（Knockout）定位影响文化绑定的特定注意力头，并通过α-缩放（α-scaling）进行推理阶段的转向（steering）实验。

Result: 研究发现每种模型中约有2-3个中间层注意力头负责文化绑定，剔除这些连接可降低9-23%的绑定强度；实验证明文化绑定能力在预训练阶段形成；通过适当的推理阶段干预（α=2-3），可将文化差异化准确率提升1-3个百分点；知识探测任务显示，模型内部蕴含的文化知识远超其在输出中所表现出的水平。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大型语言模型在处理文化背景时存在“差异意识缺失”问题，其瓶颈在于信息路由而非知识匮乏。通过识别和干预特定的注意力头，可以在保持通用推理能力的前提下，有效增强模型对文化差异的感知与处理能力。

Abstract: LLMs often default to equal treatment across cultural groups, even though context warrants differentiation: this is a lack of difference awareness. Using mechanistic interpretability and a factorial design on the N4 cultural appropriation benchmark from Wang et al. (2025), we identify 2-3 mid-layer attention heads per model that contribute causally to cultural binding across eight models (four architectures, base and instruct). Cultural binding is the process of associating cultural items with the appropriate identity. Knockout of the identity-to-item edges on these heads lowers the binding strength by 9-23%. The identified heads transfer from instruct to base models, suggesting that cultural binding is created at pre-training. An $α$-scaling shows a graded dose-response and moderate amplification steering at generation ($α= 2-3$) increases cultural differentiation accuracy by 1-3 pp while leaving neutral reasoning mostly intact. A knowledge probing task shows that models know 3-5 times more than they act upon it, indicating that the bottleneck lies in routing and not knowledge.

### [203] [Refusal Before Decoding: Detecting and Exploiting Refusal Signals in Intermediate LLM Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28553)
*Matteo Gioele Collu,Riccardo Conte,Alberto Giaretta,Denis Kleyko,Mauro Conti,Matteo Zavatteri,Roberto Confalonieri*

TL;DR: 本文发现大模型的拒绝行为在模型中间层即有明显的线性特征，并据此提出一种名为“机械自动对手生成”的方法，利用这些内部信号在无需完整模型评估的情况下，高效地生成对抗性提示词。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 利用线性探测器（Linear Probes）对Transformer各层的残差流激活进行训练，以预测模型是否会产生拒绝行为；2. 提出“机械自动对手生成”（Mechanistic AutoDAN），将探测器评分集成到遗传算法中，通过部分前向传播代替完整模型评估来引导对抗性提示词生成。

Result: 1. 拒绝行为在模型输出前的中间层即可被线性探测器有效识别；2. Mechanistic AutoDAN在保持与原始AutoDAN相当攻击成功率的同时，将单次迭代的搜索时间降低了高达72%；3. 随着模型规模的扩大，探测器引导的作用更为显著。

Conclusion: 研究表明，拒绝行为并非仅仅出现在输出层面，而是作为一种结构化且可操作的信号编码在大型语言模型的中间激活中。这一发现为理解模型安全性、探测潜在漏洞以及优化对抗攻击提供了新的机械可解释性视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate whether refusal behavior can be predicted from LLM intermediate activations before decoding using linear probes trained on residual stream activations at each transformer block. We find that refusal is linearly decodable well before the final layer, indicating that safety-relevant behavior is represented in intermediate activations before output generation. To test whether this signal is actionable, we introduce Mechanistic AutoDAN, a probe-guided variant of AutoDAN that replaces full-model fitness evaluation with partial forward passes and probe-based scoring inside a genetic prompt search loop. Across the evaluated models, our method achieves attack success rates competitive with vanilla AutoDAN while reducing per-iteration search time by up to 72%, and probe-guided prompts match or exceed AutoDAN's cross-model transfer in several configurations. We further find that the usefulness of probe guidance increases with model scale. Our results show that refusal is not only observable at the output level, but is encoded as a structured and actionable signal in intermediate LLM activations.

</details>


### [204] [A Matter of TASTE: Improving Coverage and Difficulty of Agent Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28556)
*Tomer Keren,Nitay Calderon,Asaf Yehudai,Yotam Perlitz,Michal Shmueli-Scheuer,Roi Reichert*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对智能体评估基准饱和及构建困难的问题，本文提出 TASTE 框架，通过自动化生成复杂、高覆盖率的任务来评估智能体，揭示了当前模型在复杂工具调用能力上的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体评估基准（如 τ²-Bench）已趋于饱和，且人工构建新基准任务成本高昂、覆盖面窄，难以全面衡量智能体在复杂场景下的工具使用能力。

Method: 提出 TASTE（基于工具序列演化的任务合成）框架。该方法反转了传统流程，首先通过基于 LLM 评分的自适应对比 n-gram 模型生成有效的工具序列，覆盖广泛的工具组合；随后利用聚类筛选代表性序列，将其实例化为完整任务，并进行迭代式难度演化。

Result: 利用 TASTE 构建了 τ^c-Bench 基准，测试发现现有模型在该基准上性能显著下降（如 Gemini-3-Flash 分数大幅滑落），且新任务的工具组合覆盖率是原基准的两倍以上。

Conclusion: TASTE 提供了一种可扩展、自动化的基准测试生成范式，打破了现有评估工具使用能力的局限性。研究表明，模型在现有基准测试上的高分往往源于饱和而非能力的提升，未来需要更具挑战性的评估方法来衡量智能体的鲁棒性。

Abstract: As agent capabilities advance, existing benchmarks, such as $τ^2$-Bench, are becoming increasingly saturated. Yet constructing new benchmark tasks remains complex, costly, and labor-intensive. Moreover, the standard approach, in which scenarios are first written in natural language and then mapped to tool sequences, captures only a narrow subset of the tool-use patterns agents exercise. In this paper, we address these problems by reversing the task construction process. We propose TASTE: Task Synthesis from Tool Sequence Evolution, an automatic method that generates challenging tasks with broader tool-use coverage. TASTE utilizes an Adaptive Contrastive $n$-gram model trained on LLM-judged validity signals. This enables sampling valid tool sequences that cover a vast range of tool combinations. TASTE then selects representative sequences from the pool via clustering, instantiates them into complete benchmark tasks, and refines them through iterative difficulty evolution. Using TASTE, we construct $τ^c$-Bench, a challenging extension of the three domains of $τ^2$-Bench. We evaluate $11$ agent/user LLM pairs and find that models nearly saturating $τ^2$-Bench suffer severe performance drops on our tasks (e.g., Gemini-3-Flash falls from $0.82\!-\!0.94$ to $0.28\!-\!0.61$). Beyond increasing difficulty, our generated tasks more than double the number of unique tool combinations agents must execute. Our results suggest high scores on existing benchmarks often reflect saturation rather than robust task-solving ability. By automating the generation of difficult, high-coverage benchmarks, TASTE enables continuous, scalable evaluation of future agents.

### [205] [Tree of Thoughts as a Classical Heuristic Search Problem: Formal Foundations and Design Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28566)
*Guni Sharon*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文旨在通过引入经典启发式搜索的框架，对碎片化的大模型“思维树（ToT）”研究进行统一梳理，并探讨了不同搜索算法在解决大模型短视推理问题中的应用规律与未来挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的自回归预测方式具有短视性，容易导致推理过程中的级联错误。虽然思维树（ToT）框架提供了一种改进途径，但该领域的研究在术语和实现上处于碎片化状态。因此，本文旨在通过建立统一的分类体系，整合自然语言处理与自动化规划社区的相关研究，为LLM的推理过程提供系统的理论视角。

Method: 本文采用了文献综述与理论整合的研究方法。作者通过经典启发式搜索的术语，对现有的ToT研究进行了系统性分类和映射，包括状态表示（思维粒度）、后继生成（提示算子）以及启发式评估（自我进度评估）。此外，作者通过分析现有的设计模式，对比了不同搜索策略（如最佳优先搜索、深度优先搜索、蒙特卡洛树搜索）在不同任务类型中的应用表现。

Result: 研究梳理了ToT领域的现状，明确了核心设计模式：对于浅层、确定性任务，系统性的“最佳优先搜索（Best-First Search）”更为有效；而对于需要多步推理的深层任务，具有深度预测能力的策略（如DFS、MCTS）表现更好。文章还指出了启发式搜索与LLM结合时存在的关键算法挑战。

Conclusion: 本文通过将思维树（ToT）与经典启发式搜索相结合，为大模型推理研究提供了一个统一的理论框架。研究指出，未来应关注启发式搜索与大语言模型在更深层逻辑任务中的算法创新，并鼓励启发式搜索领域的研究者深入参与该交叉领域的研究。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable reasoning capabilities, yet their standard generation process -- auto-regressive token prediction -- is inherently myopic and prone to cascading errors. To address this, the Tree-of-Thoughts (ToT) framework creates a search space over intermediate reasoning steps, allowing search models to explore, look ahead, and backtrack. However, current ToT research remains fragmented across Natural Language Processing and Automated Planning communities, often using inconsistent terminology and ad-hoc implementations. Consequently, we synthesize the ToT landscape through a unified taxonomy based on classical heuristic search terminology. We map LLM-based reasoning to classical search components: state representation (granularity of thoughts), successor generation (prompting operators), and heuristic evaluation (self-assessment of progress). We analyze existing work within the context of our taxonomy and identify emerging design patterns: systematic search (Best-First Search) for shallow, deterministic tasks and lookahead-heavy strategies (DFS, MCTS) for deep multi-step reasoning. We conclude by identifying open algorithmic challenges at the intersection of heuristic search and LLM reasoning, and call on the heuristic search community to engage with this emerging domain.

### [206] [A Conflict-Aware Penalty and Statistical Loss Framework for Balancing Modalities and Enhancing Stability in Multimodal Sentiment Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28575)
*Jianheng Dai,Jiazhang Liang,Sijie Mai*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多模态情感分析（MSA）中，预训练文本编码器的表达能力显著强于声学和视觉模态，导致模型训练过程中文本模态往往处于主导地位，抑制了其他模态的学习，并引发梯度范数冲突，造成训练不稳定。

Method: 提出了一种冲突感知惩罚（Conflict-aware Penalty, CP）方法，用于在训练过程中检测并惩罚梯度范数冲突；同时引入了统计损失（Statistical Loss, SL），通过对齐预测分布统计量与输入统计量来优化训练。此外，框架结合了自适应模态编码、门控跨模态融合以及单模态辅助头，实现了模态间的协同优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在CMU-MOSI数据集上达到了当前最优（SOTA）性能，消融实验证实了CP和SL各组件在缓解模态冲突及提升模型表现方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的冲突感知惩罚（CP）与统计损失（SL）机制有效解决了多模态情感分析中单一模态主导导致的训练不稳定问题，为处理异构多模态数据的协同优化提供了一种高效且稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal Sentiment Analysis (MSA) fuses text, acoustic, and visual streams to infer sentiment. Because pre-trained text encoders are far more expressive than their acoustic and visual counterparts, the text modality tends to dominate optimization, suppressing weaker modalities and inducing gradient norm conflicts that destabilize training. To address this, we propose a Conflict-aware Penalty (CP) that detects and penalizes gradient norm conflicts at each training step, and a Statistical Loss (SL) that aligns predicted distribution statistics with empirical input statistics. Crucially, CP prevents dominant modality gradients from interfering with the SL objective, enabling synergistic training within a unified framework incorporating adaptive modality encoding, gated cross-modal fusion, and unimodal auxiliary heads. Experiments on CMU-MOSI demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with ablation studies confirming the effectiveness of each component.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了名为CARvE的对比嵌入方法，该方法利用基于检查点的锚定（checkpoint-based anchoring）和结构化回放（structured replay）技术，实现了高效的持续模型路由，以适应不断增加的专家模型和任务需求。

Result: 在包含超过2000个候选模型的CMRBench基准测试中，CARvE在模型、模型家族及领域级别的准确率上，均显著优于零样本检索、微调及适配器合并等基准方法。

Conclusion: CARvE框架通过对比学习和基于检查点的锚定机制，有效解决了模型仓库中专家模型扩展与路由策略更新的难题，在处理大规模预训练模型选择与路由任务时表现出显著的优越性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: AI model hubs provide access to a rapidly growing collection of powerful pre-trained models, enabling off-the-shelf mixture-of-experts systems with different routing strategies. In this paper, we formalise this setting as Continual Model Routing (CMR) and propose CMRBench, a new large-scale benchmark simulating realistic hub expansion and including over 2,000 candidate models. Finally, we introduce CARvE, a contrastive embedding approach for efficient continual model routing via checkpoint-based anchoring and structured replay. Extensive empirical results and ablations show that CARvE significantly outperforms zero-shot retrieval, fine-tuning, and adapter-merging baselines in model, family, and domain-level accuracy.

### [208] [MUSE: Benchmarking Manufacturable, Functional, and Assemblable Text-to-CAD Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28579)
*Xiaoyu Dong,Zhi Li,Xiao-Ming Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 MUSE——首个专注于复杂工业级 CAD 装配体生成的评估基准与框架，旨在通过多维度的工程准则（而非仅仅几何相似度）来推动 Text-to-CAD 技术向实用化迈进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Text-to-CAD 研究多集中于单一零件的几何近似，缺乏对工业实际应用中功能性、可制造性和可装配性的评估。因此，亟需一个能够评估复杂、可编辑 B-Rep 装配体并符合工程设计标准的 benchmark。

Method: 研究团队提出了 MUSE 基准测试，包含复杂的 B-Rep 装配体及配套的设计规范。评估方法采用三阶段协议：1) 代码执行检查；2) 几何合法性检查；3) 基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的专家打分系统，用于评估设计意图对齐度、功能性、可制造性和可装配性，并经人工标注验证其可靠性。

Result: 实验评估了多个开源与闭源 LLM，结果显示模型在“代码执行 -> 几何生成 -> 工程设计”这一链路中存在显著的性能衰减。即使是最强的模型，在细粒度的工程设计准则上表现依然有限，难以满足工业设计要求。

Conclusion: MUSE 为 Text-to-CAD 模型提供了一个从单纯的几何形状生成转向工业级工程设计生成的基准与评估框架。研究表明，当前主流大模型在处理复杂装配体、功能性、可制造性及可装配性方面仍存在巨大挑战，为未来的研究指明了方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have recently advanced text-driven 3D generation, yet Text-to-CAD remains far from supporting industrial product design. Existing benchmarks focus primarily on generating single-part CAD models and evaluate them using geometric similarity metrics that fail to capture functionality, manufacturability, and assemblability. To address this gap, we introduce MUSE, a Text-to-CAD benchmark focused on complex, editable boundary representation (B-Rep) assemblies. MUSE pairs practical design instances with structured Design Specifications and evaluates generated models through a three-stage protocol: code check, geometric check, and design-intent alignment. The final stage uses design-specific rubrics to assess functionality, manufacturability, and assemblability, moving beyond shape matching toward practical design quality. To enable scalable evaluation, we use a rubric-based visual language model (VLM) judge and validate its reliability through human annotation. Experiments on closed-source and open-source LLMs reveal a clear failure cascade from executable code to valid geometry and finally to engineering-ready design, with even the strongest models achieving limited success on fine-grained engineering criteria. Together, MUSE provides a realistic benchmark and evaluation framework for advancing Text-to-CAD from geometric generation toward true engineering design. Our project website, including the leaderboard, dataset, and code, is available at https://dong7313.github.io/muse-benchmark/.

### [209] [Satisfiability Solving with LLMs: A Matched-Pair Evaluation of Reasoning Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28602)
*Leizhen Zhang,Shuhan Chen,Sheng Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了现有LLM在SAT推理上的局限性，指出现有评估指标存在偏差，并提出了一种基于配对公式的准确区分率（ADR）评估方法，证实SAT是评估LLM逻辑推理能力的严苛且有效的测试基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在涉及布尔可满足性（SAT）问题的任务中应用日益广泛，但其核心推理能力仍不明确。现有研究多依赖常规指标，可能掩盖模型在复杂逻辑问题上的真实缺陷，因此需要更严谨、更具鲁棒性的评估框架。

Method: 本研究通过系统性评估LLM在2-SAT、3-SAT及其归约问题（顶点覆盖、离散3D填充）上的表现，指出传统指标的局限性。为此，研究引入了“配对公式协议”（Paired-formula protocol）和“准确区分率”（ADR）指标。同时，通过跨表示形式（从CNF转化为图或填充问题）的一致性测试，验证模型决策的鲁棒性。

Result: 实验发现，传统指标（如准确率、F1值等）在SAT任务中具有误导性；模型在处理超出特定规模的问题时性能急剧下降，且无法捕捉到3-SAT相变点的典型特征。采用ADR指标后，能够显著区分真正的推理模型与启发式模型。此外，大多数模型在不同问题表示形式间表现出高度的一致性（超过80%）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在SAT问题上的表现并不理想，现有的评估指标往往会产生误导。研究表明，基于“配对公式协议”和“准确区分率（ADR）”的评估方法能更真实地反映模型的逻辑推理能力，且模型在不同问题表示形式间表现出了一定的决策稳定性。SAT问题作为评估LLM推理能力的保守且严苛的基准，能够有效甄别模型的真实推理能力与简单的启发式猜测。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for tasks that implicitly reduce to Boolean satisfiability (SAT), yet their reasoning ability on SAT remains unclear. We present a systematic study of LLMs on 2-SAT and 3-SAT, together with two canonical reductions, Vertex Cover and discrete 3D packing, to probe representation-invariant reasoning. We first evaluate models using conventional metrics, including accuracy, precision, recall, and F1, as well as the SAT phase-transition setting. We find that these metrics can be misleading: many models obtain high scores by over-predicting satisfiable formulas, fail to reproduce the classical easy-hard-easy signature around the 3-SAT threshold, and degrade sharply as the number of variables grows.
  To address this problem, we introduce a paired-formula protocol based on minimally different satisfiable and unsatisfiable instances, together with Accurate Differentiation Rate (ADR), which requires both members of each pair to be classified correctly. ADR separates reasoning-oriented models from heuristic ones and correlates with witness validity. Beyond CNF, we test cross-representation consistency by converting CNF to Vertex Cover and 3-SAT to discrete 3D packing. Model decisions on CNF and on the corresponding graph or packing instances agree for most models on more than 80 percent of instances, suggesting stable decision rules across representations. Overall, our results show that SAT is a conservative probe for LLM reasoning, and that paired evaluation with ADR provides a more faithful and representation-robust assessment than conventional metrics.

### [210] [Adaptive Multimodal Agents-Based Framework for Automatic Workflow Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28607)
*Susanna Cifani,Mario Luca Bernardi,Marta Cimitile*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种两阶段多智能体框架：1. 离线发现阶段：通过分析零散的执行日志，自动构建任务拓扑知识库；2. 推理阶段：采用自适应检索增强生成（Adaptive RAG）技术结合图结构知识，并引入闭环协同验证协议，实现动态任务拆解与自我纠错。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于拓扑图的知识库能够有效弥补多模态智能体在复杂、非平稳环境下的决策缺陷，通过将离线任务拓扑挖掘与在线自适应检索相结合，显著提升了智能体在自动化工作流执行中的稳健性和语义理解能力。

Abstract: Modern information systems require autonomous agents capable of navigating complex workflows, yet current methodologies often struggle with the transition from structured metadata parsing to general environmental perception. While the integration of MLLMs has enabled agents to interact directly with GUIs, existing approaches typically treat task sequences as discrete, linear episodes. This fragmentation prevents agents from capturing the underlying transition topology, limiting their effectiveness in novel or non-stationary scenarios. To address this, we propose a novel multimodal multi-agent framework that achieves automatic workflow execution through a distinct two-phase pipeline. First, during an offline discovery phase, the architecture adaptively constructs a topological knowledge base from fragmented execution logs. During inference, agents leverage Adaptive Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) over this fixed, pre-established graph, coupled with a closed-loop collaborative verification protocol to dynamically self-correct and navigate. This graph-based approach facilitates superior task decomposition and adaptive navigation performance. We validate our framework in a real-world context, demonstrating its ability to maintain high reliability and semantic awareness even with limited training data.

### [211] [Identifying and Understanding Human Values in Text: A Tailorable LLM-based Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27373)
*Eduardo de la Cruz Fernández,Marcelo Karanik,Sascha Ossowski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种模块化的大语言模型架构，无需特定理论束缚即可从文本中识别并量化人类价值观，实现了价值概念化与检测的解耦，为构建具备伦理道德意识的智能系统提供了通用的技术框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着智能系统自主性的提高，传统的效用最大化模型已不足以满足伦理需求，迫切需要使智能系统能够识别并对齐人类价值观。现有研究多局限于特定价值理论或依赖复杂的提示工程，缺乏灵活性和通用性。

Method: 提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的三模块架构：1. 根据理论框架生成结构化的价值规范；2. 利用这些规范对文本进行标注；3. 基于修辞和语义证据，通过推理模型为价值支持或反对程度进行分级评估。该架构通过分离概念化与检测任务，实现了对不同价值理论的适配。

Result: 在 ValueEval 数据集上的实验结果表明，该架构在识别和量化文本中人类价值观方面表现良好，验证了其在不同大语言模型实例化下的通用性、可扩展性和可重复性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种通用且模块化的架构，能够有效将人类价值判断从特定理论中解耦，从而实现对文本中人类价值的灵活识别与强度量化，为构建符合伦理的智能系统提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: As intelligent systems become more autonomous, the scientific community focuses on creating decision-making mechanisms that include ethical and moral considerations, unlike traditional utility-maximisation models. To achieve this, a key aspect is assessing how well these decisions align with human values. To this end, a promising line of research is centred on developing approaches based on Large Language Models (LLMs) to identify human values from text, whether explicit or implicit, enabling their recognition throughout. This paper introduces a LLM-based architecture to detect and quantify the intensity of human values in text, avoiding the limitations of previous approaches tied to specific value theory or complex prompt engineering. The architecture comprises three coordinated modules: one that generates structured value specifications from the foundational texts of any theoretical framework; one that labels texts using these specifications; and one that assigns graded support or resistance based on rhetorical and semantic evidence. This modular approach separates the tasks of conceptualising from detecting human values, creating a scalable and reproducible process driven by value specifications adaptable to various theories. The architecture was instantiated with multiple LLMs and evaluated using the ValueEval dataset. The experiments demonstrate good detection performance, confirming the generality of the pipeline.

### [212] [Bandwidth-Efficient and Privacy-Preserving Edge-Cloud Many-to-Many Speech Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28642)
*Yexing Du,Kaiyuan Liu,Youcheng Pan,Bo Yang,Ming Liu,Bing Qin,Yang Xiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ESRT的协同边缘-云MLLM框架，通过特征压缩技术实现隐私保护与带宽优化，并利用课程学习策略克服了翻译任务中“以英语为中心”的局限，实现了高效的多语言语音翻译。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM语音翻译部署面临双重挑战：纯端侧模型受限于硬件资源，而云端方案存在隐私泄露风险及高带宽消耗；此外，现有模型普遍存在“以英语为中心”的偏见，限制了多对多翻译的扩展性。

Method: 1. 设计了边缘-云协同推断架构，在边缘侧保留轻量级语音编码器和适配器，仅传输压缩后的中间特征至云端；2. 引入多任务加权课程学习策略（Multi-task Weighted Curriculum Learning）及数据平衡方法，提升模型在多语言间的性能表现与鲁棒性。

Result: 在FLEURS数据集上的实验表明，ESRT-4B和ESRT-12B模型在45种语言的多对多翻译任务中均达到了SOTA性能；带宽需求降低了10倍，同时通过中间特征传输有效防止了原始语音的隐私泄露。

Conclusion: ESRT框架通过边缘-云协同推断和多任务加权课程学习，成功解决了MLLM在语音翻译任务中的隐私保护、带宽限制及多语言能力不均衡问题，为高效、安全的跨语言语音翻译提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have demonstrated significant potential for speech-to-text translation (S2TT). However, existing deployment paradigms face critical challenges: pure on-device models suffer from resource constraints, while centralized cloud systems incur severe privacy risks and bandwidth bottlenecks by transmitting raw voice data. Furthermore, most models exhibit English-centric biases, restricting many-to-many translation scaling. In this paper, we propose Edge-cloud Speech Recognition and Translation (ESRT), a privacy-preserving and bandwidth-efficient collaborative edge-cloud MLLM framework. Specifically, we design an edge-cloud split inference architecture that retains a lightweight speech encoder and adapter on the device, transmitting only highly compressed intermediate features to the cloud. This fundamentally prevents voiceprint leakage and reduces bandwidth requirements by up to 10$\times$. To overcome English-centric bottlenecks, we introduce a multi-task weighted curriculum learning strategy with data balancing to ensure robust cross-lingual consistency. Extensive experiments on the FLEURS dataset demonstrate that our models, ESRT-4B and ESRT-12B, achieve state-of-the-art many-to-many S2TT performance across 45 languages ($45 \times 44$ directions). Code and models are released to facilitate reproducible, privacy-aware MLLM S2TT research. The code and models are released at https://github.com/yxduir/esrt.

### [213] [The Ethics of LLM Sandbox and Persona Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28647)
*Tim Gebbie,Stewart Gebbie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文认为，大语言模型的安全护栏若过度干预，会人为制造扭曲的“现实差距”，即“现实洗涤”。这种行为将认知风险转嫁给用户，是本质上不道德的。作者主张用基于任务的因果规范取代底层的道德矫正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的护栏机制和人格设定人为制造了“现实差距”（Reality Gap），即模型描述的世界与用户所处的真实世界之间的脱节。论文旨在探讨这种行为是否构成一种将认知风险转嫁给用户的“现实洗涤”（Reality Laundering）行为。

Method: 通过类比金融监管（如巴塞尔协议、伦敦鲸事件）中形式合规导致真实风险转移的现象，剖析大语言模型中的护栏机制与人格设定。作者区分了“拒绝伤害”与“拒绝现实”的本质差异，并论证了为何当前的合规手段会导致现实扭曲。

Result: 指出当前的AI安全机制往往流于表面（合规性），通过抑制真实感知来掩盖深层的复杂机制。这种做法使得AI在面对高风险建议场景时，可能因为缺乏对真实风险的触达而导致严重后果。

Conclusion: 所谓的“伦理AI”若以机构性的虚假安慰替代对真实世界的感知，其实质反而变得不道德。论文主张应当将重点从底层的道德修饰转向任务层面的自上而下的因果需求规范。

Abstract: It is well known that LLM guardrails and trained persona dynamics can produce a reality gap: the distance between the world a LLM is permitted or shaped to describe, and the world in which users must act. Here we argue that actively generating reality gaps is in fact unethical because it knowingly shifts epistemic risk back to the uninformed user -- this is reality laundering. This can potentially cause harm when operationalised at scale. The risk is sharpest in high-exposure advice contexts, where users seek orientation rather than a bounded, externally checkable task. Guardrails naively appear ethically necessary when they claim to prevent direct harm, but often become suspect when they suppress truthful perception and launder uncomfortable mechanisms into acceptable abstractions. Basel-style financial regulation, B-BBEE-style compliance, Societe Generale, and the London Whale show how formal safety systems can become legible, gameable, and performative while real exposure migrates elsewhere. The same pattern can appear in LLMs as moral compliance: safe language, distorted reality. We therefore distinguish refusing harm, from refusing reality; and then argue for top-down causal requirements specification at the task level rather than bottom-up moral correction at the response or sandbox level. Persona dynamics matter because the assistant interface is not neutral; it shapes how uncertainty, conflict, authority, and risk are staged. The conclusion is that so-called ``ethical AI'' becomes substantively unethical when it substitutes institutional reassurance for contact with reality.

### [214] [AutoScientists: Self-Organizing Agent Teams for Long-Running Scientific Experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28655)

TL;DR: AutoScientists是一个去中心化的AI智能体框架，通过模拟科研团队的自组织、批判与协作机制，显著提升了长期科学实验的自动化水平、资源利用率及科研发现的质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AutoScientists架构，采用去中心化的AI智能体团队合作模式。该方法包含：智能体根据共享状态自组织形成小组以验证假设、在执行实验前进行同行评审机制以减少无效计算、以及建立知识共享机制以记录失败经验并避免重复探索。

Conclusion: AutoScientists证明了通过去中心化AI智能体团队协作，能够有效提升科学研究的效率和质量。该框架解决了传统单智能体或集中式规划在长期复杂实验中面临的探索局限、冗余计算及知识保留问题，为自动化科学发现提供了一种鲁棒且可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Scientific research proceeds through iterative cycles of hypothesis generation, experiment design, execution, and revision. AI agents can automate parts of this process, but existing approaches typically follow a single research trajectory or coordinate through a central planner with fixed objectives. As a result, they struggle to sustain parallel exploration, adapt as experimental evidence changes, or preserve knowledge of failed directions over long-running experiments. We introduce AutoScientists, a decentralized team of AI agents for long-running computational scientific experimentation. Agents interpret a shared experimental state, self-organize into teams around promising hypotheses, critique proposals before using experimental compute, and share successes and failures to reduce redundant exploration. Under matched experimental budgets, AutoScientists improves over prior AI agents across biomedical machine learning, language-model training optimization, and protein fitness prediction. On BioML-Bench, spanning biomedical imaging, protein engineering, single-cell omics, and drug discovery, AutoScientists achieves a mean leaderboard percentile of 74.4% across 24 tasks, improving over the strongest AI agent by +8.33%. On GPT training optimization, AutoScientists reaches a target validation bits-per-byte 1.9x faster than Autoresearch and continues discovering improvements from a starting champion where the single-agent approach finds none (7 vs. 0 accepted improvements). On ProteinGym fitness prediction, AutoScientists discovers a method for ACE2-Spike binding that improves over the current state-of-the-art model by +12.5% in Spearman correlation. Applied without modification across all 217 ProteinGym assays, the same method improves over the prior state of the art by +6.5% (Spearman correlation).

### [215] [DREAM-R: Multimodal Speculative Reasoning with RL-Based Refined Drafting, Precise Verification, and Fully Parallel Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28678)
*Yunhai Hu,Zining Liu,Xiangyang Yin,Tianhua Xia,Bo Bao,Eric Sather,Vithursan Thangarasa,Sai Qian Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DREAM-R 是一种通过强化学习对齐、严格验证机制和并行处理架构来加速大模型推理的新方法，在保持模型精度的前提下显著提升了推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的投机推理在处理大型多模态模型的推理任务时，由于草稿模型与目标模型在推理逻辑上的不一致，导致其加速效果受到严重限制。本研究旨在解决这种“对齐错位”问题，以提升推理任务的生成效率。

Method: 1. 投机对齐策略优化（SAPO）：利用强化学习目标训练草稿模型，使其生成的推理路径与目标模型高度一致且更加简洁。
2. 基于阈值的验证机制（TBVM）：引入基于比例的准则，仅在置信度高时接受推理步骤，有效抑制错误传播。
3. 全并行投机推理框架（FPSR）：实现草稿生成、目标推理与验证在多步推理中的完全并行化，支持早停与高效回退。

Result: 在多个重推理基准测试中，DREAM-R 实现了显著的推理加速，同时保持了与目标模型相当的准确率，证明了其在提升效率的同时不牺牲推理质量的有效性。

Conclusion: DREAM-R 框架通过通过强化学习对齐、阈值验证机制和全并行架构，成功解决了大模型推理任务中投机推理的效率与准确性权衡难题，为加速复杂推理任务提供了高效且鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Speculative reasoning has recently been proposed as a means to accelerate reasoning-intensive generation in large multimodal models, but its effectiveness is often constrained by misalignment between speculative drafts and target-verified reasoning. In this work, we introduce DREAM-R, a framework that substantially improves the performance of speculative reasoning. At its core, DREAM-R employs Speculative Alignment Policy Optimization (SAPO), a reinforcement-learning objective that trains draft models to generate reasoning steps that are both faithful to target trajectories and concise. We further propose a Threshold-based Verification Mechanism (TBVM) that uses a ratio-based criterion to provide stable and interpretable acceptance of speculative steps only when positive evidence clearly dominates, thereby preventing error propagation. Building on these components, we develop a Fully Parallel Speculative Reasoning (FPSR) framework that parallelizes draft generation, target-side reasoning, and verification across multi-step reasoning, enabling early stopping and clean fallback. Experiments on reasoning-heavy benchmarks demonstrate up to speedup while preserving target-model accuracy, yielding substantial efficiency gains without compromising reasoning quality.

### [216] [Beyond Binary Moral Judgment: Modeling Ethical Pluralism in AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28707)
*Aisha Aijaz,Rahul Goel,Arnav Batra,Raghava Mutharaju*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于伦理多元主义的AI道德推理框架，通过概率分布建模多种规范伦理理论，有效提升了AI在复杂道德困境中决策的解释力与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI道德决策方法多依赖标量或二元判断，缺乏解释性和对复杂语境的考量，无法满足高质量道德推理与问责的需求。

Method: 提出了一种“规范伦理单纯形（Normative Ethics Simplex）”框架，结合了规范性信息与双流规范-语义架构（Two-stream Normative-Semantic Architecture）；构建了一个包含450个道德困境案例的基准数据集，并利用堆叠集成学习（Stacked Ensemble Learning）模型来拟合功利主义、美德伦理学和义务论这三大理论及其15个子类别。

Result: 实验表明，融合语境与规范先验信息能够显著提升分类准确率，模型达到了88.89%的准确度。消融实验证明了结构化伦理表征优于单纯的类比推理，且堆叠集成架构因其逐步学习粒度的特性表现最优。

Conclusion: 将道德推理建模为规范伦理理论的概率分布（伦理多元主义）是可行的，这种方法能够支持类人的道德推理、分析道德分歧，并为AI系统的未来对齐提供有效路径。

Abstract: Critical decision-making in socially consequential spaces is increasingly involving AI systems at varying capacities. Yet, despite the ubiquity of autonomous systems, most approaches to handling autonomous moral decision-making resort to scalar or binary judgments. These methods are insufficient for acceptable moral reasoning, as they provide little explanation, leaving out imperative contextual and theoretical information that must be included to support accountability. For this, we propose a framework to model moral reasoning as a distribution over normative ethical theories or ethical pluralism. We introduce a normative ethics simplex that integrates these theories. A benchmark of 450 cases across 15 fine-grained subtheories was also prepared for the purposes of stacked ensemble learning. These cases describe ethical dilemmas in natural language and have associated extracted contextual features. The implementation of the simplex was achieved via a two-stream normative-semantic architecture. This is followed by the fusion of normative information and a sequential, stacking ensemble to learn the best fit of the three broad theories: consequentialism, virtue ethics, and deontology, and the 15 subcategories. Our experiments demonstrate that the integration of contextual and normative priors with the semantic embeddings significantly improves the performance of the classification, displaying an accuracy of 88.89%. We conducted ablation studies to show that structured ethical representations contribute beyond analogical reasoning, and the chosen stacking architecture gives the best results due to the gradual learning of granularity. Ethical pluralism is also analyzed through entropy, confidence, and visualization. Thus, modeling ethical pluralism as a probabilistic normative distribution supports human-like moral reasoning, ethical disagreement analysis, and future alignment in AI systems.

### [217] [Thinking as Compression: Your Reasoning Model is Secretly a Context Compressor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28713)
*Guoxin Ma,Yibing Liu,Chengzhengxu Li,Yu Liang,Yan Wang,Yueyang Zhang,Kecheng Chen,Zhaohan Zhang,Zhiyuan Sun,Daiting Shi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的上下文压缩方法通常依赖复杂的专用压缩模块或特定训练，未能充分挖掘大语言模型本身的内在压缩能力；此外，如何平衡压缩比与信息损失仍是长文本处理的挑战。

Method: 提出了“思考即压缩”（Thinking as Compression, TaC）范式，直接引导模型生成包含核心信息的思考轨迹；进一步引入了 TaC-C，通过简单的奖励驱动优化框架，约束思考过程的长度与质量，从而实现可控且高效的压缩。

Result: 在四个长上下文问答基准测试中，TaC-C 在 4 倍和 8 倍压缩率下表现卓越，平均 F1 分数分别领先最强竞争对手 17.4% 和 23.4%，平均精确匹配得分（EM）分别提升了 15.7% 和 21.7%。

Conclusion: 通过将模型自身的思考过程作为压缩后的上下文，TaC-C 证明了无需专用压缩模块即可实现高效的上下文压缩，为长文本处理提供了一种更具解释性和性能优势的新范式。

Abstract: Context compression aims to shorten long context inputs with minimal information loss for LLM inference acceleration. While existing methods have shown promise, they typically rely on complex compression modules or compression-specific training, leaving the intrinsic capabilities of LLMs underexplored. In contrast, this work reveals that a thinking model itself can naturally compress long contexts by organizing task-relevant information. We thus derive Thinking as Compression (TaC), a new compression paradigm that treats thinking itself as compressed context. Without relying on specific dedicated compressor, TaC directly prompts the thinking model to generate thinking traces as the shortened context, already outperforming most representative compression methods. Further, given that raw thinking output may struggle with budget control and shortcut behaviors, we introduce Thinking as Compression Constrained (TaC-C), leveraging a simple reward-driven optimization framework to elicit intrinsic thinking as compact and controllable compressed context. Experiments across four long-context QA benchmarks demonstrate that TaC-C consistently outperforms existing baselines. At 4x and 8x compression ratios, it surpasses the strongest competitor by 17.4% and 23.4% in average F1, and by 15.7% and 21.7% in average Exact Match Score (EM), respectively.

### [218] [Multi-Adapter Representation Interventions via Energy Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28722)
*Manjiang Yu,Hongji Li,Junwei Chen,Xue Li,Priyanka Singh,Yang Cao,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型表征干预中“一刀切”导致性能下降的问题，本文提出了 MARI 方法。它通过动态适配器和能量门控机制，根据不同输入自适应地调整干预强度和方向，在显著提升模型对齐效果与安全性的同时，有效保留并优化了模型的通用处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的表征干预方法通常对所有输入施加固定的干预，这导致了干预效果的普适性差，且容易损害模型在良性输入上的通用能力。因此，亟需一种能够根据样本特性动态调整干预策略的方法，以实现对齐效果与模型性能的平衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为“基于能量校准的多适配器表征干预”（MARI）的方法。该方法包含两个核心组件：1）竞争性多适配器机制，利用多个专家模型捕捉非线性修正模式，并为不同样本动态确定干预方向和强度；2）基于能量的门控模块，通过分析模型内部传播动力学来识别哪些样本需要进行干预，从而避免对无害输入造成不必要的干扰。

Result: 实验表明，MARI 在 TruthfulQA、BBQ 和多个安全性基准测试中均达到了最先进的性能，同时在 MMLU 和 ARC 等任务中不仅保持了原有的通用能力，甚至在某些情况下实现了性能提升。

Conclusion: MARI 通过引入样本感知的自适应干预机制，有效解决了传统静态表征干预方法在对齐效果与通用能力保持之间的权衡难题，为大模型的对齐提供了一种高效、灵活且具备可解释性的新范式。

Abstract: Representation intervention has emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning large language models toward desired behaviors without modifying model weights. Existing methods typically apply a fixed intervention uniformly across all inputs. However, we find that the appropriate intervention direction and strength vary substantially across samples, and such indiscriminate intervention leads to degradation of general capabilities on benign inputs. To address these challenges, we propose Multi-Adapter Representation Interventions via Energy Calibration (MARI). Specifically, we introduce a competitive multi-adapter mechanism in which specialized experts capture non-linear correction patterns and adaptively determine the appropriate intervention direction and strength for different samples. Furthermore, we design an energy-based gating module that leverages internal propagation dynamics to distinguish inputs that are applicable for intervention. Extensive experiments across diverse model families and parameter scales demonstrate that MARI achieves state-of-the-art alignment performance. Our method significantly improves performance on TruthfulQA, BBQ, and safety benchmarks, while maintaining and even improving general capabilities on tasks such as MMLU and ARC. Our code is available at https://github.com/V1centNevwake/MARI.

</details>


### [219] [Utility-Aware Multimodal Contrastive Learning for Product Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28733)
*Xiaohang Feng,Yiling Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种效用感知多模态对比学习框架，通过优化新型损失函数，使生成式AI不仅能生成与文本语义一致的图像，还能通过融入消费者需求数据，提升产品图像的实际市场销售转化率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成式AI模型虽然能实现文本与图像的高度语义对齐，但并未直接优化电商市场的商业转化表现。语义对齐并不等同于能够促进销售，因此亟需一种能将消费者需求转化为视觉生成导向的机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为“效用感知多模态对比学习”（Utility-Aware Multimodal Contrastive Learning）的框架。该方法通过引入一种新型的“效用感知InfoNCE损失函数”（Utility-Aware InfoNCE loss），将消费者的购买需求数据融入到图像-文本的表征学习过程中，引导生成模型在保持语义一致性和图像保真度的同时，侧重于生成能提升市场需求的视觉特征。

Result: 在亚马逊和Airbnb的数据集上，该方法生成的图像在提升市场需求方面优于现有的先进模型。实验结果显示，该方法不仅提升了产品的商业吸引力，还成功保留了美学和独特性等属性的“倒U型”需求规律，并通过人类主观评估验证了其商业实效性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功将消费者需求指标整合进多模态对比学习框架中，不仅证明了语义对齐并非电商转化的唯一决定因素，还通过理论和实证研究表明，需求导向的表征空间学习能显著提升生成图像的商业性能，为生成式AI在电商领域的实际应用提供了新路径。

Abstract: Product images strongly influence consumer decision-making in online marketplaces. Empowered by multimodal contrastive learning, generative AI can output images that closely align with text prompts. Yet existing generative AI models do not directly optimize marketplace performance. This is a critical gap, since semantic alignment alone does not guarantee that an image will sell. To address this limitation, we propose a \textit{utility-aware multimodal contrastive learning} framework that incorporates consumer demand into a novel Utility-Aware InfoNCE loss. Optimizing this utility-aware objective guides generation toward images that are both semantically coherent and demand-enhancing. This effect arises directly from a shift in the learned image-text representation space toward demand-driven visual cues, which we also validate through the theoretical bound of the proposed objective. In downstream applications on Amazon and Airbnb, product images generated and edited by our method outperform state-of-the-art models in increasing demand and preserving fidelity, while maintaining text-image consistency. Notably, our utility-aware framework preserves inverse U-shaped demand patterns for attributes such as aesthetics and uniqueness, improving demand-based performance while preserving fidelity and semantic consistency. Human-subject experiments further validate its commercial effectiveness. As generative AI technology continues to evolve, our utility-aware component can be flexibly embedded into emerging generative models to improve direct commercial use.

### [220] [CORE: Contrastive Reflection Enables Rapid Improvements in Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28742)
*Linas Nasvytis,Simon Jerome Han,Ben Prystawski,Satchel Grant,Noah D. Goodman,Judith E. Fan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CORE的非参数化学习算法，通过对比成功与失败的推理轨迹并将其转化为自然语言见解，显著提升了语言模型在推理任务中的学习效率，减少了对训练数据和计算资源的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型推理提升方法（如RLVR等参数化方法或提示词优化等非参数化方法）通常需要大量的训练样本和模型展开（rollouts），计算成本高昂且在某些场景下不可行。因此，研究人员寻求一种更高效、数据需求更少且具备可解释性的自我提升方法。

Method: 提出了一种非参数化学习算法——对比反思（CORE）。该算法通过对比过往的成功与失败的推理轨迹，自动生成简短的自然语言见解，用于总结推理策略和约束条件，并将其整合到后续推理任务中。

Result: 在四项推理任务中，CORE相比参数化（GRPO）和多种非参数化基准方法（如GEPA、episodic RAG等），能以更少的模型展开次数实现更快的性能提升；在极小样本（仅5个样本）的情况下，依然保持了优于或持平的性能，且在上下文窗口的利用上更具效率。

Conclusion: 对比反思（CORE）证明了将成功与失败推理轨迹之间的差异提炼为自然语言见解，是实现模型自我提升的一种比参数更新、提示词优化或直接重用轨迹更高效、更具可解释性的路径。

Abstract: Language models can use verifiable rewards to improve at a wide variety of reasoning tasks. However, both parametric (e.g. RLVR) and non-parametric (e.g. prompt optimization) approaches to doing so typically require hundreds of training samples and thousands of model rollouts, making them expensive in the best case and intractable in the worst. To address this challenge, we introduce Contrastive Reflection (CORE), a non-parametric learning algorithm that compares past reasoning traces to generate insights: short natural-language descriptions of reasoning strategies and constraints that capture differences between successful and unsuccessful problem attempts. Across four reasoning tasks, we demonstrate that CORE enables more rapid improvement than both parametric (GRPO) and non-parametric (GEPA, episodic RAG, and MemRL) methods, while using fewer rollouts. Under fixed rollout budgets with as few as five training samples, we then show that CORE also achieves comparable or greater performance gains than each baseline. Finally, we highlight how CORE is also substantially more context-efficient than non-parametric baselines, requiring fewer prompt tokens while storing learned knowledge as compact, interpretable natural-language insights. Our results therefore suggest that distilling contrasts between successful and unsuccessful reasoning traces into abstract and useful insights can provide a more efficient and interpretable route to model self-improvement than weight updates, prompt optimization, or direct reuse of stored reasoning traces.

</details>


### [221] [CubePart: An Open-Vocabulary Part-Controllable 3D Generator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28763)
*Yiheng Zhu,Kangle Deng,Jean-Philippe Fauconnier,Inaki Navarro,Daiqing Li,Ava Pun,Yinan Zhang,Peiye Zhuang,Xiaoxia Sun,Maneesh Agrawala,Kiran Bhat,Tinghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CubePart是一个能够根据用户定义的语义部件需求，生成可控且直接适用于游戏引擎的3D模型框架，解决了传统生成模型输出资产难以整合进动画与物理系统的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的生成式3D模型大多产生单一网格或随意的部件划分，无法满足游戏与模拟中对特定语义部件（用于动画、物理模拟等）的需求，导致生成的资产难以直接投入实际应用，需要大量的手动后处理。

Method: 1. 构建大规模开放词汇、带部件标签的3D数据集；2. 采用两阶段生成架构：第一阶段进行全局形状合成，第二阶段进行局部零件解码；3. 在推理阶段引入用户自定义的“部件模式（parts schema）”作为明确的控制信号，确保生成的多个零件能拼装成连贯的整体。

Result: CubePart能够根据全局文本提示和用户定义的部件列表，生成一组逻辑连贯且语义对齐的3D网格。这些生成的资产可直接导入游戏引擎并应用于动画和脚本控制，无需人工后续处理，在可控性和实用性上表现优异。

Conclusion: CubePart成功证明了在生成式3D建模中引入显式部件控制的可行性。通过将全局形状合成与局部部件解码解耦，该框架实现了高度可控、符合特定应用需求的3D资产生成，填补了生成式模型与实际游戏开发工作流之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Interactive 3D assets used in games and simulation are typically decomposed into specific semantic parts to support animation, physics, and scripted behaviors, yet most generative 3D models produce either monolithic meshes or arbitrary part decompositions that cannot be aligned with application-specific requirements. We present CubePart, a generative framework for open-vocabulary, part-controllable 3D mesh generation that exposes part structure as an explicit inference-time control signal. Given a global text prompt and a user-defined parts schema expressed as an open-ended list of part names, our method generates a set of meshes - one per schema element - that assemble into a coherent object while respecting the specified semantic structure. To enable this capability, we introduce a scalable data pipeline to construct a large open-vocabulary, part-labeled 3D dataset, along with a two-stage generative architecture that separates global shape synthesis from part-level decoding. We demonstrate that the resulting assets can be directly integrated into game engines and driven by animation and behavior scripts without manual post-processing. Project Page: https://cubepart.github.io/

</details>

### [222] [$E^3$-Agent: An Executable and Evolving Agent for Resource Management of Edge Generative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27428)
*Rui Bao,Yaping Sun,Zhiyong Chen,Feng Yang,Meixia Tao,Nan Li,Wenjun Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: $E^3$-Agent 是一种用于边缘 AIGC 的自适应资源管理器，通过将快速路由与基于 LLM 的慢速元控制器相结合，实现在复杂、动态的边缘环境中实时调整配置，显著降低了延迟并提升了系统稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘计算中 AIGC 推理面临模型性能未知及环境非平稳（如负载波动、设备变动）的挑战，导致传统的离线调优资源管理器难以维护且表现脆弱，因此迫切需要一种能够在线学习并实时适应环境变化的资源管理机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为 $E^3$-Agent 的架构，采用“快路径路由 + 慢路径 LLM 元控制器”的分层控制策略：快路径负责毫秒级的调度决策，慢路径则通过工具接口（风险门控、配置、性能校准）动态调整策略，并基于在线执行反馈持续进化以适应非平稳环境。

Result: 实验结果表明，$E^3$-Agent 在多种动态场景下表现优异，平均延迟较最优静态基准降低了 65%-73%，性能与全信息在线 Oracle 仅有 7%-10% 的差距，并能有效抑制语义降级导致的卡顿现象。

Conclusion: $E^3$-Agent 通过结合快路径路由决策与慢路径 LLM 元控制，实现了边缘侧 AIGC 资源管理的高效自适应，证明了利用 LLM 进行动态环境下的资源调度具有显著优势。

Abstract: Edge deployments of generative inference increasingly face two practical realities: per-device per-model performance is often unknown at deployment time, and it is non-stationary due to user-driven semantic events, background load, and device churn. Consequently, a resource manager that is tuned offline under a fixed regime can become brittle and expensive to maintain. This paper presents $E^3$-Agent, an executable and evolving agent for edge artificial intelligence generated content (AIGC) resource management. $E^3$-Agent separates a fast-path router that makes millisecond-level dispatch decisions from a slow-path, event-driven large language model (LLM) meta-controller that mitigates regime shifts through a small, explicit control surface exposed via a tool interface, including risk gating, router configuration, and rapid performance calibration. The agent learns online from execution feedback and continuously adapts to unknown and time-varying service-time mappings. We evaluate $E^3$-Agent in a discrete-event simulator driven by MLPerf-derived device-model measurement priors, covering cold-start warmup and three dynamic regimes: semantic dynamics, device churn, and hidden drift. Across the dynamic scenarios, $E^3$-Agent reduces average latency by 65%-73% compared to the best static baseline, stays within 7%-10% of an online full-information Oracle used for evaluation, and effectively suppresses stutter rate under semantic degradation.

</details>


### [223] [Detect by Yourself: Self-Designing Agentic Workflows for Few-Shot Graph Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27470)
*Tairan Huang,Qiang Chen,Yili Wang,Yueyue Ma,Changlong He,Xiu Su,Yi Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SignGAD 是一种基于智能体工作流的图异常检测框架，通过动态构建检测流程并结合守卫式微调策略，解决了少样本场景下模型适应性差及异常证据利用不充分的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图异常检测方法面临两大核心痛点：一是受限于固定模型架构，导致在有限监督下的任务适应性较弱；二是难以显式整合上下文与结构性异常证据，导致异常检测的证据链较弱。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SignGAD 的框架：1）将异常检测任务重构为“任务驱动的检测工作流设计”，根据具体任务动态选择图编码和检测器组件；2）引入“守卫式最终微调策略（guarded final refit strategy）”，通过校准微调的接受度，增强了模型在少样本条件下的鲁棒性和可靠性。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，SignGAD 在少样本异常检测任务中显著优于现有的前沿方法，验证了该框架在利用任务特定证据和提升检测性能方面的有效性。

Conclusion: SignGAD 通过将图异常检测任务从固定的训练模式转变为任务驱动的智能体工作流设计模式，有效解决了传统方法在少样本场景下适应性差及异常信号利用不足的问题，证明了智能体在复杂图学习任务中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Graph anomaly detection aims to identify anomaly nodes in attributed graphs and plays an important role in real-world applications. However, existing graph anomaly detection methods still face two key challenges: 1) fixed pipelines, which restrict their adaptability across different graph tasks under limited supervision; 2) weak evidence, which prevents them from explicitly incorporating contextual and structural anomaly signals into the detection process. In this paper, we propose a novel framework, self-designing agentic workflows for few-shot graph anomaly detection (SignGAD). Specifically, we propose a novel paradigm that reformulates graph anomaly detection task from training a fixed anomaly detector to designing task-conditioned detection workflows. By constructing detection workflows, SignGAD selects suitable graph encodings and detector designs to exploit task-specific anomaly evidence. Meanwhile, we introduce a guarded final refit strategy to refine the selected workflow by calibrating refit acceptance, enhancing reliability under limited supervision. Extensive experiments conducted on several real-world datasets demonstrate that SignGAD achieves strong performance against state-of-the-art methods, highlighting its effectiveness on graph anomaly detection tasks.

</details>


### [224] [Balancing Fidelity and Diversity in Diffusion Models via Symmetric Attention Decomposition: Hopfield Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27476)
*Hyunmin Cho,Woo Kyoung Han,Kyong Hwan Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究将 Transformer 注意力矩阵分解为对称（能量）和反对称（循环）两部分，通过 Hopfield 动力学分析解释了模型特征检索的稳定性，并据此提出了一种调节生成保真度与多样性权衡的控制方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 Transformer 在各种任务中取得了成功，但其注意力机制背后的动力学机制尚不清晰。研究者旨在从 associative memory（联想记忆）的角度，通过数学分解揭示注意力矩阵如何编码特征关联及驱动潜在动力学，从而更好地理解和控制模型的生成行为。

Method: 1. 将 Transformer 中的预 Softmax 注意力矩阵分解为对称成分（定义能量景观）和反对称成分（驱动能量景观上的循环）；2. 利用对称成分诱导的能量公式，推导出用于量化特征检索稳定性的 Hopfield 风格稳定性度量；3. 提出通过调节注意力矩阵中的循环（反对称成分）来动态控制生成过程中保真度与多样性之间权衡的方法。

Result: 实验表明，Hopfield 风格的稳定性度量与生成模型中的保真度-多样性权衡存在显著的相关性。基于此发现，研究者提出了一种可控的调节机制，能够通过修改注意力矩阵的循环部分，实现对生成结果属性的有效调制。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了 Transformer 注意力矩阵中对称与反对称成分的物理意义，并将这种动力学特征与生成模型的保真度-多样性权衡联系起来，为模型控制和性能优化提供了新的理论视角和调节工具。

Abstract: We characterize the pre-softmax attention matrix $\mathbf{QK^\top}$ in transformers as an associative memory matrix encoding pairwise associations between input features. By decomposing this matrix into its symmetric and skew-symmetric parts, we interpret the symmetric component as governing the structure of the energy landscape, and the skew-symmetric component as driving circulation on that landscape. Leveraging the energy formulation induced by the symmetric component, we derive Hopfield-style stability measures that quantify the stability of retrieved features. We observe meaningful correlations between Hopfield-style stability measures and the fidelity-diversity trade-offs in generation. Finally, we propose a controllable knob to modulate this trade-off by modifying the circulation of the underlying dynamics. Code is available at our GitHub (https://github.com/hyeon-cho/Attention-Symmetric-Decomposition).

</details>


### [225] [Energy-Structured Low-Rank Adaptation for Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27482)
*Longhua Li,Lei Qi,Qi Tian,Xin Geng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 E^2-LoRA 的持续学习方法，通过将知识集中于低秩主导方向并动态分配秩，有效解决了传统正交子空间方法导致的能量弥散和容量消耗问题，在多项基准测试中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续学习（CL）正交子空间方法存在能量在基向量间弥散的问题，导致知识压缩效率低下并过快耗尽模型容量。研究者旨在通过分析参数更新引起的输出特征漂移，寻找更有效的参数更新策略，以在保持任务性能的同时优化容量利用率。

Method: 提出了一种名为 E^2-LoRA 的方法。该方法基于输出特征漂移的低秩特性，通过理论证明确定了沿主导方向保存参数的必要性。核心机制包括：1) 将知识显式地排序并集中在低秩空间中；2) 设计了一种动态秩分配策略，通过联合优化能量保留和模型塑性来平衡稳定性与塑性。

Result: 在多个持续学习基准测试中的实验结果表明，E^2-LoRA 在保持任务性能的同时显著提升了知识存储效率，达到了当前该领域的最优性能（SOTA）。

Conclusion: E^2-LoRA 通过在主导方向上进行知识压缩和动态秩分配，有效地解决了持续学习中的任务干扰和参数空间受限问题，实现了性能的最优权衡，是目前持续学习领域的一种前沿解决方案。

Abstract: While orthogonal subspace methods try to mitigate task interference in Continual Learning (CL), they often suffer from energy diffusion across the basis, hindering knowledge compaction and exhausting capacity for future tasks. We observe that output feature drift induced by parameter updates is inherently low-rank, and theoretically prove that preserving parameters along the principal directions of this drift minimizes the output reconstruction error. Motivated by this, we propose \textbf{E}nergy-Concentrated and \textbf{E}nergy-Ordered \textbf{Lo}w-\textbf{R}ank \textbf{A}daptation (E$^2$-LoRA). By explicitly ordering and concentrating knowledge into leading ranks, E$^2$-LoRA frees capacity for subsequent tasks. Furthermore, we design a dynamic rank allocation strategy to balance stability and plasticity by jointly optimizing energy retention and model plasticity. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that E$^2$-LoRA achieves state-of-the-art performance.

</details>


### [226] [Information-theoretic Multimodal Representation Learning for Electrocardiogram Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27583)
*Phu X. Nguyen,Konstantinos Kontras,Wei Dai,Huy Phan,Christos Chatzichristos,Paul Pu Liang,Bert Vandenberk,Maarten De Vos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MERIT，一种结合掩码ECG建模与跨模态对比学习的预训练框架。该方法从信息论角度出发，成功整合了ECG波形的生理结构与临床语义，在分类任务及辅助文本生成中表现优异，显著提升了模型在精细化医疗诊断中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态ECG模型往往难以同时保留ECG波形中从宏观诊断到微观形态的多层次生理结构，临床报告无法完全覆盖信号细节。研究旨在通过信息论方法构建一种能够同时保持ECG结构完整性并融合语义信息的表征学习框架，以解决传统方法在精细化诊断上的不足。

Method: MERIT（Multimodal ECG Representation via Information Theory）：该方法采用双分支预训练框架。一是引入掩码ECG建模（Masked ECG Modeling），旨在通过信息论目标函数捕捉ECG信号的多尺度波形结构；二是采用ECG-文本对比学习（Contrastive Alignment），将临床语义特征融入表征空间。两者结合，在联合优化的基础上实现结构与语义的对齐。

Result: 在PTB-XL等基准数据集上，MERIT表现优异，在All类和SubClass分类任务上分别实现了超过3%和5%的F1分数提升。在零样本（Zero-shot）场景下同样表现稳健，AUC和F1分别提升了2.66%和2.11%。此外，该模型生成的表征在辅助大语言模型进行临床文本生成时，显著提升了生成文本的质量。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MERIT框架通过信息论视角成功统一了ECG波形结构特征与临床语义特征，证明了在预训练阶段同时利用掩码建模和跨模态对比学习是提升ECG表征临床价值的有效途径，为精细化心血管诊断与报告生成提供了更强大的基础模型。

Abstract: Electrocardiograms (ECGs) are widely used non-invasive measurements of cardiac activity and play a central role in clinical diagnosis. Recent multimodal approaches align ECG signals with clinical reports to incorporate diagnostic semantics, but clinical reports often fail to preserve the rich physiological structure of ECG waveforms, particularly across multiple levels of abstraction ranging from coarse diagnostic categories to fine-grained morphology. To address this limitation, we formulate ECG representation learning from an information-theoretic perspective and derive a tractable objective that jointly preserves signal structure and integrates clinical semantics. Based on this principle, we propose \textbf{MERIT} (Multimodal ECG Representation via Information Theory), a dual-branch pretraining framework combining masked ECG modeling with ECG--text contrastive alignment. Extensive experiments on PTB-XL and additional benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over prior methods, including gains exceeding $3%$ F1 on PTB-XL All and $5%$ F1 on SubClass classification. In zero-shot evaluation, MERIT further improves performance by up to $ +2.66\%$ AUC and $ +2.11\%$ F1 on PTB-XL SubClass, while also demonstrating robustness under multiple distribution-shift settings. Moreover, leveraging the learned ECG representations for ECG-conditioned clinical text generation with large language models improves text quality across several metrics, including ROUGE and METEOR. Together, these results demonstrate that MERIT learns more informative and clinically meaningful ECG representations, particularly for fine-grained clinical applications.

</details>


### [227] [Evaluating Local Explainability Metrics for Machine Learning Models on Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27618)
*Tomás Pereira,João Vitorino,Eva Maia,Isabel Praça*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过对LIME、SHAP等主流局部可解释性技术进行大规模基准测试，揭示了这些方法的可靠性与模型表现并无直接关联，并指出数据特征分布与复杂度才是制约解释效果的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管可解释性技术被广泛应用，但其生成的解释往往难以真实反映模型内部的推理机制（即“表面合理但实质不符”）。本文旨在探究在复杂表格分类任务中，现有局部可解释性技术在评估指标下的可信度，以解决解释的可靠性问题。

Method: 研究者针对LIME、SHAP和特征消融（Feature Ablation）三种主流局部可解释性技术进行了基准测试。在32个复杂表格分类数据集上，评估了这些技术在忠实度（Faithfulness）、鲁棒性（Robustness）和复杂性（Complexity）三个维度的表现，并对比了模型在“共识正确”与“共识错误”样本上的表现差异。

Result: 实验结果表明，解释结果与模型预测准确率之间并不存在必然的相关性。相反，解释的可靠性高度依赖于输入数据集的复杂程度及特征本身的分布特征。在面对复杂数据时，现有的流行解释方法可能无法提供准确反映模型逻辑的解释。

Conclusion: 模型解释的质量并不直接等同于模型预测性能的优劣。数据集的复杂度和特征分布是影响可解释性技术可靠性的核心因素，研究结果强调了在实际应用中需审慎对待现有局部可解释性工具生成的解释。

Abstract: Despite the wide use of explainability techniques to attempt to understand the behavior of Artificial Intelligence (AI), the generated explanations may not always be reliable. An explanation can appear plausible to humans but fail to capture the internal reasoning of a model, particularly when dealing with complex tabular data. This paper studies the trustworthiness of local explainability techniques when applied to complex tabular classification tasks, considering evaluated metrics for three main properties: faithfulness to the model's predictions, robustness to input data variations, and complexity of the explanation itself. A benchmark was performed for Local Interpretable Model-Agnostic Explanations (LIME), Kernel SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP), and Feature Ablation techniques, across 32 datasets and different types of machine learning models. Model performance ranges were analyzed to identify two groups: consensus-correct, which are samples that all models predicted correctly, and consensus-wrong, samples that all models predicted incorrectly. The obtained results demonstrate that that the explanations are not always correlated with a model's predictive performance. Instead, dataset complexity and feature distributions seem to be the main factors affecting explanation quality and reliability.

### [228] [Supervised Distributional Reduction via Optimal Transport and Dependence Maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27619)
*Sai-Aakash Ramesh,Archit Sood,Andrew Corbett,Tim Dodwell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了监督分布缩减（SDR）算法，通过融合Gromov-Wasserstein目标与依赖最大化技术，学习既保留数据几何特征又具备强预测能力的紧凑表示，并进一步利用该方法构建了用于非平稳高斯过程建模的自适应核函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数据压缩与预测精度之间取得平衡是一个核心挑战。现有的分布缩减方法（结合了聚类与降维）虽然能有效总结数据，但在保留特定任务相关的关键信号（即监督信息）方面研究尚不充分。因此，需要一种能够同时捕捉内在几何结构与目标相关结构的表示学习方法。

Method: 该研究提出了一种名为“监督分布缩减”（SDR）的算法。该算法基于融合Gromov-Wasserstein（FGW）目标函数，将输入分布的结构关系与一组代表性点进行对齐；在此基础上，引入了一个明确的依赖最大化项，以确保学习到的嵌入不仅反映数据的几何结构，还最大限度地保留了预测任务所需的监督信号。此外，该方法还通过目标感知分布对齐重新定义了距离度量，从而构建出能够适应局部数据结构与预测目标变化的自适应核函数。

Result: 实验结果表明，SDR方法能够生成既紧凑又具有高度预测相关性的表示。同时，在应用层面，该方法所衍生的数据依赖型非平稳几何结构，能有效提升高斯过程（GP）在处理复杂数据建模任务时的表现，通过最优传输视角为非平稳核函数的设计提供了理论支撑与应用价值。

Conclusion: 本文提出的监督分布缩减（SDR）方法成功结合了最优传输与依赖最大化，为学习既保留数据几何结构又具备强预测能力的紧凑表示提供了一种统一且有效的框架。该方法不仅在表示学习上表现优异，还通过构建自适应核函数为非平稳高斯过程建模开辟了新思路。

Abstract: Learning representations that capture both intrinsic data geometry and target-relevant structure remains a fundamental challenge, particularly in settings where data reduction must balance compression with predictive fidelity. While distributional reduction-encompassing joint clustering and dimensionality reduction-offers a principled way to summarize data, its supervised variants remain relatively under-explored, despite the importance of retaining task-relevant signal for downstream prediction and decision-making. We propose Supervised Distributional Reduction (SDR), an algorithm for learning target-aware representations by combining optimal transport with explicit dependence maximization. SDR builds on the Fused Gromov-Wasserstein (FGW) objective to align the relational structure of the input distribution with a set of representative points, while augmenting it with a direct dependence term that encourages the learned embeddings to capture predictive signal more explicitly. This results in compact representations that reflect both geometric structure and supervision. Beyond representation learning, SDR naturally induces a data-dependent, non-stationary geometry that can be leveraged for settings such as Gaussian Process (GP) modelling. By redefining distances through target-aware distributional alignment, SDR enables the construction of adaptive kernels that respond to local variations in both data geometry and supervision, offering an optimal transport-based perspective on non-stationary kernel design.

### [229] [Aligning LLMs with Human Uncertainty: A Beta-Bernoulli Calibrator for LLM Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27668)
*Hui Dai,Ryan Teehan,Parsa Torabian,Mengye Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Beta-Bernoulli校准器（BBC）的新方法，通过整合二元结果和众包数据，将LLM的点预测转化为概率分布，显著提升了概率预测的校准精度与认知不确定性估计能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM概率预测方法通常仅依赖二元结果进行 verbalized 预测，忽视了众包预测中包含的概率估计和专家一致性等丰富信息。因此，本研究旨在探索如何有效利用这些众包信号来提升概率预测的准确性和校准性。

Method: 提出了一种名为Beta-Bernoulli校准器（BBC）的方法。该方法将模型的初始点估计转换为事件可能性的分布（Beta分布），利用二元结果和众包预测数据进行监督学习，通过Beta分布的均值获取校准后的点预测，并利用方差量化认知不确定性。

Result: 实验结果证明，BBC在校准精度和预测准确性上均优于传统的后验校准方法及专门微调的预测模型；此外，BBC捕获的认知不确定性比模型自身的言语置信度更能可靠地预测预测误差。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过结合二元结果和众包预测信息，Beta-Bernoulli校准器（BBC）能够有效地提升大语言模型的概率预测能力。该方法不仅在校准精度上优于传统方法和微调模型，还能提供更可靠的认知不确定性度量。

Abstract: Probabilistic forecasting estimates the likelihood of uncertain future events. To improve LLM forecasting, existing methods typically learn from binary outcomes to output verbalized forecasts. However, while aggregated human forecasts contain rich information in both the crowd probability estimate and the degree of agreement among forecasters, how to utilize these signals remains underexplored. To address this, we propose the Beta-Bernoulli Calibrator (BBC), which converts an initial point estimate forecast from any model into a distribution over event likelihood, using supervision from both binary outcomes and human forecasts. BBC models event likelihood $p \sim \text{Beta}(α, β)$ and outcome $y \sim \text{Bernoulli}(p)$, with the mean as the calibrated point forecast and the variance as the epistemic uncertainty. Our results show that BBC generally provides better calibrated and more accurate forecasts than both traditional post-hoc calibration methods and models fine-tuned specifically for forecasting, while remaining lightweight and having good generalization. We also show that the epistemic uncertainty captured by BBC is a more reliable predictor of forecasting error than verbalized confidence.

### [230] [Heterogeneous Parallelism for Multimodal Large Language Model Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27678)
*Yashaswi Karnati,Kamran Jafari,Akash Mehra,Li Ding,Pranav Prashant Thombre,Ali Roshan Ghias,Shifang Xu,Parth Mannan,Yu Yao,Hao Wu,Eric Harper,Ashwath Aithal,Nima Tajbakhsh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型训练，提出了一种异构并行训练框架，允许模型中不同模块采用独立的并行化策略，显著提升了算力利用率和训练吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型训练中，单一的并行策略（如针对LLM优化的布局）难以同时兼顾结构迥异的编码器和LLM，特别是在长上下文任务中，固定布局限制了系统吞吐量和硬件资源的高效利用。

Method: 研究提出了一种“异构并行”（Heterogeneous Parallelism）抽象，允许计算图中的不同模块（如编码器与LLM）采用独立的并行布局（TP/CP/PP/DP/EP）和资源部署方案。通过引入“边界通信器”（Boundary Communicators）实现跨布局的前向激活转换和反向梯度路由，并扩展了调度机制，支持在共享GPU上共置或在不同GPU组上分离执行。

Result: 在多模态工作负载和不同规模GPU集群上的实验表明，共置异构并行将GPU TFLOPS提升了高达49.3%；非共置异构并行则使聚合令牌吞吐量提升了13.0%，GPU TFLOPS提升了9.6%，且保证了模型损失收敛的一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的异构并行机制有效地解耦了多模态模型中不同模块的并行策略，解决了传统单一并行布局导致的资源浪费和通信瓶颈问题，为大规模多模态模型训练提供了更高的灵活性和硬件利用率。

Abstract: Foundation model training is becoming multimodal, from post-training pipelines to large-scale pretraining. As modality coverage broadens, context windows grow, and encoder LLM scales diverge, a single LLM-centric TP/CP/PP/DP/EP layout increasingly limits throughput. This coupling forces encoders to inherit LLM-driven sharding and placement choices that can add communication, limit encoder parallelism, or constrain the LLM schedule; the mismatch is most pronounced at long contexts, where LLM context parallelism is needed for the fused multimodal sequence but encoder inputs remain bounded. We present heterogeneous parallelism for multimodal large language model training, an abstraction that lets modules in one end-to-end graph use independent layouts and rank placements, supporting colocated execution on shared GPUs and non-colocated execution on disjoint rank sets. The key challenge is preserving boundary tensor semantics across independent layouts: forward activations must be materialized for the destination layout, while backward gradients must be routed back to the source layout. We address this with boundary communicators that implement forward and backward layout transforms, plus scheduling extensions for both placement modes. We evaluate optimized homogeneous, colocated heterogeneous, and non-colocated heterogeneous configurations across multimodal workloads and GPU scales to characterize when added layout and placement freedom exposes a better operating point. Across this sweep, colocated heterogeneity improves TFLOPS/GPU by up to 49.3%, while non-colocated heterogeneity improves aggregate token throughput by up to 13.0% and TFLOPS/GPU by up to 9.6%. We validate loss convergence parity against homogeneous baselines and release the system as an open-source Megatron-LM extension.
