### [231] [Bayesian Deployment Approval for Learned Landing Controllers under Finite Rollout Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27720)
*Fei Jiang,Lei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对强化学习自主控制器提出了一种贝叶斯审批框架，通过不确定性量化与顺序验证，解决了仅凭有限模拟经验指标评估系统部署风险导致过度自信的问题，为自主系统的安全部署提供了更稳健的决策依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习与自主控制器评估主要依赖有限模拟下的经验指标（如累积奖励和成功率），这些指标无法提供足够的统计证据来证明系统在不确定性环境下的部署安全性，往往导致对系统准备情况的误判。

Method: 1. 建立基于触地安全满足条件的概率着陆能力模型。2. 利用贝叶斯后验推断量化学习策略的真实部署能力。3. 引入“后验审批概率”和“后验部署风险”作为评估指标。4. 开发支持“批准/拒绝/继续”决策的顺序验证框架。

Result: 仿真实验（基于PPO和SAC控制器）显示，在验证数据有限的情况下，基于传统经验指标的评估倾向于产生过度自信的判断。相比之下，所提出的贝叶斯审批推断能够提供更具统计意义且经过不确定性校准的部署准备度评估。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，仅依靠经验指标（如累积奖励或成功率）评估强化学习策略存在过度自信的风险。通过引入贝叶斯审批框架，可以在有限的实验数据下，实现对自主系统部署准备情况的统计学严谨评估，从而提升安全性和可靠性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning and data-driven autonomous controllers are commonly evaluated using cumulative reward and empirical success frequency under finite simulation trajectories. However, such empirical metrics do not necessarily provide sufficient statistical evidence regarding deployment readiness under uncertainty. This work develops a Bayesian approval framework for learned autonomous landing controllers under finite rollout evidence. A probabilistic landing capability formulation is introduced based on touchdown safety satisfaction under uncertain operating conditions, while Bayesian posterior inference is used to quantify uncertainty regarding the true deployment capability of learned policies. Posterior approval probability and posterior deployment risk are further introduced for deployment-oriented evaluation, together with a sequential validation framework supporting approve/reject/continue decisions during progressive rollout testing. Simulation experiments using PPO and SAC controllers demonstrate that empirical success and reward optimization may produce overconfident deployment interpretation under limited validation evidence, whereas posterior approval inference provides a more uncertainty-calibrated assessment of deployment readiness. The proposed framework provides a practical statistical connection between conventional reinforcement-learning evaluation and deployment-oriented validation under uncertainty and may be generalized to broader classes of learned autonomous systems.

### [232] [Can Entry-Wise Clipping Give Spectral Control of Stochastic Gradients?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27733)
*Zitao Song,Cedar Site Bai,Zhe Zhang,Brian Bullins,David F. Gleich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型训练中由重尾梯度噪声引起的训练不稳定性，本文提出了一种低成本、高效的逐元素平滑收缩方法，显著提升了训练效率并能够与现有谱归一化技术互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型训练中常见的损失峰值（loss spikes）主要源于随机梯度噪声。由于训练数据中存在罕见表达以及多层组合效应，梯度噪声呈现重尾分布，且难以通过简单的Mini-batch平均消除。现有的向量范数裁剪（缺乏对矩阵结构的考虑）或谱归一化（计算成本高）方案存在局限性，作者旨在寻找一种在结构控制与计算成本之间取得更好平衡的方案。

Method: 作者通过一阶扰动分析发现梯度噪声具有局部化特性，进而推导出了一个在高斯信号先验下的贝叶斯最优逐元素估计器的易处理替代方案（即平滑收缩方法）。该方法通过对梯度进行逐元素的裁剪或收缩，在不引入高额矩阵运算成本的情况下实现了谱控制。

Result: 理论上，在柯西分布噪声干扰下，该方法建立了O(ε⁻⁴)的收敛保证。实验证明，在NanoGPT预训练任务中，使用平滑收缩方法相比标准Adam优化器节省了约7%的训练Token；将其应用于Muon优化器之前，可在Muon的基础上额外节省约2%的Token。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于逐元素收缩的梯度正则化方法，通过一阶扰动分析证明了其在控制重尾梯度噪声方面的有效性。该方法计算高效且易于实现，既能独立提升训练效率，也能与谱归一化方法（如Muon）兼容并进一步优化性能。

Abstract: Training instabilities such as loss spikes are frequently the result of stochastic gradient noise. Because of rare expressions in language training data, and multiple layer composition, the noise impact is heavy-tailed and survives mini-batch averaging. Existing remedies trade off structure against cost: vector-norm clipping ignores the matrix structure of weight updates, while spectral normalization (e.g., Muon (Jordan et al., 2024)) respects it at additional cost. We show that this trade-off can be balanced. Real gradient noise appears to be similar to entry-wise heavy-tailed contamination, and a first-order perturbation analysis reveals a localization property of such noise, under which a simple entry-wise method achieves spectral control. Exploiting this, we derive a tractable surrogate for the Bayes-optimal entry-wise estimator under a Gaussian signal prior. We establish $O(ε^{-4})$ convergence guarantee under Cauchy-contaminated noise. Empirically, we find that smooth shrinkage improves Adam on NanoGPT pretraining, saving ${\sim}7\%$ of training tokens. We further find that applying the entry-wise clipping before spectral normalization yields a ${\sim}2\%$ token saving on top of Muon.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Online reinforcement learning is becoming increasingly important for aligning diffusion models with non-differentiable objectives. However, existing methods still face limitations in assigning fine-grained credit along denoising trajectories and in realizing stable value-based optimization. We propose a state-aligned latent actor-critic framework for diffusion post-training, in which the diffusion model serves as its own timestep-conditioned value function and predicts values directly on noisy latent states. This enables trajectory-level PPO training, supports stable actor-critic optimization with simple conditioning and value pretraining strategies, and naturally allows the learned critic to be reused for inference-time steering. We further extend the framework to multi-reward optimization, where joint training with complementary rewards helps alleviate reward hacking. Across both UNet- and DiT-based backbones, our method consistently outperforms prior group-relative RL and actor-critic baselines on single-reward and multi-reward benchmarks, while test-time steering provides additional gains in generation quality.

### [234] [A Paired Testing Protocol for Batch-Conditioned Refusal Robustness in LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27763)
*Sahil Kadadekar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了批处理配置对大语言模型安全评估的影响，发现批处理环境会导致小规模的行为翻转，并建议在评估时必须考虑生产环境的批处理配置以确保结果的可重复性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的安全评估通常将服务配置视为固定的背景设施，忽视了批处理（batching）作为变量可能对评估结果产生影响。研究旨在探究在不同并发或调度配置下，同一提示词是否存在评估结果的不一致性。

Method: 研究采用了一套包含四个部分的配对测试协议：(A) 本地发现、评分校正及批处理确认测试；(B) 跨模型泛化性测试；(C) 连续批处理组合测试；(D) 批处理不变内核消融实验。通过对比模型在不同批处理条件下的输出稳定性，量化分析了批处理带来的行为翻转率。

Result: 研究发现，批处理环境确实会导致模型安全行为发生翻转（尽管比例较低，约为0.16%），且安全类标签的变化比能力类标签更频繁。实验表明，输出的不稳定性是导致这种脆弱性的核心因素（相关性达0.909），而特定的内核配置（如vLLM的批处理不变模式）可以有效消除这种不确定性。总体而言，未发现全局性的安全偏向干扰。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了批处理配置（如并发、调度策略）会对大语言模型的安全评估产生干扰，导致评估结果的不稳定性。作者建议采用“精确栈验证”（exact-stack validation）方法，即在实际部署的批处理环境下进行评估，并将行为翻转与聚合性能指标分开报告，以确保评估的准确性。

Abstract: Safety evaluations of language models often treat serving configuration as fixed background infrastructure, but batch condition is an untested treatment variable whenever the same prompt may be evaluated alone, in a synchronized batch, or inside a continuous-batching scheduler. We synthesize four artifact-backed studies into a paired testing protocol: Study A combines local discovery, scorer-corrected adjudication, and true-batching confirmation; Study B tests cross-model generalization; Study C tests continuous-batch composition; and Study D runs a batch-invariant-kernel ablation. The local test finds safety-label changes more often than capability-label changes (0.51% vs. 0.14%), but adjudication of 63 candidate rows leaves only 17 genuine behavioral flips, implying a corrected full-set rate of 0.16%. The 15-model extension finds no detectable universal safety-over-capability skew: flips are near parity (0.94x), alignment type has no detectable association ($p=0.942$, $η^2=0.033$), and output instability is the strongest tested fragility screen ($r=0.909$, bootstrap 95% CI [0.65, 0.97]). In the targeted kernel ablation, standard vLLM reproduces 22/55 label flips on current score-flip candidates, while enabling VLLM_BATCH_INVARIANT=1 reduces the same test to 0/55 flips; the composition test separately finds no aggregate effect at 4.7pp sensitivity. The testing recommendation is exact-stack validation: evaluate refusal at the served batch setting, pair safety prompts with capability controls, and report low-rate directional flips separately from aggregate null effects.

</details>


### [235] [Restoring the Sweet Spot: Pass-Rate Weighted Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27765)
*Zehao Liu,Yuanpu Cao,Jinghui Chen,Vasant G. Honavar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 SC-SDPO 方法，通过引入基于模型预测置信度的动态加权机制，优化了大语言模型的自我蒸馏强化学习过程，实现了更高效的信度分配，显著提升了模型在复杂任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习方法（如 GRPO）通过组相对优势实现了对中等难度问题的学习聚焦，而基于 KL 散度的 SDPO 缺乏这种难度感知机制，导致模型在学习过程中无法有效分配信度，限制了训练效率和性能提升。因此，研究旨在引入一种类似于 GRPO 的难度加权机制来优化 SDPO 的学习过程。

Method: 该研究提出了一种名为 SC-SDPO 的改进方案。其核心方法是通过分析 GRPO 的优势归一化机制，推导出 SDPO 的损失函数应根据 $[\hat{p}(1-\hat{p})]^{1/2}$ 进行加权。这些权重通过在线策略采样和批次自适应归一化（batch-adaptive normalization）获取，从而构建了一个随模型能力动态演进的隐式学习课程。

Result: 实验结果表明，SC-SDPO 在科学推理和工具使用基准测试中均优于标准 SDPO。在 Qwen3-8B 模型上，mean@16/maj@16 指标分别提升了 3.2 和 4.3 个百分点；在 OLMo-3-7B 模型上分别提升了 1.8 和 3.0 个百分点，同时保持了训练过程的稳定性。

Conclusion: SC-SDPO 通过引入基于任务难度（即模型预测置信度）的自适应加权机制，成功弥补了传统 SDPO 在难度感知上的不足。该方法不仅实现了更有效的信度分配，而且在不增加额外计算开销的前提下，显著提升了大型语言模型在推理和工具使用任务中的性能，证明了通过归一化梯度来隐式构建学习课程的有效性。

Abstract: Self-Distillation Policy Optimization (SDPO) provides dense token-level credit assignment for reinforcement learning with large language models by leveraging the model's own feedback-conditioned predictions as a self-teacher. Unlike GRPO, however, whose group-relative advantage naturally concentrates learning on a sweet spot of intermediate-difficulty questions, SDPO's KL-based advantage lacks an implicit notion of difficulty awareness.
  We analyze this gap through the lens of GRPO's advantage normalization. Extending the learnability framework to normalized rewards, we show that normalization absorbs the variance term $p(1-p)$, equalizing leading-order learnability across questions and leaving $\sqrt{p(1-p)}$ as the sole residual scaling factor in the per-question gradient. This analysis yields a simple prescription: weight each question's SDPO loss by $[\hat{p}(1-\hat{p})]^{1/2}$, resulting in SC-SDPO, a scale-consistent variant of SDPO.
  The proposed weights are obtained as a zero-cost byproduct of on-policy rollouts with batch-adaptive normalization, inducing an implicit curriculum that dynamically tracks the model's evolving competence. Experiments on scientific reasoning and tool-use benchmarks demonstrate that SC-SDPO consistently improves over SDPO, yielding gains of +3.2/+4.3 (mean@16/maj@16) on Qwen3-8B and +1.8/+3.0 on OLMo-3-7B, while preserving stable training dynamics throughout optimization.

</details>


### [236] [Fine-Tuning Dynamics of In-Context Factual Recall in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27774)
*Ruomin Huang,Eshaan Nichani,Jason D. Lee,Rong Ge*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型如何通过上下文学习来触发和检索内部参数中存储的事实知识。研究通过定义“上下文事实召回”（IC-recall）任务，从理论和实验上证明了 Transformer 能通过学习特定的成对注意力模式，以极高的样本效率实现事实知识的检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的上下文学习（In-context learning）理论研究多关注如何从提示词（prompt）中提取纯粹的信息，而忽略了模型如何利用其参数中存储的大量事实性知识。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索模型如何将上下文作为线索来触发并检索内部存储的事实知识。

Method: 1. 形式化定义“上下文事实召回”（IC-recall）任务：模型需根据上下文提供的 (主体, 答案) 对推断隐含关系，并从内部记忆检索对应的答案。
2. 构建简化的 Transformer 模型：使用具有单层 MLP 关联记忆的 Transformer，存储 (主体, 关系, 答案) 三元组。
3. 理论分析：推导模型在监督微调下的动态过程，证明其收敛于特定的成对注意力机制。
4. 实验验证：通过仿真实验验证理论预测，并测试预训练 MLP 层下的表现。

Result: 1. 证明了 Transformer 在 IC-recall 任务中可以通过极少量的样本（对存储知识库大小呈多对数级）完成学习。
2. 揭示了模型实现该任务的关键机制：收敛于一种特定的成对注意力模式。
3. 实验证明该注意力机制具有稳健性，即使在 MLP 层是预训练而非人工构造的情况下，该模式依然能够涌现。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明和实验验证表明，Transformer 能够通过学习特定的成对注意力模式（pairwise attention pattern）来高效地执行上下文事实召回任务。这种机制不仅在人工构建的存储中有效，在预训练的 MLP 层中也能自然涌现，且所需的微调样本量极小。

Abstract: In-context learning \ -- performing tasks based on examples given in the prompt \ -- is an important capability that has emerged in large language models and has received significant attention in both theory and practice. Existing theoretical work often focuses on settings where the learning uses information purely from the prompt. However, many practical instances of in-context learning require the model to retrieve factual knowledge stored in the model's parameters, with the context serving to identify which knowledge is relevant. In this work, we study how in-context learning leverages factual knowledge recall. We formalize this behavior by introducing the \emph{in-context factual recall (IC-recall)} task, where a transformer is provided a context of (subject, answer) pairs generated from a hidden relation, along with a query subject, and must both infer this hidden relation and retrieve the corresponding answer. Factual knowledge is modeled by the transformer having access to a simple pre-constructed MLP associative memory storing (subject, relation, answer) triplets. We analyze the supervised fine-tuning dynamics of a one-layer transformer on IC-recall data and prove that the model successfully performs IC-recall by converging to a particular pairwise attention pattern. This fine-tuning stage requires a very small number of samples \ -- only polylogarithmic in the number of stored knowledge triplets. Experiments verify our theoretical predictions and show that the pairwise attention pattern emerges even when the MLP layer is pretrained instead of constructed.

### [237] [Revisiting ML Training under Fully Homomorphic Encryption: Convergence Guarantees, Differential Privacy, and Efficient Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27782)
*Yvonne Zhou,Mingyu Liang,Ivan Brugere,Danial Dervovic,Yue Guo,Antigoni Polychroniadou,Min Wu,Dana Dachman-Soled*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 引入了基于多项式近似的梯度下降法，以适配FHE对非线性运算的限制；2. 设计了一种新型差分隐私机制，通过避免传统的逐样本梯度裁剪来降低计算开销；3. 提出了与数据无关的超参数选择策略及多项式近似的理论基础。

Result: 1. 首次为FHE下的机器学习训练提供了理论收敛性证明；2. 在保持相当模型效用的前提下，相比标准的差分隐私梯度下降（DP-GD）显著提升了计算效率；3. 提供了一套无需逐样本裁剪的隐私保护框架，验证了该方案在可扩展加密学习中的可行性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过理论证明和算法改进，克服了全同态加密（FHE）与差分隐私（DP）结合在机器学习训练中的效率瓶颈。研究表明，在不需要昂贵的逐样本梯度裁剪的情况下，利用多项式近似进行加密训练是可行且高效的，为处理敏感数据提供了兼顾隐私、安全与效率的实用方案。

Abstract: We present the first theoretical convergence analysis of machine learning training under fully homomorphic encryption (FHE), combined with a differentially private (DP) training algorithm tailored to encrypted computation. Our approach improves computational efficiency over standard differentially private gradient descent (DP-GD) while achieving comparable utility. In particular, we prove convergence of approximate gradient descent using polynomial approximations of activation and loss functions, which are required for FHE compatibility. To preserve privacy in downstream tasks, we integrate differential privacy without relying on costly per-sample gradient clipping, enabling scalable encrypted learning. We also provide data-independent hyperparameter selection and theoretically grounded strategies for polynomial approximation which can be of independent interest. Together, these contributions advance the feasibility of efficient, private, and secure machine learning on sensitive data.

### [238] [Locality-Aware Redundancy Pruning for LLM Depth Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27786)
*Vincent-Daniel Yun,Youngrae Kim,Woosang Lim,YoungJin Heo,Minkyu Kim,Sunwoo Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型深度冗余问题，本文提出了一种无需训练的深度剪枝框架LoRP，通过计算“表征局部性分数”量化层间相似度，实现按需剪枝，有效提升了推理效率与模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM深度剪枝方法往往过度依赖局部重要性或假设架构具有固定的冗余度，忽略了不同模型架构间冗余分布差异（局部集中或全局分布）的问题。为了解决这一痛点，作者旨在提出一种能够感知表征局部性的通用剪枝框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为“表征局部性分数（RLS）”的指标，用于衡量模型层间的全局隐藏状态相似度；利用该指标将模型层进行聚类，并根据簇内的残余冗余度进行自动化的深度剪枝分配，无需任何训练过程。

Result: 在多种主流LLM架构上进行实验，结果表明LoRP方法在保持甚至提升困惑度（Perplexity）及下游任务准确率的同时，实现了有效的模型深度压缩。

Conclusion: LoRP框架成功证实了利用表征局部性（Representation Locality）进行无训练深度剪枝的有效性，通过动态量化层间冗余，在不牺牲模型性能的前提下显著提升了大模型的推理效率，为模型压缩提供了一种高效且具备通用性的新方案。

Abstract: Large language models are known to contain representational redundancy across network depth, making depth pruning an effective approach for improving inference efficiency. Existing one-shot pruning methods rely on local layer importance or fixed redundancy assumptions across architectures. We propose Locality-Aware Redundancy Pruning (LoRP), a training-free one-shot depth pruning framework guided by representation locality. We show that inter-layer redundancy can be either localized or globally distributed depending on the LLM architecture. To characterize this phenomenon, we introduce Representation Locality Score (RLS), derived from global inter-layer hidden-state similarity. Using a small calibration set, LoRP computes pairwise layer similarity, clusters layers by representational similarity, and allocates pruning according to residual intra-cluster redundancy. Experiments across diverse LLM families show improvements in both perplexity and downstream task accuracy.

### [239] [Knowing When to Ask: Segment-Level Credit Assignment for LLM Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27788)
*Abhijit Kumar,Zoey Wu,Mohit Suley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CARL 是一种通过强化学习训练模型“何时求助”的新方法。它通过对工具调用轨迹进行自动分解并赋予精确的归因，使模型能够自动区分哪些问题可以用自身知识解决，哪些需要调用工具，从而大幅提升了小参数模型的性能并降低了冗余的工具调用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型（LLM）缺乏判断何时需要外部工具（如计算器）的自我认知能力。传统的提示工程难以解决这一边界问题，而基于轨迹的强化学习由于缺乏对单次工具调用贡献的精确归因，往往无法有效惩罚不必要的工具使用或奖励关键的工具调用。

Method: 提出了“能力感知强化学习”（CARL）。该方法训练一个评价器（critic）来识别模型的参数化知识边界，通过在自然工具使用边界（如代码块分隔符）处分解执行序列，无需外部裁判或逐步标注，利用单次二元结果为每个片段分配独立的奖励信号，从而实现对不必要或错误工具调用的精确归因。

Result: 在五个涵盖算术、多跳问答和财务表格推理的基准测试中，CARL显著优于现有的强化学习基线。在7B模型上准确率提升了6.7个点，3B模型上提升了9.7个点。此外，该模型在可直接回答的问题上减少了53%的工具调用，且准确率保持稳定；研究发现小参数模型从“感知工具使用边界”中获益更多。

Conclusion: CARL通过学习模型的能力边界，成功实现了在无需人工标注的情况下，优化语言模型调用外部工具的决策能力。该研究证明，对于参数规模较小的模型，明确何时利用工具比仅仅提升计算规模更能显著提高任务处理精度，从而实现了更高效的计算资源利用。

Abstract: Humans know when to reach for help e.g. $347 \times 28$ warrants a calculator while $2+2$ does not. Language models do not. Prompt-based approaches can instruct a model when to invoke tools, but this scaffolding does not teach it to recognize the boundary of its own knowledge. RL approaches that assign a single outcome reward to the whole trajectory fare no better: trajectory-level credit cannot isolate which tool call in a successful episode actually helped, nor penalize unnecessary calls. We propose \textbf{CARL} (\textbf{C}ompetence-\textbf{A}ware \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{L}earning), which trains a critic on the model's own rollouts to learn where parametric knowledge suffices and where it needs external help. By decomposing each rollout at natural tool-use boundaries (e.g., code fence delimiters and context block transitions), CARL assigns independent credit to each segment from a single binary outcome, without external judges or step-level annotations. As a result, erroneous tool calls, incorrect extractions, and unnecessary calls each receive appropriately signed advantages. The trained critic captures the model's domain competence: it separates parametrically solvable from tool-dependent questions with AUC 0.93 at 7B. On five benchmarks spanning arithmetic, multi-hop factual QA, and numerical reasoning over financial tables, CARL improves exact-match accuracy by 6.7 points at 7B and 9.7 points at 3B over the best RL baseline, with the largest gain (+8.3 EM at 7B, +9.0 EM at 3B) on Musique. The model issues 53\% fewer tool calls on parametrically answerable questions while remaining ${\sim}10$ EM points more accurate on them. Gains are largest at small scale: the 3B improvement is $1.4\times$ the 7B improvement, suggesting that knowing when to ask disproportionately benefits models with smaller parametric memory.

</details>

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models have accelerated open-vocabulary EEG-to-imagined-text decoding, where non-invasive neural activity recorded during visual perception is translated into coherent natural language descriptions of viewed stimuli. However, existing systems remain highly vulnerable to biological noise, where corrupted neural projections induce hallucinated or semantically unstable generation in frozen language models. We introduce SYNAPSE (Symbolic Neural Alignment for Precise Semantic Extraction), a lightweight neuro-symbolic framework that stabilizes neural text generation through inference-time symbolic regularization. By purifying EEG-derived semantic candidates using commonsense graph structure and latent exemplars, SYNAPSE improves semantic stability without end-to-end LLM fine-tuning. Experiments across popular EEG decoding benchmarks and multiple frozen LLM backends demonstrate consistent gains over unconstrained prompting baselines, robustness under object-label ablation, and performance commensurate with substantially more resource-intensive fine-tuned systems, while preserving biometric privacy by localizing raw EEG processing entirely within the encoder stack.

### [241] [Density-aware Sample-specific Attack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27809)
*Qiyuan Wang,Yao Li,Raymond K. W. Wong*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用干净数据分布低密度区域构造后门触发器的新方法，通过分布引导确保攻击在微调和剪枝防御下依然具有极高的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的后门攻击方法极易受到微调（fine-tuning）或剪枝（pruning）等后训练防御手段的抵御，导致攻击失效。研究旨在寻找一种更鲁棒的触发器构造策略，以克服这些防御措施。

Method: 作者推导了基于贝叶斯最优模型下样本特定触发器的构建准则，提出了一种双层优化框架，通过条件时间评分匹配（conditional time-score matching）估计密度比，并利用混合模型目标函数将触发样本引导至干净数据分布的低密度区域。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在防御前攻击成功率超过99%，在微调防御下，攻击成功率比最强基线高出50至85个百分点；在神经元剪枝防御下展现出完全免疫，没有任何神经元被识别为需要移除。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，目前的后门防御范式在面对利用数据分布稀疏区域的攻击时存在根本性缺陷，强调了开发能够超越干净数据分布支持域的防御技术的紧迫性。

Abstract: Despite recent progress in backdoor attacks, existing methods remain susceptible to post-training defenses that erase the backdoor through fine-tuning or pruning. We revisit the core objectives of backdoor attacks and derive principled criteria characterizing optimal sample-specific trigger construction under a Bayes-optimal model of the victim's training. Our analysis reveals that both attack success and clean-accuracy preservation are simultaneously optimized when triggered samples are steered into low-density regions of the clean data distribution, a distributional condition that controls all moments of the poisoned distribution at once rather than a handful of input-space summary statistics. We introduce a bilevel optimization framework that estimates density ratios via conditional time-score matching and optimizes a mixture-model objective to place triggered samples in these sparse regions. Extensive evaluations on MNIST, CIFAR-10, GTSRB, and TinyImageNet demonstrate that our method achieves above 99\% attack success rate before defense and retains 50--85 percentage points higher post-defense ASR than the strongest baselines under fine-tuning defenses. Against neuron-pruning defenses, the method exhibits complete immunity, with zero neurons identified for removal across all pruning thresholds. These results expose a fundamental gap in current defense paradigms and underscore the need for defenses that operate beyond the support of the clean distribution.

</details>


### [242] [ReSAE: Residualized Sparse Autoencoders for Multi-Layer Transformer Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27819)
*Prathyush Poduval,Calvin Yeung,Neel Desai,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决多层稀疏自编码器（SAE）干预中的信息冗余和交互问题，本文提出了残差稀疏自编码器（ReSAEs），通过对残差进行训练，有效提升了多层模型干预的准确性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逐层训练的 SAE 忽略了 Transformer 残差流激活在深度上的强耦合性，导致不同层的字典重复表示相同信息，且多层同时替换时会产生意料之外的交互，影响干预效果。

Method: 提出残差稀疏自编码器（ReSAEs）。该方法在选定层之间拟合仿射映射，并让后续层的 SAE 仅针对未解释的残差部分进行训练，而不是针对完整的激活值；重建后的信息通过仿射链映射回原始空间以维持干预协议的兼容性。

Result: 在 Pythia-1.4B 和 Gemma-2-9B 模型上的实验表明，ReSAEs 降低了解码器的冗余度，改善了稀疏探测和目标扰动效果；在多层替换场景下，尽管其对原始激活方差的重建能力略低，但能恢复更多的 Transformer 交叉熵。

Conclusion: 移除层间线性可预测的结构是进行多层稀疏自编码器（SAE）干预的有效默认方法。ReSAEs 能够更好地捕捉对模型下游计算至关重要的特征，从而在多层干预中展现出优于传统 SAE 的性能。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders are usually trained one layer at a time, even though transformer residual stream activations are strongly coupled across depth. This creates a practical problem for multi-layer interventions: different layerwise dictionaries can spend capacity representing the same carried-forward information, and replacing several layers at once can produce interactions that are not predicted by single-layer behavior. We introduce Residualized Sparse Autoencoders (ReSAEs), which fit an affine map between selected layers and train each later-layer SAE on the unexplained residual rather than on the full activation. Reconstructions are mapped back into the original activation space through the fitted affine chain, so ReSAEs can be evaluated with the same intervention protocols as ordinary SAEs. On Pythia-1.4B and Gemma-2-9B, residualization reduces decoder redundancy and improves sparse probing and targeted perturbation in most tested settings. Despite reconstructing less of the raw activation variance, ReSAEs recover more transformer cross entropy under multi-layer replacement. This gain is clearest under teacher-forcing and at sufficient sparsity online, indicating that ReSAEs preserve the components of the activation most relevant to the model's downstream computation. These results suggest that removing linearly predictable cross-layer structure is a useful default for multi-layer SAE interventions.

### [243] [Reward Transfer from Inverse Reinforcement Learning: A Coupled Minimax Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27834)
*Guang-Yuan Hao,Lars van der Laan,Aurélien Bibaut,Nathan Kallus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种处理逆强化学习中奖励跨环境迁移的耦合估计方法，通过联合求解源与目标环境的贝尔曼方程，有效降低了迁移过程中的误差传播，提高了学习效率与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在逆强化学习中，从受控环境收集的专家演示数据往往难以直接迁移至新的目标环境中。现有的顺序迁移方法受限于源环境的估计偏差，导致迁移效果不佳，因此需要一种更具稳健性的跨环境奖励迁移框架。

Method: 作者将问题建模为源环境与目标环境联合的贝尔曼方程组，并推导了目标软Q函数的极大极小（minimax）估计量。与传统的“先估计源奖励再代入目标问题”的顺序方法不同，该方法采用耦合求解策略，能够有效抵消源环境估计误差的传播。

Result: 理论分析表明，耦合方法消除了源环境贝尔曼残差的一阶影响，并给出了有限样本下的软Q函数误差界和策略遗憾界（regret bounds）。脓毒症模拟实验证实了耦合方法在性能上显著优于传统的顺序估计方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种联合估计源环境和目标环境价值函数的方法，该方法在理论上优于传统的顺序估计方法，通过消除源环境贝尔曼残差的一阶影响，显著提高了迁移学习的稳健性和性能，并通过脓毒症模拟实验得到了验证。

Abstract: We study the transfer of rewards learned using inverse reinforcement learning from expert demonstrations in one environment to reinforcement learning in a new, different environment. This arises naturally when demonstrations are collected in a controlled environment. We formulate the problem as a joint system of Bellman equations across the source and target environments and develop minimax estimators for the target soft-$q$-function. Whereas a sequential solution approach first estimates the source reward and then plugs it into the target control problem, a coupled approach solves the source and target system of equations jointly. We show that, in contrast to the sequential approach, the coupled approach removes the first-order influence of source Bellman residual error. We characterize the local behavior of each approach, develop finite-sample soft-$q$-function error bounds, and prove regret guarantees for the resulting soft-control policy. An empirical investigation using a sepsis simulator validates the theoretical comparison.

### [244] [CAREF: Calibration-Aware Regularization for Explanation Faithfulness Without Rationale Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27835)
*Naphat Nithisopa,Teerapong Panboonyuen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CAREF 是一种新型参数高效微调框架，通过统一的“校准感知”损失函数，在无需理由标注的前提下，仅利用极少量的参数即实现了大语言模型预测精度与解释忠实度的同步提升，性能优于 LoRA 等现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型解释性微调方法往往需要在预测准确性和解释忠实度之间进行权衡，且通常依赖昂贵的理由（Rationale）标注，或者在计算资源消耗上过高。因此，作者旨在构建一个能够在保持低参数量的前提下，无需额外标注即可兼顾模型预测效果与解释准确性的统一框架。

Method: 提出了名为 CAREF 的参数高效微调框架，核心在于引入了“校准感知解释忠实度正则化（LSCED）”损失函数。该方法通过结合基于熵的校准（Entropy-based calibration）与基于标记的稀疏性控制（Token-level sparsity control），在无需人类理由标注的情况下，实现了预测准确度与解释忠实度的联合优化。

Conclusion: CAREF 是首个将熵正则化与稀疏性控制统一在单一训练目标下的高效微调框架，证明了在无需理由标注的情况下，通过校准感知正则化可以同时优化大语言模型的预测准确性与解释忠实度，为可解释的高效大模型微调提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce CAREF, a parameter-efficient fine-tuning framework that jointly optimizes predictive accuracy and explanation faithfulness via calibration-aware regularization. At its core, CAREF couples entropy-based calibration with token-level sparsity control through a single unified loss, the Calibration-Aware Regularization for Explanation Faithfulness (LSCED), without requiring rationale supervision. Evaluated on four NLE benchmarks (COS-E, ECQA, ComVE, e-SNLI) with Flan-T5, our lightweight CAREF-AQ variant attains the best average accuracy (89.04) and explanation alignment (81.00 nBERT) using only 6.43% of trainable parameters, outperforming LoRA and AdaLoRA. To our knowledge, CAREF is the first method to unify entropy and sparsity regularization in a single training objective for interpretable LLM fine-tuning.

### [245] [SPAR: Support-Preserving Action Rectification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27877)
*Jiaxin Zhao,Weihang Pan,Xun Liang,Binbin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SPAR是一种新型离线强化学习框架，通过在行为克隆的残差空间内进行局部修正和潜在自我模仿，消除了分布拟合与价值优化间的梯度冲突，实现了高性能的策略改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线强化学习在价值最大化与拟合数据分布之间存在内在冲突：传统的加权回归方法过于保守，导致性能受限；而基于梯度的方法又容易导致梯度冲突，使得策略偏离数据流形，导致训练不稳定。

Method: 提出“支持保持动作校正”（SPAR）框架：1. 将策略学习重新定义为锚定于冻结行为克隆策略的局部残差修正，从而压缩搜索空间；2. 引入“潜在自我模仿”（Latent Self-Imitation），采用潜在采样加权回归机制，有效解决了残差空间内的梯度冲突问题，避免了策略偏离数据流形。

Result: 理论上证明了潜在自我模仿机制能够消除标准价值梯度产生的流形法向漂移；在D4RL基准测试中的广泛实验表明，SPAR能够从次优基线中提取显著增益，达到当前最优（SOTA）性能。

Conclusion: SPAR通过将全局策略学习转化为基于残差的局部修正，成功解决了离线强化学习中价值最大化与分布拟合之间的矛盾。该方法不仅在理论上消除了梯度漂移问题，还在实证中展现了超越现有最优方法的性能，证明了通过锚定行为克隆策略来约束搜索空间的有效性。

Abstract: Offline policy improvement faces an inherent conflict between maximizing value and fitting the data distribution. While in-sample weighted regression is stable, it suffers from over-conservatism that suppresses high-value actions in the distribution tail; conversely, gradient-based approaches often exhibit a fitting-optimization conflict of gradients, which drives the policy off the data manifold. To address this, we propose Support-Preserving Action Rectification (SPAR), which reframes global learning as a local residual rectification anchored to a frozen pure behavior cloning policy. This framework performs fine-grained fitting and local policy improvement in the residual space, thereby contracting the search space. We further introduce Latent Self-Imitation, utilizing a latent-sampling weighted-regression mechanism to address fitting-improvement gradient conflict in the residual space. Theoretically, we prove this mechanism eliminates the manifold-normal drift of standard value gradients, while extensive D4RL experiments show SPAR extracts significant gains from suboptimal baselines to achieve state-of-the-art performance.

</details>

*Jun Bai,Ziyang Song,Yue Li*

Method: 提出 FedEHR-Gen 框架：

   - 第一阶段：采用联邦自编码器，通过“层级匹配聚合”机制，将高维稀疏的 EHR 特征投影到统一的全局潜空间，确保跨院语义一致性。

Abstract: Synthetic Electronic Health Record (EHR) generation provides a promising avenue for data augmentation and cross-hospital modeling in privacy-constrained healthcare settings. However, most existing EHR generative models are centralized and require pooling data across hospitals, which is often infeasible when real-world data sharing is restricted. While federated EHR generation offers a natural solution, direct federated modeling often collapses or diverges due to the high dimensionality, sparsity, and cross-hospital heterogeneity of EHR data. In this work, we propose FedEHR-Gen, the first federated framework for synthetic time-series EHR generation across distributed hospitals. FedEHR-Gen uses a two-stage learning paradigm. First, we introduce a federated autoencoder that projects high-dimensional and sparse EHR features onto a compact latent space. To ensure semantic consistency across hospitals, we develop a layer-wise matching aggregation mechanism that aligns local encoders into a unified global latent space. Second, operating on this aligned latent space, we train a federated temporal conditional variational autoencoder (TCVAE) with distribution-aware aggregation, enabling stable temporal generative modeling under severe cross-hospital heterogeneity. Extensive experiments on the eICU and MIMIC-III datasets demonstrate that FedEHR-Gen achieves generation fidelity, downstream utility, and privacy risk comparable to centralized training, while consistently outperforming the standard federated baseline.

### [247] [Cyclical Entropy Eruption: Entropy Dynamics in Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27954)
*Wendi Li,Shawn Im,Sharon Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文识别了智能体强化学习中导致训练不稳定的“循环熵爆发”现象，并提出SEAL损失函数，通过在表征层面分离轨迹，有效抑制了模型训练中的退化模式，显著提高了智能体的训练稳定性和任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管智能体大模型在复杂任务中表现优异，但其强化学习训练过程中的动态机制尚不明确，容易出现训练不稳定及生成内容退化（如重复、幻觉）的问题，缺乏有效的诊断与改进手段。

Method: 研究人员首先对智能体RL中的“循环熵爆发”进行了理论建模与实证分析，将其分为三个阶段；随后，基于这一发现，提出了SEAL（Separation-Enhanced Agent Learning）方法，这是一种通过在表征空间中区分正确与错误轨迹的辅助损失函数，旨在从根源上缓解熵爆发并防止退化模式的积累。

Result: 实验表明，智能体RL的训练过程中存在明显的“循环熵爆发”现象，这与模型退化模式（如幻觉和句子重复）的积累密切相关。应用SEAL方法后，多个基准测试显示训练过程变得更加稳定，模型在下游任务中的性能得到了显著提升。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了智能体强化学习（Agent RL）中独特的“循环熵爆发”现象，并提出了一种名为SEAL的轻量级辅助损失函数。通过在表征空间分离正确与错误的轨迹，SEAL能够有效抑制这种训练不稳定性，从而提升智能体的学习效果和性能表现。

Abstract: Agentic large language models are increasingly used to solve real-world tasks by reasoning over goals, invoking tools, and interacting with external environments. Reinforcement learning provides a natural framework for improving these behaviors, and recent agent RL methods have achieved strong results across domains. However, the training dynamics of agent RL remain poorly understood, limiting our ability to diagnose instabilities and design more effective training algorithms. In this work, we identify a previously underexplored phenomenon in agent RL, which we term cyclical entropy eruption. Unlike single-turn reasoning RL, where entropy typically collapses and stays low, agent RL training exhibits unique recurring cycles of sharp entropy eruption and gradual subsidence. We decompose this dynamic into three phases and provide theoretical and empirical analyses of each, explaining the mechanisms underlying its cyclical oscillation. We further show that degenerate patterns such as sentence duplication and hallucination, once acquired during eruption, can persist and accumulate across cycles. Motivated by these findings, we propose SEAL (Separation-Enhanced Agent Learning), a lightweight auxiliary loss that separates correct and incorrect trajectories in representation space, directly targeting the root cause of entropy eruption. Experiments across multiple benchmarks, models, and RL algorithms demonstrate that SEAL stabilizes training and yields stronger downstream agent performance.

### [248] [Law of Neural Interaction: Depth-Width Shape, Interaction Efficiency, and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27989)
*Wenjie Sun,Jinning Yang,Shuai Zhang,Mengnan Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“神经交互定律”，通过在梯度空间分析叠加现象，揭示了深度-宽度比对大模型资源利用效率及泛化能力的决定性作用，为优化模型架构设计提供了新准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型遵循缩放定律（Scaling Laws）导致资源需求激增，但模型在固定预算下的资源利用效率尚未得到充分优化。研究旨在探究模型内部“神经交互”机制，从而提升模型在资源受限环境下的泛化表现。

Method: 1. 基于神经特征 Ansatz（Neural Feature Ansatz），将叠加理论从参数空间扩展至梯度空间，定义“神经交互”（Neural Interaction）。2. 分析不同深度-宽度比对模型交互效率及泛化性能的影响。3. 在MMLU-Pro基准测试上对不同架构的模型进行对比验证。

Result: 1. 良好的泛化能力与高效的神经交互正相关。2. 通过调整深度-宽度比可将模型置于高效交互区间，且该区间随预算扩展保持相对稳定。3. 运行在高效交互区间的模型在MMLU-Pro测试中表现出更优的性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，深度-宽度比（R_{D/W}）是决定大语言模型资源利用效率和泛化能力的关键因素。通过调整模型形状使其处于“高效交互区间”，可以在固定预算下显著提升模型性能。这一发现为大模型架构设计和初始化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The guidance of scaling laws has increased the resource demands of modern large language models (LLMs), yet it remains questionable whether these models utilize resources effectively under a fixed budget. Previous research has proved superposition as a key contributor to loss. By leveraging the Neural Feature Ansatz, we extend superposition from parameter space to gradient space and define it as neural interaction. We find that under a fixed budget, good generalization is usually accompanied by efficient neural interactions, and the model can be placed in an efficient interaction interval by adjusting its depth-width ratio ($R_{D/W}$). In addition, as the budget scales up, the efficient interaction interval of the model remains relatively stable. By comparing existing small scale dense LLMs, we observe that models operating near this interval tend to perform better on the MMLU-Pro benchmark. Our findings reveal that the $R_{D/W}$ influences resource utilization efficiency and thereby affects generalization, providing insights into model shape initialization and the understanding of model generalization mechanisms. TL;DR: 本文针对扩散模型后验采样中人工权重调节的问题，提出了一种基于阻尼高斯-牛顿校正的自动化、高性能采样框架，显著提升了求解复杂逆问题的稳定性和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散后验采样方法（DPS）高度依赖人工调节的引导权重（guidance weights），且在处理复杂的、具有强算子依赖曲率的逆问题时，会导致采样过程不稳定且效率低下。

Method: 提出了一种基于扩散状态坐标的逐噪声水平阻尼高斯-牛顿校正方法。该方法：1. 通过反向传播经过降噪器来计算似然梯度；2. 使用单侧曲率模型以避免昂贵的降噪器雅可比矩阵计算；3. 应用与降噪器残差对齐的、扩散校准的秩一阻尼；4. 使用无矩阵GMRES和自动微分进行求解；5. 采用带有闭式漂移/噪声分离的方差保持朗之万转换。

Result: 在FFHQ和ImageNet数据集的各类反问题中，该方法实现了极具竞争力的图像质量指标（PSNR/SSIM/LPIPS），且运行速度显著快于多数对比基线；在加速磁共振成像（MRI）重建任务中，表现出最优的PSNR和SSIM指标。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入一种基于阻尼高斯-牛顿法的校正方案，成功解决了扩散模型后验采样中手动调节权重导致的各种不稳定性，为求解各类反问题提供了一种高效、稳定且自动化的新途径。

Abstract: Diffusion posterior sampling conditions diffusion priors on measurements, but data-consistency updates are typically scaled by hand-tuned guidance weights and can destabilize sampling under stiff, operator-dependent curvature. We replace scalar guidance with a per-noise-level damped Gauss--Newton correction computed in diffusion-state coordinates. The correction pulls likelihood gradients back through the denoiser, uses a one-sided curvature model that avoids forward denoiser Jacobians, and applies diffusion-calibrated rank-one damping aligned with the denoiser residual. Each correction is solved with matrix-free GMRES using automatic differentiation, and sampling proceeds with a variance-preserving Langevin transition with a closed-form drift/noise split. On FFHQ and ImageNet across inverse problems, it achieves competitive PSNR/SSIM/LPIPS while running markedly faster than most of the compared baselines; on accelerated MRI reconstruction, it achieves the best PSNR/SSIM among the compared baselines.

</details>


### [250] [AOE: Exhaustive Out-of-Distribution Detection via Recalibrating Outlier Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28021)
*Fengqiang Wan,Qing-Yuan Jiang,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有OOD检测中离群点标签“过平滑”的问题，本文提出了AOE方法，通过引入自适应软目标来保留类别关联，从而更有效地扩大了ID与OOD样本间的决策边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离群点暴露（OE）方法在训练时强制要求离群点具有均匀分布的预测，导致忽略了离群点与内部分布类别之间的内在语义关联（即“过平滑”效应），从而限制了OOD检测的边界优化效果。

Method: 提出了一种名为“自适应置信度离群点暴露（AOE）”的方法。该方法通过引入温度缩放（Temperature Scaling）机制，将离群点标签从固定的均匀分布调整为自适应软目标。通过学习到的温度参数对预测分布进行平滑处理，既抑制了模型对离群点的过置信预测，又保留了离群点与内部分布（ID）类别之间的语义关系。

Result: 在多个基准测试集上的实验表明，AOE方法能够显著提升OOD检测性能，有效地在抑制过置信预测与保持语义边界之间取得了平衡，优于现有的多种代表性OE方法。

Conclusion: AOE通过引入自适应软目标，成功解决了传统离群点暴露（OE）方法中因标签均匀化导致的“过平滑”问题，在保留类别关系的同时有效提升了OOD检测的判别能力与泛化性能。

Abstract: Out-of-distribution (OOD) detection is essential for deploying machine learning models in open-world and safety-critical scenarios, where test inputs may deviate from the training distribution and overconfident predictions on unknown samples can lead to unreliable decisions. Outlier Exposure (OE) has emerged as a promising OOD detection paradigm by introducing auxiliary outliers during training to enlarge the margin between in-distribution (ID) and OOD samples. Existing OE-based methods typically enlarge this margin by employing uniform labels to maximize the entropy of OOD samples over ID categories. However, we theoretically show that uniform labels inevitably disregard the relations between OOD samples and ID categories, termed the over-softening effect, leading to a suboptimal margin bound. Our theoretical analysis further reveals that explicitly exploiting such relations can instead yield improved OOD detection performance. Motivated by this insight, we propose \underline{A}daptive Confidence \underline{OE} (AOE), a simple yet effective method that leverages temperature scaling to recalibrate outlier labels. Specifically, AOE generates adaptive soft targets from temperature-scaled model predictions for OOD samples, where the learnable temperature smooths the prediction distribution without fully erasing class-wise relational information. By supervising OOD samples with these adaptive soft targets, AOE preserves the semantic proximity between OOD samples and ID categories while encouraging the softened targets to approach a high-entropy distribution, thereby suppressing overconfident OOD predictions and enlarging the separation margin. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of AOE.

</details>


### [251] [RW-TTT: Batched Serving for Request-Owned Test-Time Training State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28053)
*Jian Yang,Zhizhuo Kou,Yao Tian,Hao Zhang,Han Chen,Sirui Han,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 RW-TTT 架构，解决了 LLM 测试时训练（TTT）在批处理推理中因动态状态更新导致的竞争问题，通过标签化的读写管理机制，在保障模型准确性的前提下，大幅提升了并发处理能力与推理吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时训练（TTT）通过动态更新模型权重来提升 LLM 表现，但这种更新机制破坏了传统 LLM 推理所依赖的“共享静态权重”假设。传统的批处理方式会导致请求间状态相互干扰，而序列化执行又过于缓慢。因此，需要一种新的服务架构来解决 TTT 带来的状态读写冲突问题。

Method: 提出了 RW-TTT（Read-Write TTT Serving）架构。该方法通过为每个解码步骤添加所有者（Owner）、版本（Version）以及读/写（READ/WRITE）操作标签，实现对请求状态的精确控制，仅对兼容的请求阶段进行批处理，并确保更新仅提交给相应的请求所有者。

Result: 在单 GPU 上，RW-TTT 在八个“InPlace-TTT”快速权重流中达到了 274.61 tok/s 的聚合吞吐量，相比序列化推理提升了 9.31 倍，相比同内存预算下的单流副本方式提升了 3.44 倍，同时在 RULER 长上下文基准测试中保持了原始性能。

Conclusion: RW-TTT 成功解决了测试时训练（TTT）在批处理推理中面临的状态竞争问题，通过精细化的标签机制实现了高效的并发推理，在保持模型性能的同时显著提升了吞吐量。

Abstract: Test-time training (TTT) adapts an LLM during generation by reading and updating request-owned state, such as fast weights, low-rank deltas, or streaming learner state. This breaks batched LLM serving, which assumes shared static weights: serial execution is correct but slow, while naive batching can corrupt request state. We formulate this problem as read-write TTT serving and present RW-TTT , which tags each decode step with its owner, version, and READ/WRITE effect, batches only compatible phases, and commits updates only to the owner. On one GPU with eight fast-weight InPlace-TTT streams, RW-TTT reaches 274.61 aggregate tok/s, 9.31x over sequential serving and 3.44x over per-stream replicas under the same memory budget. It preserves behavior on RULER, a long-context benchmark, and passes owner/version checks.

</details>

TL;DR: PINE是一种新型的树集成剪枝方法，通过共形校准在特定的“分布内”区域内确保预测不变，从而在不牺牲关键预测性能的前提下，有效提高了模型的压缩比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的树集成剪枝方法存在矛盾：传统方法在优化精度与压缩比时可能破坏预测一致性，而要求全空间预测等价的“忠实剪枝”方法则导致压缩比过低。研究旨在寻找一种既能保证实际应用场景下预测一致性，又能实现更高压缩率的折中方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为PINE的剪枝方法。该方法引入了一个由参数α控制的“分布内区域（in-distribution region）”，通过共形校准技术在该区域内保证模型的预测等价性，从而在维持预测可靠性的同时，比传统的完全忠实剪枝方法获得更高的压缩比。

Result: 在12个公共表格数据集上的实验结果表明，与现有的忠实剪枝方法相比，PINE在保持相当的预测一致性水平的同时，将模型压缩率提升了最高30%。

Conclusion: PINE提供了一种在预测一致性与模型压缩率之间取得更好平衡的剪枝策略，通过共形校准在保证特定分布区域内预测等价性的前提下，显著提升了树集成模型的压缩效率。

Abstract: Tree ensembles are machine learning models with strong predictive performance and interpretability, and remain widely used for tabular data. Standard pruning methods for tree ensembles typically optimize an accuracy-compression trade-off and may change a subset of predictions, potentially compromising decision consistency. Faithful pruning methods address this issue by preserving prediction equivalence over the entire input space, but this requirement leads to lower compression ratios. We propose PINE, a pruning method that provides strong guarantees within an in-distribution region. PINE preserves prediction equivalence within this region and controls the region size using a single parameter $α$ via conformal calibration. Experiments on 12 public tabular datasets show that PINE improves the compression ratio by up to $30\%$ while preserving predictions at a comparable level to existing faithful pruning methods.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Many learning problems require predicting how populations evolve under an unknown transformation. A natural representation for such populations is a probability measure, with point clouds as a key example. In this work, we study the measure-to-measure (M2M) regression problem, in which one seeks to learn a map between probability measures from a finite collection of observed input-output pairs. In contrast to classical regression, where individual samples are transformed independently, M2M regression treats entire distributions as the data points. This perspective is vital in certain scientific applications, for example, cellular and molecular biology, where cells are known to evolve not as independent data points but as a collection. However, few existing approaches address the problem of M2M regression with sufficient expressivity and scalability. We present a formalization of nonlinear M2M regression and introduce two easy-to-use, expressive, and scalable approaches to learn such operators: transformers as static M2M maps and transformers as dynamic M2M velocity fields. Our approach leverages the natural measure-dependent and mean-field structure of transformers to learn nonlinear M2M maps on the space of probability distributions. We illustrate the effectiveness of our proposed method to generalize to unseen measures on synthetic experiments, interacting particle systems, and a large-scale patient-derived organoid dataset for predicting treatment response in colorectal cancer.

### [254] [Long Live The Balance: Information Bottleneck Driven Tree-based Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28109)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出 IB-Score 指标：基于信息瓶颈理论，量化推理步骤的多样性与正确答案之间互信息的权衡。
2. 提出 IB-TPO 框架：将 IB-Score 作为优化目标，并结合创新的 IB 引导树状采样策略，在相同 token 预算下提升采样效率（增加 50% 轨迹），并复用树结构进行蒙特卡洛估计。

Result: 在标准基准测试中，IB-TPO 显著优于 GRPO 基准（提升 2.9% 至 3.6%），并在采样效率和性能表现上超越了现有的主流在线强化学习方法。

Abstract: Recent advances in online reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated promising performance in complex reasoning tasks. However, they often exhibit an imbalanced exploration-exploitation trade-off, resulting in unstable optimization and sub-optimal performance. We introduce IB-Score, a novel metric grounded in Information Bottleneck theory that evaluates policy's exploration-exploitation balance by quantifying the trade-off between step-level reasoning diversity and mutual information shared with the correct answer. Analysis based on IB-Score shows that popular online RL approaches (e.g., GRPO) with common regularizers fail to consistently maintain balance during training with suboptimal results. To address this, we propose Information Bottleneck-driven Tree-based Policy Optimization (IB-TPO), a principled framework that formulates IB-Score as a fine-grained optimization objective and utilizes a novel IB-guided tree sampling strategy that not only improves the efficiency of online sampling with 50% more trajectories under the same token budget, but also reuses the tree structure for effective IB-Score Monte Carlo estimation. Extensive experiments across standard benchmarks show that our method significantly outperforms GRPO baseline by 2.9% to 3.6% and also outperforms other state-of-the-art online RL approaches. Our code is available at https://github.com/alibaba/EfficientRL.

We introduce Chreode, a one-step cell world model that predicts action-conditioned cell-state transitions through a structured residual transition operator. ### [256] [Adaptive Coarse-to-Fine Subgoal Refinement for Long-Horizon Offline Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28127)
*Kaiqiang Ke,Shenghong He,Chengdong Xu,Yuheng Luo,Xiangyuan Lan,Chao Yu*

Method: 提出了一种名为“粗到细层级目标强化学习（CFHRL）”的离线强化学习框架。该方法从最终目标出发，利用基于回放数据训练的候选器递归生成中间子目标，并结合学习到的可达性代价函数，在子目标被评估为“局部可执行”时自动停止细化过程。这种方法允许模型自适应地根据状态-目标对的距离调整层级深度。

Result: 在OGBench基准测试中的实验结果显示，CFHRL在多个长程任务上均取得了显著的性能提升，且消融实验验证了所提的递归细化机制和停止策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的CFHRL框架通过递归细化目标的策略，有效解决了长程离线目标条件强化学习中引导误差累积的问题，证明了分层递归细化方法在处理长程任务时的有效性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) is challenging in long-horizon tasks, where distant state--goal pairs provide weak supervision and value estimates become vulnerable to accumulated bootstrapping errors. Hierarchical methods mitigate this difficulty by introducing intermediate subgoals, but fixed temporal abstractions or fixed hierarchy depths can be mismatched to state--goal pairs with different reachability horizons. We propose Coarse-to-Fine Hierarchical Goal Reinforcement Learning (CFHRL), a fully offline GCRL framework that adaptively refines distant goals before execution. Starting from the final goal, CFHRL recursively proposes intermediate targets, trained from replay-supported candidates, and stops refinement once the current target is estimated to be locally executable by a learned reachability cost. The key idea is that a subgoal need not be an exact midpoint or globally optimal waypoint; it only needs to provide reliable progress and reduce the remaining reaching difficulty, enabling subsequent refinement over shorter horizons. A stylized analysis further supports the robustness of approximate recursive contraction. Experiments on OGBench show substantial gains on several long-horizon tasks, with ablations validating the proposed refinement and stopping mechanisms

TL;DR: 本文研究了价值随时间动态变化的重复拍卖竞价问题，提出了一种结合微分方程与置信界技术的学习算法，实现了在不同价值模型下的近最优后悔界，有效解决了竞价者在动态环境下的策略优化与参数学习难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有竞价模型多假设投标者价值是静态的，而现实中投标者价值往往具有动态特性（即当前价值依赖于过去的竞价结果）。本研究旨在解决在价值随时间动态演化且仅能获得聚合反馈的重复第二价格拍卖中，竞价者如何平衡当前竞价收益与未来价值影响，并同时学习未知环境参数的问题。

Method: 提出了一类结合插件估计器（plug-in estimators）与最优策略微分方程表征的学习方法。特别是，采用了一种特定的置信界算法，能够在连续时间到达的拍卖中，根据有限的反馈信息进行策略学习与参数估计。

Result: 在分段线性价值函数下，算法实现了 $\widetilde{O}(\log N)$ 的近最优后悔值；在一般的平滑价值函数下，实现了 $\widetilde{O}(N^{1/3})$ 的后悔值，且上述结果均在无需显式随机化的情况下获得。

Conclusion: 研究通过理论分析和数值实验证明，所提出的基于置信界（confidence bound）的学习算法在处理具有动态价值的重复竞价问题时是有效的，且无需显式随机化即可达到近最优的后悔值，为动态环境下的投标策略提供了强有力的理论支撑。

Abstract: We study the problem of learning to bid when the bidder's value is dynamic, i.e., when the current value depends on past outcomes. Specifically, we consider a bidder participating in repeated second-price auctions whose value depends on the time elapsed since their last successful bid, with auctions arriving in continuous time and only aggregated feedback revealed at the end of the horizon. Such a bidder must (1) balance the immediate benefit of winning the current auction against its impact on future values and (2) learn unknown environmental parameters. We derive regret bounds for a class of learning methods that combine plug-in estimators with a differential-equation characterization of the optimal policy, and show that a specific confidence bound algorithm learns the optimal policy with a near optimal regret of $\widetilde{O}(\log N)$ for piecewise linear primitives, and $\widetilde{O}(N^{1/3})$ for general, smooth primitives, achieving these regrets without explicit randomization. These theoretical results are supported by numerical experiments.

</details>


### [258] [Self-Consistency via Marginal Sharpening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28142)
*Aleksei Arzhantsev,Otmane Sakhi,Nicolas Chopin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出通过优化“答案边缘分布”而非“完整输出序列”来提升模型推理能力，并引入了一种高效的并行采样算法，在数学和编程任务中实现了性能与速度的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理时采样方法通常对模型的完整输出进行分布锐化，倾向于选择单个概率最高的路径。然而，推理能力的核心不在于单个路径的概率，而在于答案是否能被多条合理的推理路径所支撑。因此，需要改变采样目标，将关注点从完整输出序列转移到答案的边缘分布上。

Method: 研究者提出了一种将自洽性（Self-consistency）内化为推理时目标的方法。不同于传统对完整输出序列进行分布锐化的做法，该方法转向对“答案边缘分布”（Answer Marginal）进行锐化。为此，作者设计了一种纯自回归的并行采样算法，能够高效近似从该锐化边缘分布中采样。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在数学和编程基准测试中表现优于标准的强力采样方法。此外，由于采用了高效的并行采样算法，该方法在推理速度上比现有方法快几个数量级。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的从全输出分布转向锐化答案边缘分布的方法，有效提升了语言模型在数学和编程任务中的推理能力。该方法通过简单的自回归并行采样算法，在大幅提高推理效率的同时，超越了现有的强力采样（Power-sampling）效果，验证了直接优化“答案支持度”比优化“单个完整推理路径”更为有效。

Abstract: Inference-time sampling can elicit strong reasoning abilities from language models without additional training. Existing power-sampling methods do so by sharpening the distribution over full generated outputs, favoring completions that are individually likely under the model. We argue that this is the wrong object to target for reasoning: a completion entangles a reasoning trace with a final answer, whereas what matters is whether an answer is supported by many plausible reasoning paths. We therefore shift the target from the full-output distribution to the sharpened answer marginal, making self-consistency an inference-time objective rather than a post-hoc voting criterion. Surprisingly, this marginal target admits an efficient approximation: we propose a simple, purely autoregressive parallel sampling algorithm that approximately samples from the sharpened answer marginal, eliciting stronger performance than standard power sampling on mathematics and coding benchmarks while being orders of magnitude faster.

</details>

### [260] [Sign-Aware Gated Sparse Autoencoders: Modeling Anticorrelated Features with Bi-Jump-ReLU Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28149)
*Bartosz Wieciech,Zmnako Awrahman,Marcin Czelej,Victor Hugo Jaramillo Velasquez,Wioletta Stobieniecka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SA-GSAE通过引入符号感知门控和双极性特征共享机制，解决了传统稀疏自编码器在处理互斥概念时的冗余问题，实现了更高的参数利用率和极低的死特征率，显著提升了大模型可解释性分析的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏自编码器（SAE）通常强制特征非负，这使得模型必须为互为相反的概念（如“压力过高”与“压力过低”）分配不同的潜空间向量，导致了模型字典容量的浪费，特别是在处理抗相关特征时效率低下。

Method: 提出了“符号感知门控稀疏自编码器”（SA-GSAE），核心创新包括：1. 双侧门控稀疏性，允许特征同时表示正负两极；2. 符号大小路径，避免了L1正则化带来的收缩偏差；3. 辅助重构损失，防止门控崩溃；4. 引入Bi-Jump-ReLU激活函数，实现特征的双极性共享；5. 采用对称参数绑定策略（将正负向参数绑定），在保证性能的同时提升参数效率。

Result: 实验表明，半宽度的SA-GSAE在重构性能上完全优于或等同于双倍宽度的传统Gated SAE。在Pythia-1B和SmolLM3-3B模型上的测试显示，SA-GSAE显著减少了死特征比例（最高可降低500倍），且在MLP输出层及残差流中展现了更强的特征表达能力和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SA-GSAE 通过引入双极性特征表达，有效解决了传统稀疏自编码器（SAE）因强制非负约束导致的资源浪费问题。该模型不仅在参数效率上实现了跨越式提升，显著降低了“死特征”比例，还为理解大模型内部的抗相关概念提供了一种更优的解释性框架，证明了符号感知在特征表示学习中的重要性。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) extract interpretable features from Large Language Models, but standard variants enforce non-negativity, forcing separate latents for diametrically opposed concepts (e.g., "pressure too high" vs. "pressure too low") and wasting dictionary capacity when features are anticorrelated. We propose the Sign-Aware Gated SAE (SA-GSAE): two-sided gated sparsity with signed magnitude and auxiliary supervision. A polarity-sensitive gate selects support on either sign, a signed-magnitude path avoids L1 shrinkage, and an auxiliary reconstruction prevents gate collapse. Bipolar sharing - one latent encoding both signs along a shared direction - is realised via a new Bi-Jump-ReLU activation; parameter accounting shows sign-awareness stays parameter-efficient even when anticorrelated pairs are rare.
  On real LLM activations across three mid-depth hookpoints on Pythia-1B and SmolLM3-3B (6 cells, 3 seeds), a half-width SA-GSAE at width H strictly Pareto-dominates a full-width Gated SAE at 2H over the entire swept L0 overlap on 3 of 6 cells (both MLP-output hookpoints and resid-mid/Pythia-1B); on the remaining 3 it matches R^2 within 0.025 (max gap -0.008) while cutting dead fraction by 0.35-0.62 absolute. Sweep-geomean dead-fraction reductions are ~100x-500x on MLP-output cells and Pythia-1B resid, ~2x-4x on attention cells and SmolLM3-3B resid. Ablations show the two-sided gate and auxiliary loss are load-bearing (no auxiliary collapses LR to 0.27, 98% dead); tying r_i^+ = r_i^- is indistinguishable (|Delta R^2| = 0.0015), and we recommend this symmetric variant as default. MLP-output gains come from most latents carrying both polarities; on attention, bipolar structure concentrates in a small set of top latents. Full-width SA-GSAE exhibits a reproducible reconstruction collapse at SmolLM3-3B resid that the half-width entirely avoids.

### [261] [Off-Policy Learning to Reason Works Because It Is More Pessimistic Than You Think](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28150)
*Otmane Sakhi,Aleksei Arzhantsev,Imad Aouali,Flavian Vasile*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大规模语言模型强化学习中因离线数据导致的PPO不稳定性，本文提出了一种基于“隐式悲观主义”的离线学习框架，通过无需重要性采样的方法实现稳定优化，并提出了一种改良策略来进一步提升学习效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模语言模型推理强化学习中，由于生成过程存在滞后或异步，训练天然属于离线（off-policy）场景。现有的基于PPO的信任域方法在处理离线数据时，依赖重要性采样修正分布偏移，容易导致方差过大、训练不稳定及熵崩塌。因此，研究者寻求无需重要性权重的离线学习新范式。

Method: 提出了一个涵盖现有成功离线策略目标的通用直观构建框架，并证明其有效性源于“隐式悲观主义”（即算法倾向于向比目标策略更保守的策略优化）。在此基础上，提出了一种能够稳定诱导分布并提升学习性能的原则性修正方法。

Result: 研究表明，抛弃重要性权重后的离线目标函数具有“隐式悲观”特性，从而保证了训练的稳定性。提出的改进方法能够有效控制有效目标分布，在离线学习中表现出比传统方法更强的性能与稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文通过“隐式悲观主义”视角统一解释了离线策略优化目标的有效性，并提出了一种通过显式控制目标分布来稳定学习过程的原则性方法，为大规模强化学习提供了更稳健的理论与实践基础。

Abstract: Large scale reinforcement learning has become a central tool for improving reasoning in large language models. At this scale, generation is often lagged or asynchronous, so updates are performed on data collected by older policies. This makes learning inherently off-policy. Most existing approaches nevertheless remain rooted in PPO-style trust-region objectives, treating training as approximately on-policy and using importance weights to correct distribution mismatch. These corrections can introduce high variance, destabilize optimization, and accelerate entropy collapse. Recent work suggests an alternative: rather than correcting the mismatch, one can embrace off-policy data and remove importance weights, often yielding stronger algorithms. In this paper, we provide an intuitive construction of off-policy objectives that include successful off-policy objectives and show that their effectiveness can be understood through implicit pessimism: they optimize toward target policies that are more conservative than their nominal objectives suggest. This perspective explains why some particular implementation choices improve stability: they implicitly control the effective target distribution. We then propose a principled modification that stabilize this induced distribution and improve off-policy learning.

### [262] [Unification and Optimization of Robust Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28165)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者将现有的鲁棒学习方法归纳为三个设计轴，并将鲁棒训练过程分解为四个连续阶段（参考分布增强、输入空间扰动、标签空间扰动、样本级聚合），每个阶段允许选择不同的策略取向（悲观、中立或乐观）。通过这种方式构建了一个统一的设计空间，并利用联合超参数优化来自动搜索最佳的鲁棒性配置。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个统一的鲁棒学习框架，能够根据具体任务需求自动组合不同的鲁棒化策略。实验表明，该方法作为一种通用选择，在多种任务中表现优异，避免了用户预先盲目选择单一鲁棒方法的困境。

Abstract: The literature has proposed various robust alternatives to empirical risk minimisation to address failure modes such as distribution shift, label noise and finite-sample degeneracies. Examples include distributionally robust optimization, label smoothing, vicinal risk minimization, and Mixup. However, such approaches are typically developed in isolation, forcing practitioners to commit a priori to a single failure mode even when the dominant mode for the task is unclear. To address this, we organize a broad class of existing methods along three common design axes and derive a tractable training procedure that decomposes robust learning into sequential stages (reference distribution enrichment, input-space perturbation, label-space perturbation, and sample-level aggregation), each with a choice of stance (pessimistic, neutral, or optimistic). This results in a unified design space in which joint hyperparameter optimization can compose and configure robustness strategies suited to the task at hand. Across tabular, image, and reward modeling benchmarks, joint hyperparameter optimization is competitive with the best single-method baseline in each setting, offering a reliable default for practitioners who do not know a priori which failure mode dominates their task.

### [263] [QuITE: Query-Based Irregular Time Series Embedding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28166)
*JungHoon Lim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 QuITE，一种针对非规则多元时间序列（IMTS）的嵌入模块。它通过可学习的查询标记直接处理非规则观测，无需插值或模型重构，即可直接增强现有主流时间序列模型的表现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 QuITE（基于查询的不规则时间序列嵌入）的方法。该方法摒弃了传统的固定网格插值策略，利用可学习的查询标记（query tokens）通过单层自注意力机制对不规则观测数据进行聚合，将不规则输入转化为与主流模型（Backbone）兼容的潜在特征表示。

Result: 在多个真实世界基准测试中，QuITE 能够持续提升现有 MTS 模型的性能，在预测任务中实现了最高 54.7% 的平均相对性能提升，在分类任务中提升了 15.8%。实验证明了该模块在不同数据集和基础架构下的有效性和广泛适用性。

Abstract: Irregular Multivariate Time Series (IMTS) are common in practice, yet their irregular sampling complicates effective modeling. Existing approaches typically either (i) design specialized architectures that limit the reuse of proven Multivariate Time Series (MTS) models, or (ii) map IMTS onto regular temporal grids through interpolation, which may distort temporal dynamics by introducing artificial values. To address these limitations, we propose a new input-embedding-based approach. We identify that the key bottleneck lies not in the backbone architecture, but in conventional embedding layers that assume uniform sampling. In this work, we introduce QuITE (Query-Based Irregular Time Series Embedding), a simple yet effective plug-and-play embedding module for IMTS. QuITE employs learnable query tokens to aggregate irregular observations through a single self-attention layer, directly producing backbone-compatible latent representations without artificial value generation or architectural modification. Extensive experiments on real-world benchmarks show that QuITE consistently improves MTS models, yielding average relative gains of up to $54.7\%$ in forecasting and $15.8\%$ in classification across diverse datasets and backbone architectures. Code is available at: https://github.com/Meaningfull9502/QuITE.

Experimental results show that our H-TDBU approach improves train-synthetic-test-real performance over neural baseline methods while preserving semantic consistency. Our results suggest that hierarchical rule-guided synthesis provides an effective mechanism for combining controllability, semantic coherence, and statistical fidelity in synthetic data generation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单细胞RNA测序（scRNA-seq）缺乏空间背景，而空间转录组（ST）分辨率较低且受限于固定的采样网格。当前的集成方法通常依赖于去卷积或将细胞映射到预定义的网格上，这在处理未配对数据时存在较大局限性，难以还原真实的组织空间几何结构。因此，作者旨在提出一种不依赖于预定义坐标系或细胞类型标注的空间重构框架。

Method: GEARS采用了一种“几何优先”的框架：1. 学习一个领域不变的表达编码器，将空间转录组（ST）点与单细胞（scRNA-seq）数据对齐；2. 利用排列等变生成器结合扩散模型，在位姿不变的监督下生成局部空间几何结构；3. 在推理阶段，通过聚合多个子集的预测距离，求解全局距离几何问题，从而获得二维坐标和稠密的距离矩阵。

Result: 实验结果表明，GEARS在全局距离保持、局部邻域保真度以及空间分布对齐方面均优于现有的空间映射和去卷积基准方法。此外，GEARS在跨切片泛化能力上也表现出显著优势。

Conclusion: GEARS通过几何优先的策略，实现了对单细胞RNA测序数据空间结构的有效重构。该方法证明了在无需细胞类型标签、组织学图像或显式细胞-点分配的情况下，通过学习领域不变编码器和排列等变生成器，能够获取更具普适性和准确性的空间坐标及距离矩阵，为研究复杂组织的空间组织形式提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Single-cell RNA sequencing (scRNA-seq) profiles large numbers of cells but loses spatial context, whereas spatial transcriptomics (ST) preserves partial spatial structure at lower resolution. Most existing integration methods either deconvolve spot mixtures or map cells onto a measured spot lattice, which ties reconstructions to a fixed grid and slide-specific coordinate systems, a limitation that is especially problematic in unpaired settings. We propose GEARS, a geometry-first framework that reconstructs an intrinsic single-cell spatial geometry guided by ST, without relying on cell-type labels, histological images, or cell-to-spot assignment. GEARS first learns a domain-invariant expression encoder that aligns ST spots and dissociated cells, and then trains a permutation-equivariant generator with a diffusion-based refiner with EDM-style preconditioning to generate local spatial geometries under pose-invariant supervision derived from ST coordinates. At inference, GEARS reconstructs geometry on many overlapping subsets of scRNA-seq cells, aggregates predicted pairwise distances across subsets, and solves a global distance-geometry problem to obtain canonical two-dimensional coordinates and a dense distance matrix. Extensive quantitative and qualitative experiments, including cross-section generalization, show that GEARS consistently improves global distance preservation, local neighborhood fidelity, and spatial distribution alignment compared to strong spatial mapping and deconvolution baselines.

### [266] [Refining Multidimensional Video Reward Models via Disentangled Influence Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28203)
*Muyao Wang,Zeke Xie,Hideki Nakayama*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本生成视频（T2V）奖励模型在处理多维度评估时，忽略了“维度异质性”——即同一个训练样本在不同评价维度下具有不同的可靠性，导致基于全局度量的过滤方法无法有效提升模型对齐效果。

Method: 提出了一个解耦影响框架（Disentangled Influence Framework）来估计特定维度的监督风险，并据此设计了两种细化策略：维度解耦剪枝（Dimension-Disentangled Pruning）和维度解耦重加权（Dimension-Disentangled Reweighting）。

Result: 实验表明，该研究所提出的解耦策略在多个指标上显著优于传统的全局过滤基线方法，使得奖励模型能更准确地对齐地面实况。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入维度解耦框架，有效解决了多维度视频奖励模型（MVRM）训练中的“维度异质性”问题，通过对不同维度的监督风险进行精细化控制，显著提升了奖励模型与人类评价的一致性。

Abstract: As Text-to-Video (T2V) generation models continue to evolve, the complexity of video evaluation necessitates a fine-grained assessment across various axes. To address this, recent works have focused on developing Multidimensional Video Reward Models (MVRMs), which decompose the evaluation process to better align with the multifaceted nature of human visual perception. However, training effective MVRMs is fundamentally challenged by the complex nature of video data. In this work, we identify a critical phenomenon termed Dimensional Heterogeneity: the reliability of a training sample can vary substantially across evaluation dimensions, meaning that a sample may provide reliable supervision for one objective while inducing high supervision risk for another. Consequently, prevailing data-centric methods that filter based on global scalar metrics are ill-posed for T2V tasks. To address this, we propose a disentangled influence framework that that efficiently estimates dimension-specific supervision risk. Leveraging this framework, we introduce two dimension-disentangled refinement strategies: Dimension-Disentangled Pruning, which removes extreme high-risk samples, and Dimension-Disentangled Reweighting, which softly down-weights high-risk supervision. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our disentangled strategies significantly outperform global filtering baselines, yielding reward models with superior alignment to ground truth.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过数学推导建立了此类受控流的表达性原则（Expressivity Principle），证明了在可控性和适定性假设下，该模型能够将源分布变换为目标分布。在合成数据集上的实验验证了该方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于Chow-Rashevskii定理的受控流生成模型，通过学习少数标量控制函数来调制固定的向量场。这种方法不仅实现了高效的生成建模，还证明了通过少量控制通道即可实现复杂的概率分布变换，为高维流模型的参数化提供了具有几何解释性的新思路。

Abstract: We introduce a continuous-time generative modeling framework, motivated by the Chow-Rashevskii theorem, that builds expressive flows from a small set of fixed vector fields and learned scalar controls. Instead of learning an unconstrained high-dimensional vector field, our framework constructs the velocity by modulating fixed vector fields with learned scalar control functions. When the fixed fields are bracket-generating, their Lie algebra spans the ambient space, providing a mechanism for expressive transport with only a small number of learned control channels and offering a parameter-efficient geometric alternative to standard vector-field parameterizations. This decoupled formulation yields a structured and interpretable generative model in which the number of learned scalar output channels can be chosen independently of the ambient dimension. We formulate an expressivity principle showing that, under suitable controllability and well-posedness assumptions, such controlled flows can transport a source distribution to a target distribution. We train the resulting model using a continuous-normalizing-flow likelihood objective and present proof-of-concept experiments on synthetic distributions.

Method: 1. 文本建模：引入超图表示，将文档建模为连接所有共现词的超边，词频作为节点权重。

Abstract: Dynamic topic modeling is widely used to analyze evolving trends in scientific literature, medical records, and social media. Traditional topic models represent each topic through a single probability vector on the multinomial simplex and implicitly couple word occurrence and repetition within one probabilistic mechanism. However, this formulation restricts the dependence structure among words and overlooks informative higher-order interactions, particularly in dynamic corpora with overlapping semantics. To address these limitations, we introduce a hypergraph representation of text where each document is modeled as a hyperedge connecting all co-occurring words, with repetition intensities encoded as node weights. This representation naturally separates word occurrence from repetition and induces a novel hypergraph-based multinomial distribution with a nonlinear normalization depending on the observed word set of each document. Building on this likelihood, we develop a dynamic topic modeling framework via structured low-rank factorizations with explicit temporal regularization on topic-word profiles. Moreover, we establish local convergence guarantees and derive non-asymptotic error bounds despite the intrinsic nonconvexity induced by bilinear factorization and document-specific nonlinear normalization. Numerical experiments on synthetic data and an application to the International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR) corpus demonstrate consistent improvements over existing multinomial-based topic models.

### [270] [Commit to the Bit: Reactive Reinforcement Learning Done Right](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28276)
*Onno Eberhard,Claire Vernade,Michael Muehlebach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对非马尔可夫环境，提出了一种在特征改变时才更新策略的“提交Q学习”算法，证明了在更弱的鲁棒性假设下可收敛至最优策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习算法大多基于马尔可夫假设，这与现实中存在部分可观测性或因函数近似导致特征非马尔可夫的情况不符。因此，作者旨在解决在非马尔可夫环境下学习最优反应式策略的问题，并寻求比现有$q_\star$-可实现性条件更弱的收敛假设。

Method: 提出“提交Q学习”（Committed Q-learning）算法，该算法要求智能体在进入某一特征状态时锁定一个动作，仅在该状态特征发生改变时才重新采样动作；同时引入准马尔可夫环境的分析框架，并在满足“重连鲁棒性”（rewire-robustness）的条件下证明了算法的几乎确定收敛性。

Result: 理论证明了Committed Q-learning算法在重连鲁棒性假设下，能够以概率1收敛到最优反应式策略，且该假设条件严格弱于先前的研究工作。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种适用于非马尔可夫环境的“提交Q学习”（Committed Q-learning）算法。通过引入准马尔可夫环境概念和“重连鲁棒性”（rewire-robustness）假设，证明了该算法在比以往文献中$q_\star$-可实现性条件更弱的情况下，能以概率1收敛到最优反应式策略，为处理部分可观测或函数近似环境下的强化学习提供了更具鲁棒性的理论框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning algorithms are commonly analyzed (and designed) under the Markov assumption. This is unrealistic, as most environments encountered in practice are either partially observable, or require function approximation that restricts the agent to access non-Markovian state features. We consider the problem of learning an optimal reactive policy in a finite environment with deterministic observations (or equivalently, hard state aggregation). We introduce a new algorithm, Committed Q-learning, and prove almost-sure convergence to the optimal reactive policy under an intuitive assumption we call rewire-robustness. This assumption is strictly weaker than the $q_\star$-realizability condition used in prior work. Our algorithm is a variant of classical Q-learning in which the behavior policy commits to a single action upon entering a feature, and only resamples actions when the observed feature changes. A crucial part of our analysis is the introduction of quasi-Markov environments.

Unlike existing approaches that generally overfit to a specific chemical formula, we establish a multi-composition training scheme that enables a broad generalization across diverse chemistry, guided by energy- and validity-based rewards. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在匹配市场中，玩家的效用与手臂的语境（context）呈线性关系。语境的微小变化可能导致稳定匹配基准的剧烈重构，从而引发其他玩家巨大的 regret，传统的赌博机模型难以直接处理这种复杂的联动效应。

Method: 本文针对随机语境提出了基于最小偏好间隙（minimum preference gap）的算法，实现实例相关（instance-dependent）的对数 regret 边界；针对对抗性语境，引入了一种可行的 regret 定义，并设计了能实现实例无关（instance-independent）亚线性 regret 边界的自适应算法。

Abstract: We study bandit learning in matching markets, where players and arms constitute the two market sides, and the players' utilities are linear in the arm contexts. In each round, new arms arrive with observable contexts. Then, the algorithm matches them to players, aiming to minimize each player's regret against a stable matching benchmark. This contextual structure creates significant complexity: subtle context shifts can slightly alter one player's utility while completely reconfiguring the underlying benchmark, causing large regret spikes for others. We address this in two settings: stochastic contexts, drawn from a latent distribution, and adversarial contexts, which may be arbitrary. For the stochastic case, we introduce a novel minimum preference gap to capture learning difficulty and provide a fully adaptive algorithm with an instance-dependent poly-logarithmic regret upper bound. We also establish matching instance-independent regret upper and lower bounds under a mild distributional assumption. For the adversarial setting, we propose a tractable regret notion that remains valid under arbitrary contexts and achieves an instance-independent sublinear regret bound via an adaptive algorithm.

### [273] [ProRL: Effective Reinforcement Learning for Proactive Recommendation via Rectified Policy Gradient Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28293)
*Hongru Hou,Tiehua Mei,Denghui Geng,Jinhui Huang,Ao Xu,Hengrui Chen,Jiaqing Liang,Deqing Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对主动推荐系统中的强化学习训练难点，提出了ProRL框架，通过消除路径长度偏置和降低梯度方差，实现了更精准、高效的用户兴趣引导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的主动推荐系统（PRS）在使用强化学习进行路径规划时，直接应用策略梯度存在严重缺陷：一是路径级奖励分解为正均值的步级奖励时，产生与路径长度相关的偏置，导致策略倾向于盲目延长路径；二是直接使用全局路径奖励对每一步加权，忽略了奖励的分解结构，导致梯度方差过大。

Method: 提出了一种名为ProRL的强化学习框架，核心机制包括：1. 逐步奖励中心化（Stepwise Reward Centering）：通过减去期望奖励来消除与路径长度相关的偏差；2. 位置特定优势估计（Position-Specific Advantage Estimation）：利用奖励分解结构计算与步长相关的基线，以降低梯度方差。

Result: 在三个真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，ProRL在引导用户偏好转移和推荐效果方面显著优于现有的先进主动推荐系统（SOTA）。

Conclusion: ProRL通过引入分步奖励中心化和位置特定优势估计，有效解决了主动推荐系统中强化学习存在的梯度偏差和高方差问题，为实现长期有效的用户兴趣引导提供了一个鲁棒的框架。

Abstract: Proactive Recommender Systems (PRSs) aim to guide user preference shift toward target items by generating paths of intermediate recommendations. Reinforcement learning (RL) provides a principled framework for optimizing such sequential decision tasks, as path rewards can naturally capture both short-term acceptance and long-term guidance effectiveness. However, naively applying policy gradients to PRS results in deficient gradient estimation. We identify two deficiencies: (1) path-level rewards decompose into step-level rewards with positive mean, creating a length-dependent bias that causes gradients to favor path extension over meaningful exploration; (2) weighting each step by the entire path-level reward ignores the decomposition structure, leading to high gradient variance. To rectify these two deficiencies, we propose an effective RL framework ProRL with two novel mechanisms for proactive recommendation. First, Stepwise Reward Centering subtracts expected rewards to neutralize length-dependent bias, ensuring that path extension yields zero expected gradient signal. Second, Position-Specific Advantage Estimation leverages the reward decomposition structure to compute step-dependent baselines, reducing gradient variance. Together, these mechanisms yield policy gradients that precisely target path quality. Our experiments on three real-world datasets demonstrate that ProRL significantly outperforms state-of-the-art PRSs. Our code is available at https://github.com/hongruhou89/ProRL.

</details>


### [274] [Compositional Generalization in Autoregressive Models via Logit Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28304)
*Aakash Kumar,Maria Sofia Bucarelli,Emanuele Natale*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于因子化条件假设的自回归模型组合策略，在理论上证明了该组合方式能有效隔离不同模型组件的影响，从而在保持组合稳定性的同时实现复杂行为的融合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在组合不同任务学习到的行为或技能方面仍面临巨大挑战。现有研究缺乏关于如何有效地将多个自回归模型组合成一个协同系统、并保证组合行为可控且稳定的系统性理论支持。

Method: 提出了一种受扩散模型组合方法启发的新型自回归系统组合策略。利用“因子化条件（factorized-conditionals）”假设，从理论上推导并证明了该策略的投影特性，并通过数学推导验证了该特性在特征空间重参数化及长度泛化场景下的稳健性。

Result: 研究证明了在因子化条件假设下，组合后的模型是投影性的，能够有效避免不同组件模型间的相互干扰。此外，研究还通过特征空间定理和长度泛化分析，确定了模型组合在重参数化和不同生成长度下保持稳定性的边界条件。

Conclusion: 本文通过“因子化条件假设”，为自回归模型的组合提供了一个具有数学基础的理论框架。证明了在特定条件下，模型组合具有投影性（即各组件保持对各自子空间的控制），并在特征空间中具有稳定性。这些发现为理解大语言模型如何融合不同任务能力及模型合并的有效性提供了重要的理论依据，指出了模型交互保持稳定的必要条件。

Abstract: Composing autoregressive models remains a core challenge in understanding how large language models can combine behaviors or skills learned across tasks. We introduce a new and principled composition strategy for autoregressive systems, inspired by composition methods developed for diffusion models. Under a factorized-conditionals assumption, we show that the resulting composition is projective: each component model preserves control over its own designated subspace of the output distribution avoiding interference between models. This property is further preserved under smooth reparameterizations of the output space, yielding a feature-space theorem. Finally, we show that composition preserves length-generalizing behavior when the factorization assumptions and component guarantees hold uniformly at the target length. These results provide a principled understanding of when model composition and merging succeed in autoregressive systems and identify conditions under which their interactions remain stable.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模随机优化算法基准测试中，确定为了保证结果可靠性所需的最少重复运行次数至关重要，但传统的盲目重复会导致巨大的计算成本浪费，研究旨在通过机器学习自动判断何时已收集到足够证据，从而实现效率与可靠性的平衡。

Method: 研究人员利用Nevergrad在COCO基准测试中产生的13.2万次运行数据，提取了包括统计特征、无能量特征、形状与稳定性特征在内的23个维度。通过基于这些特征训练分类器，预测自适应启发式算法给出的“所需运行次数估计”是否可靠，重点优化了对不可靠估计的识别能力（通过少数类召回率进行评估）。

Abstract: In large-scale benchmarking of stochastic optimization algorithms, the key challenge is no longer whether repeated runs are needed for reliability, but how to determine when sufficient evidence has been collected without incurring unnecessary computational cost. We study a learning-based extension of a recent empirical online heuristic that adaptively estimates the required number of runs using outlier handling and skewness-based symmetry checks. Using annotated outcomes from 132{,}000 Nevergrad runs on COCO (24 problems in 20 dimensions, 10 instances each, 11 optimizers), we train classifiers on 23 statistical, energy-free, and shape and stability features to predict whether a run-number estimate is reliable, prioritizing detection of incorrect estimates via minority-class recall. We evaluate reliability prediction using a within-configuration learning setup, where models are trained and tested on data sharing the same optimizer. The results show that run-number reliability can be learned in a within-configuration scenario, enabling detection of unreliable estimates with high minority-class recall, although performance remains limited by the restricted data diversity within fixed configurations.

Abstract: When generating outputs for domains with specific validity constraints (e.g., a program should compile), LLMs often fail in a small number of focused ways: for example, by using Python function names when generating TypeScript. We observe that these error patterns can be represented using a small number of constraints that can be learned in practice. We propose \emph{prefix filters}, which are per-domain-and-LLM symbolic functions, as objects to capture the error patterns, Palla as an algorithm to learn prefix filters efficiently in practice, and implement Palla. Prefix filters learned by Palla i) help us quantitatively analyze the error patterns of LLMs, and ii) can be used to constrain the outputs of a model via constrained sampling algorithms. For example, Palla boosts compile rates for Qwen2.5-1.5B on TypeScript generation, by over 60%, allowing Qwen2.5-1.5B to achieve similar performance to Llama3.1-8B unconstrained.
