### [313] [Ocean4Rec: Offline LLM-Derived OCEAN Profiles for Request-Time VOD Reranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27429)
*Wonkyun Kim,Sehyun Bae,Kwanki Ahn,Mungyu Bae,Saeun Choi,Soyeon You,Chandra Prabhakar,Sehyun Kim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Ocean4Rec通过将LLM的使用从在线推理转为离线特征工程，将大五人格（OCEAN）心理维度引入推荐重排序，在保障系统低延迟的同时显著提升了推荐准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业级视频点播（VOD）系统对延迟高度敏感，现有的“LLM作为重排序器”方案因反复执行提示构建、推理和解析，导致高延迟、高计算成本及难以保障的系统吞吐量，限制了其在大规模在线场景的部署。

Method: 提出Ocean4Rec重排序层：1. 离线阶段：利用LLM分析元数据，将物品映射至大五人格（OCEAN）维度；用户画像通过近期交互记录的时间衰减聚合生成。2. 在线阶段：舍弃实时LLM推理，仅对预计算的OCEAN评分、基础推荐分值及物品时效性进行数值化合并与重排序。

Result: 在三星智能电视VOD数据集上测试，相比基准模型（Base+Recency），Ocean4Rec在NDCG@20指标上，对NCF生成器提升了7.6%，对LightGCN生成器提升了61.5%；对LightGCN的HR@20指标提升达67.3%。

Conclusion: Ocean4Rec证明了通过离线构建基于心理学模型（OCEAN）的物品与用户画像，可以有效提升推荐系统的准确性，同时避免了实时调用大语言模型（LLM）带来的高延迟与复杂计算开销，是工业级推荐系统在性能与效果平衡上的理想选择。

Abstract: Industrial video-on-demand (VOD) recommenders need richer content understanding, but LLM-as-reranker designs repeat prompt construction, token generation, model invocation, output parsing, and fallback handling for each request. In high-volume latency-sensitive services, these request-time operations complicate throughput planning, tail-latency control, capacity isolation, and predictable operation. This paper presents Ocean4Rec, a reranking layer that uses an LLM only offline to materialize item OCEAN profiles from content metadata. Items are mapped into Openness, Conscientiousness, Extraversion, Agreeableness, and Neuroticism scores, while user profiles are built by time-decayed aggregation of recently clicked and deep-linked items in the same five-dimensional space. At request time, Ocean4Rec joins precomputed item profiles, user profiles, base recommender scores, and catalog recency, then performs numeric reranking without an LLM call. On anonymized Samsung Smart TV VOD logs, same-candidate Top1000 temporal-holdout offline evaluations show that Ocean4Rec improves NDCG@20 over a stronger non-OCEAN Base+Recency ordering by 7.6% for an NCF generator and 61.5% for a LightGCN generator. HR@20 is inconclusive for NCF and improves by 67.3% for LightGCN, reflecting sparse exact-item replay labels and the strength of recency as an industrial baseline. The result should be read as offline replay evidence for a bounded auxiliary content-taste feature that preserves the deployability advantage of a request-time-LLM-free serving path.

</details>


### [314] [Prominence-Stratified Failure Modes in Retrieval-Augmented Commercial Recommendation: A 37,000-Run Audit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27439)
*Will Jack,Noah Lehman,Keller Maloney,Sarah Xu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了AI助手作为推荐引擎的运作逻辑，发现不同知名度的品牌在AI生成结果中的可见性与转化率差异巨大，证明了传统的SEO策略已失效，品牌需根据市场地位制定精细化的AI营销战略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI助手（如ChatGPT和Claude）正从搜索引擎转型为推荐引擎，它们直接提供品牌建议而非链接列表。营销人员迫切需要理解在这一新范式下，品牌如何通过内容、定位和产品匹配度来影响AI的推荐决策，而非仅仅追求传统的搜索引擎排名。

Method: 研究团队进行了约37,000次模型运行测试，涵盖4种模型配置、215个商业导向提示词及19个行业。研究通过包含533个品牌的参考目录（按知名度分为5个阶梯，即L1至L5）作为基准，对比分析了不同知名度品牌在AI推荐结果中的出现频率及转化表现。

Result: 研究发现不同阶梯品牌的失败模式各异：L1领军品牌几乎总是出现，但转化率并不高（25-41%），主要受限于差异化能力；L2挑战者转化率最高（37-52%）；L3品牌处于市场拐点，面临模型偏见和 persona 影响；L4及L5品牌则遭遇严重的“隐形”危机，近半数在测试中从未被提及。

Conclusion: AI已成为一种全新的商业推荐引擎，传统的SEO策略不再适用。品牌必须根据自身在行业中的地位（知名度阶梯）采取差异化的营销策略：行业领军者需强化品牌差异化以提升推荐转化率，而中小型品牌则需重点解决被AI模型“忽略”的可见性问题。不存在通用的优化公式，营销投入必须与品牌所处的阶梯位置精确对齐。

Abstract: AI assistants like ChatGPT and Claude are recommendation engines, not search engines: they answer commercial queries by directly nominating brands rather than returning a list of links. Marketing to AI is therefore a broader problem than "show up in search" -- positioning, content, and product fit matter as much as discoverability. We audit ~37,000 production runs across four model configurations and 215 commercially-framed prompts spanning 19 sectors, evaluated against a 533-brand reference catalog stratified into five prominence tiers (L1 category leaders to L5 regional players) sourced from external authority lists. The ladder proxies a brand's awareness footprint within its sector, not revenue or market share. The failure mode differs sharply by tier. L1 brands appear in nearly every relevant retrieval but win only 25-41% of the recommendation slots they reach -- the leverage is differentiation, not visibility. L2 challengers carry the highest conversion rates of any tier (37-52%) but lose to persona-mediated substitution on the Anthropic models. L3 mid-market brands are the inflection level: aggregate coverage drops to 88%, conversion to 34-40%, and persona effects peak. L4 specialists and L5 regional players face catastrophic invisibility -- 48-52% never surface in any of the 37,000 runs. No uniform optimization recipe wins; the right marketing investment depends on where the brand sits on the prominence ladder.

</details>


### [315] [Paraphrase Brittleness in Production Retrieval-Augmented Commercial Recommendation: Reproducibility Below the Rerun-Stability Baseline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27440)
*Will Jack,Noah Lehman,Keller Maloney,Sarah Xu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: AI助理对提示词的措辞极其敏感，导致基于单一提示词的“AI品牌可见度”追踪指标在统计上极不稳定且存在偏差。该研究表明，目前的商业监测方法无法准确反映真实的市场可见度，迫切需要开发更稳健的评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI搜索和AI助理的普及，企业开始关注其在AI中的品牌可见度（AEO/GEO）。本研究旨在揭示：AI模型对用户查询措辞的细微变化是否过于敏感，以及当前衡量品牌AI可见度的指标（即通过固定提示词计数）是否具有科学有效性。

Method: 研究人员对OpenAI和Anthropic的模型进行了约6,000次同义改写测试（paraphrase runs）及约6,000次相同提示词的对照测试。通过计算Jaccard相似度来衡量不同措辞（包括修辞调整和增加约束条件）下品牌推荐结果的重合度，并分析了模型推理努力程度对结果的影响。

Result: 研究发现，AI生成的品牌推荐对用户措辞极其敏感，甚至超过了对核心购买意图的关注。同义改写的推荐结果重合度（Jaccard系数）仅为0.135-0.288，远低于相同提示词下的重合度（0.50-0.61）。增加模型的推理努力程度并不能显著降低这种差异。这意味着，当前品牌追踪工具观测到的所谓“品牌可见度”波动，主要源于选用的提示词措辞而非模型本身的偏好。

Conclusion: 针对大语言模型生成的品牌推荐，现有的“提示词即时追踪”（Prompt-by-prompt mention tracking）衡量方式在结构上是不稳定的。由于AI对提示词措辞高度敏感，单一或少量提示词无法代表真实的品牌可见度。未来的评价指标需要从基于提示词的测量转向更稳健、更具概括性的评估方法。

Abstract: Small changes to how a buyer phrases a question -- "best CRM" vs "top CRM" vs "best CRM for a SaaS startup" -- produce substantially different brand recommendations from AI assistants. Across ~6,000 paraphrase runs and ~6,000 same-prompt rerun controls on OpenAI and Anthropic models, the recommendation-set similarity (Jaccard) between two paraphrases of the same underlying buying intent is 0.288 for cosmetic rewordings (clustered 95% CI [0.215, 0.361]) and 0.135 for constraint-adding rewordings ([0.098, 0.175], pooling region/language and specificity-ladder axes) -- both far below the 0.50-0.61 same-prompt rerun baseline. The prompt string, not the underlying buyer intent, is the dominant input to which brands surface. Increasing reasoning effort does not narrow the gap (bounded by +/-0.05). This is a direct challenge to an increasingly popular AEO/GEO practice. Tracking a brand's "AI visibility" by counting brand mentions over a fixed set of prompts produces a metric whose dominant source of variance is which paraphrase the tracker happens to issue, not the model's behavior toward the brand: the same buyer intent in two natural paraphrases produces recommendation sets that overlap 14-29% in Jaccard versus 50-61% for same-prompt reruns. Sampling more paraphrases per intent reduces the artifact in principle, and efficient multi-prompt evaluation methods exist in the academic literature, but the natural buyer-phrasing space is much larger than the benchmark-scale prompt sets those methods have been validated on, and far beyond what any commercial tracker issues per brand-intent combination. Prompt-by-prompt mention tracking is therefore structurally unstable as a unit of measurement; meaningful improvement likely requires a different unit rather than a larger prompt set.

</details>


### [316] [Memory-Based vs. Context-Only Conditioning Produces Distinct Behavioral Patterns in Stateful Personalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27389)
*Junsoo Park,Youssef Medhat,Htet Phyo Wai,Ploy Thajchayapong,Ashok K. Goel*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该研究对比了教育推荐系统中“上下文”与“记忆”两种条件设置，发现前者更关注即时问题响应，后者更具个性化历史依赖性，并强调了行为层面诊断对评估个性化推荐系统的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨在面向教师的教育推荐系统中，不同的条件设置（Conditioning Context）如何塑造个性化行为，以理解系统在响应当前教学问题与考虑长期学习者历史之间的权衡。

Method: 研究采用了对比实验法，将基于当前学生问题的上下文条件设置与基于持久性学习者信息的记忆型条件设置进行了比较；并通过偏差相关性分析和成对统计检验来评估推荐系统的行为差异。

Result: 结果显示，基于上下文的推荐表现出更强的针对当前问题的响应能力，而基于记忆的推荐则表现出依赖历史的行为，能够在相同输入下产生针对不同学习者的差异化推荐；教师评估反馈表明这些推荐具有良好的可解释性和可操作性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，嵌入式相似度度量能够有效捕捉对当前问题的响应性，但无法完全表征基于学习者历史的个性化，因此有必要采用基于行为层面的诊断方法来深入探究不同条件设置（上下文与记忆）的影响。

Abstract: We study how conditioning context shapes personalization behavior in a teacher-facing educational recommender system. We compare contextual conditioning based on the current student question with memory-based conditioning using persistent learner information. Using deviation correlation and paired statistical tests, we find that contextual recommendations exhibit stronger question-level responsiveness, while memory-based recommendations exhibit history-dependent behaviors, including learner-specific differentiation under identical input. Teacher-facing evaluation signals suggest these recommendations are interpretable and actionable. These results indicate that embedding-based similarity metrics capture responsiveness to the current question but do not characterize personalization grounded in learner history, motivating behavior-level diagnostics for studying conditioning effects.

</details>


### [317] [FD-RAG: Federated Dual-System Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27432)
*Tianhao Gao,Kai Yang,Yiyang Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: FD-RAG是一个为边缘环境设计的联邦检索增强生成框架，通过在设备端构建紧凑超图记忆并结合按需推理机制，在保障隐私的同时，显著提升了资源受限场景下的检索准确率并大幅降低了延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统多假设知识集中化且算力充足，但在边缘环境下，知识分布在不同设备且存在隐私限制，重复调用LLM代价昂贵，因此迫切需要一种去中心化的、轻量级的RAG解决方案。

Method: 提出一种名为FD-RAG的联邦双系统框架：1) 构建语义感知自适应超图并将知识提炼为紧凑的QA记忆；2) 设计双系统推理，通过直接记忆匹配处理常见查询，仅在必要时调用LLM；3) 采用联邦学习策略，在不共享原始数据的前提下跨设备聚合记忆，并提供收敛性理论保证。

Result: 在问答基准测试中，FD-RAG将准确率提升了7.8%，并将推理延迟降低了8.4倍；同时在理论上证明了其超图学习算法具有O(1/ε²)的收敛速率。

Conclusion: FD-RAG 通过联邦超图学习与双系统推理架构，有效解决了边缘计算环境下知识碎片化、隐私敏感及计算资源受限的难题，为去中心化环境下的检索增强生成提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) has emerged as a paradigm for grounding large language models in external knowledge, yet most existing RAG systems assume centralized knowledge access and ample computation. These assumptions break down in edge environments, where knowledge is fragmented across devices, raw data cannot be shared, and repeated LLM calls are prohibitively expensive. We propose FD-RAG, a federated dual-system RAG framework that decouples lightweight memory access from on-demand LLM reasoning for decentralized deployment. Specifically, FD-RAG learns semantic-aware adaptive hypergraphs over local corpora and distills them into compact QA memories. At inference time, it answers well-covered queries via direct memory matching and invokes LLM-based reasoning only when necessary, while tracing retrieved memories to hypergraph-grounded evidence. To mitigate cross-device knowledge fragmentation, FD-RAG aggregates anonymized memories across devices without exposing raw documents. Experiments on QA benchmarks show that FD-RAG improves accuracy by up to 7.8\% while reducing latency by 8.4$\times$ compared with strong local and federated baselines. We also provide theoretical analysis establishing an $\mathcal{O}(1/ε^{2})$ convergence rate for the proposed hypergraph learning, supporting its tractable deployment in edge settings.

</details>


### [318] [RE-TRIANGLE: Does TRIANGLE Enable Multimodal Alignment Beyond Cosine Similarity in Retrieval?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27436)
*Arijit Ghosh,Aritra Bandyopadhyay,Chiranjeev Bindra,Jingfen Qiao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究对TRIANGLE多模态对齐框架进行了复现性分析，确认了其在零样本检索中的有效性，但也揭示了该方法在模型训练初期存在优化不稳定问题，并指出几何对齐带来的性能提升存在领域依赖性和泛化能力受限的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的多模态对齐策略多采用两两匹配方式，忽略了外围模态（如视频和音频）之间的相互一致性，导致存在“几何盲区”。作者旨在通过TRIANGLE框架，利用模态三元组的几何约束来实现更全面的模态对齐。

Method: 研究人员对TRIANGLE框架进行了可重复性验证，通过在合成数据集上进行实验分析，评估了将模态三元组区域最小化作为几何约束的效果，并对比了不同损失函数（如Data-Text Matching损失）与余弦正则化对模型训练稳定性的影响。

Result: 研究证实TRIANGLE在零样本检索任务中表现优于基线模型，Recall@1提升高达8.7个百分点；然而，未能成功复现原始论文中从零开始训练的结果，分析指出几何对齐与匹配损失联合优化时存在不稳定性；此外，余弦正则化主要对文本到视频的检索有稳定作用，且领域微调会增加几何对齐的收益，但代价是降低了模型的跨数据集泛化能力。

Conclusion: TRIANGLE框架通过几何对齐有效地提升了多模态检索性能，但其在从零开始训练时存在优化不稳定性。研究表明，几何对齐的收益具有领域依赖性，且在增强特定领域表现的同时可能削弱模型的跨数据集泛化能力。未来研究需进一步关注几何约束与基础匹配损失函数之间的平衡与稳定性。

Abstract: Multimodal alignment is critical for bridging the semantic gap in information retrieval. However, traditional pairwise strategies introduce a geometric blind spot: while they align anchor modalities (e.g., text) with others, they lack constraints to enforce mutual consistency between peripheral modalities (e.g., video and audio). The TRIANGLE framework addresses this by minimizing the area of modality triplets on a hypersphere to enforce holistic alignment. In this reproducibility study, we verify the robustness of this geometric objective for retrieval tasks. We confirm that TRIANGLE outperforms pairwise baselines in zero-shot settings, achieving Recall@1 gains of up to +8.7 points, though benefits are domain-dependent. However, we fail to reproduce the reported learning-from-scratch results. Analysis using a synthetic toy dataset attributes this to instability when jointly optimizing geometric alignment with Data-Text Matching (DTM) loss. Furthermore, we find that cosine regularization primarily stabilizes text-to-video retrieval, and fine-tuning with domain supervision amplifies geometric benefits but reduces cross-dataset generalization. Our findings support the efficacy of geometric alignment while highlighting critical optimization sensitivities. Code available at https://github.com/ARIJIT00171/RE-TRIANGLE.

</details>


### [319] [A Systematic Evaluation of Retrieval-Augmented Generation and Language Models for Space Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27444)
*Ruben Belo,Marta Guimarães,Cláudia Soares*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文评估了RAG技术在空间操作领域的应用，证实了其通过整合大模型与检索技术，能显著优化知识处理流程，为复杂航天决策提供可靠支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着空间活动规模的急剧扩大，技术文档、操作指南及科学文献呈爆发式增长，导致空间操作中的信息处理与决策支持面临严峻挑战，亟需能够高效处理异构信息源的先进工具。

Method: 系统性地评估了多种RAG流程，对比分析了不同的检索策略、嵌入模型（embedding models）以及大语言模型生成结果，以探讨其对信息准确性、相关性及可靠性的影响。

Result: 研究表明，RAG流程能够有效增强知识获取能力，降低空间操作中的不确定性，并为复杂任务下的决策制定提供有力支持。

Conclusion: 检索增强生成（RAG）技术通过将大语言模型与专业知识库有效集成，能够显著提升空间操作领域的信息获取效率与准确性，是解决复杂航天任务中信息过载与决策支持难题的有效途径。

Abstract: The rapid expansion of space activities has led to an unprecedented accumulation of technical documentation, operational guidelines, and scientific literature, creating challenges for timely decision-making in space operations. Effective management in space operations requires tools capable of efficiently processing vast and heterogeneous information sources. This paper systematically evaluates the performance of Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) pipelines, combining Large Language Models (LLMs) with information retrieval techniques for extracting and synthesizing actionable knowledge from domain-specific documents. We compare various retrieval strategies, embedding models, and LLM answers to assess their impact on information accuracy, relevance, and reliability. Our results demonstrate that RAG pipelines can significantly enhance knowledge access, reduce uncertainty, and support decision-making in complex space operations.

</details>

Result: RAGe能够有效帮助研究人员识别最适合其操作需求的领域特定RAG配置，在保证生成质量的同时显著优化计算效率，并支持在受限硬件资源下的快速原型开发。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的RAGe框架通过整合性能遥测与智能组件推荐，有效降低了开发高性能RAG应用的门槛，使得在消费级硬件上实现领域特定优化成为可能。

Abstract: Deploying Large Language Model (LLM) applications, particularly those relying on Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), remains challenging due to high computational demands, outdated knowledge bases, and the need to manually select optimal pipeline components. In this work, we propose a modular framework for benchmarking and guiding the efficient development of RAG applications by focusing on resource telemetry and component recommendation, suggesting the best components for a domain-specific dataset. Our approach leverages core techniques in LLM applications, including document chunking, vector databases, embedding models, and retrievers, to evaluate trade-offs among accuracy, efficiency, and scalability. By directly correlating retrieval and generation quality with underlying hardware constraints, RAGe supports researchers to identify the most effective, domain-specific RAG setups for their specific operational needs, facilitating rapid prototyping even on consumer-grade hardware.

### [321] [Checking Fact with Better Retrieval: Dynamic Contrastive Learning for Evidence Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27449)
*Zhongtian Hua,Yi Luo,Meijia Yu,Yingjie Han*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态事实核查中检索证据“语义相似但相关性弱”的问题，本文提出DACLR方法。该方法利用MLLM提取事件级特征，并通过两阶段检索和动态自适应对比学习，实现了语义与事件相关性的精准匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用的多模态检索方法主要基于语义相似度，导致检索到的证据虽然在语义上相似，但与事实核查的真实相关性不足，从而影响下游的声明验证效果。

Method: 1. 预处理：利用多模态大语言模型（MLLM）将证据和声明统一转换为文本模态，并提取事件级特征。
2. 检索框架：采用“召回-重排序”的两阶段检索策略。
3. 优化策略：基于InfoNCE损失设计了语义和事件两个层面的三种损失函数，并引入三种硬负样本挖掘策略。
4. 动态调整：通过批内样本的准确性监督信号，动态调整不同损失函数的权重，实现语义与事件相关性的平衡学习。

Result: 实验结果表明，DACLR方法显著提升了证据检索的准确性。通过消融实验验证了该方法中动态自适应对比学习机制和事件感知优化策略的有效性，证明了其在多模态证据检索领域的领先优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DACLR方法通过引入事件级特征提取和动态自适应对比学习机制，有效解决了多模态事实核查中证据检索相关性差的问题。实验证明该方法在多模态证据检索任务中具有显著优势。

Abstract: In the field of multimodal fact checking, the accuracy of retrieving evidence from different modalities has a significant impact on the downstream claim verification process. Existing general multimodal retrieval methods are often constructed based on semantics, resulting in the retrieved evidence being similar but not relevant to the claim. This paper proposes a \textbf{D}ynamic \textbf{A}daptive \textbf{C}ontrastive \textbf{L}earning method for evidence \textbf{R}etrieval called DACLR to address these issues. DACLR first uses a Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) to uniformly convert multimodal evidence and claims into text modalities, and extracts the features of these information at event level. Then, it conducts evidence retrieval through a two-stage retrieval method of recall-rerank. DACLR enhances the model's event perception ability of the retrieval stage by optimizing the contrastive loss and mining hard negative samples. Specifically, DACLR designs three loss functions at two levels (semantic and event) based on the InfoNCE loss.Corresponding to these, three sets of hard negative sample candidates are set up. The model dynamically adjusts the ratio based on the accuracy supervision signal of intra-batch samples, allowing the model to learn the correlation between claims and positive samples at the event level without forgetting the semantic retrieval ability. Extensive comparison and ablation experiments demonstrates the effectiveness of DACLR and its internal optimization methods. Further research also prove the advantages of DACLR in the field of multimodal evidence retrieval.

</details>


### [322] [Eliot: Interactively $\underline{E}$xploring Fast-Changing Scientific $\underline{Li}$terature Trends with $\underline{O}$nline Da$\underline{t}$a and Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27610)
*Bernardo A. Denkvitts,Nitin Gupta,Biplav Srivastava*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Eliot是一个创新的交互式系统，旨在帮助研究人员通过查询时实时聚类和时间分布可视化，追踪和理解快速变化的科学研究领域，其核心优势在于提供透明、可审计的文献演变分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着科学出版物的爆炸式增长，现有的搜索和基于大模型的摘要工具往往缺乏对文献语料选择、组织逻辑以及时间演变模式的透明度，导致研究人员难以有效追踪快速变化的技术领域。

Method: 该系统采用模块化流程：1. 基于用户查询实时检索arXiv论文；2. 利用MiniLM嵌入模型对论文标题和摘要进行表征；3. 使用UMAP进行降维；4. 通过凝聚聚类（Agglomerative Clustering）算法对语料进行主题聚类并提取关键词；5. 对各主题进行时间分布可视化呈现。研究还通过离线实验对比了不同算法组合的性能指标。

Result: 离线评估确定了“MiniLM+UMAP(10维)+凝聚聚类”为最佳实践配置；在用户研究中，85%的参与者认为聚类标签具有明确的意义；专家评估表明该系统在提供快速变化技术领域的可审计概览方面具有极高价值。

Conclusion: Eliot通过结合实时聚类与时间分布可视化，为研究人员提供了一种可审计、可交互的科学文献探索工具。该研究证明了在自动化文献分析中，基于查询的实时处理方案优于传统的手工分类，能有效帮助学者追踪并理解快速发展的技术领域。

Abstract: The rapid growth of scientific publishing has made it increasingly difficult to track how fast-moving areas evolve. Search engines and LLM-based assistants retrieve or summarize papers, but often hide how the corpus was selected, organized, or connected to temporal patterns. We present $\texttt{Eliot}$, a publicly deployed interactive system for traceable exploration of evolving scientific literature. Motivated by two studies on Large Language Models (LLMs) and Automated Planning and Scheduling (APS), $\texttt{Eliot}$ generalizes literature-evolution analysis beyond hand-built taxonomies and domain-specific scripts. Given explicit query terms and filters, it retrieves arXiv papers at query time, represents each paper by title and abstract, clusters the corpus into themes, assigns representative keywords, and visualizes each cluster's publication-year distribution. We evaluate $\texttt{Eliot}$ as both an applied system and an interactive research aid. An offline configuration study across eight arXiv domains compares document representations, dimensionality reduction methods, and clustering algorithms using intrinsic clustering and topic-coherence metrics; the results support MiniLM embeddings with 10-dimensional UMAP and Agglomerative Clustering as a practical default. A scenario-based survey and expert focus group assess interpretability and use contexts: participants rated cluster labels as meaningful in 85% of scenario responses, and feedback indicated that $\texttt{Eliot}$ is most valuable for auditable overviews of rapidly changing technical areas. These results suggest that query-time clustering and temporal inspection can complement search and generation tools by helping researchers inspect and refine the evidence behind literature trends.

</details>


### [323] [Fine-Tuned LLM as a Complementary Predictor Improving Ads System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27856)
*Hui Yang,Daiwei He,Kevin Jiang,Taejin Park,Kungang Li,Jiajun Luo,Yuying Chen,Xinyi Zhang,Sihan Wang,Haoyu He,Yu Liu,Lakshmi Manoharan,David Xue,Shubham Barhate,Runze Su,Duna Zhan,Ling Leng,Siping Ji,Jinfeng Zhuang,Alice Wu,Leo Lu,Han Sun,Zhifang Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在大规模工业广告系统中应用大模型的新范式：将大模型用作“广告主预测器”，通过提供高价值的辅助先验信息来增强现有召回和排序系统的性能，并在实际生产环境中取得了显著的业务收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在各个领域表现出色，但在大规模广告和生产级推荐系统中应用大模型的案例仍然稀缺。现有方法（如生成式检索、后期重排序、辅助信号增强）各有限制，需要一种能够高效结合大模型知识与大规模工业推荐系统需求的实用方案。

Method: 研究者引入了一种互补的新范式：利用微调后的开源大语言模型，不直接进行端到端推荐或仅作排序，而是将其作为“广告特定的辅助预测器”。该模型基于用户画像和历史行为，预测用户可能感兴趣的广告主，并将这些预测结果作为先验信息补充到现有的召回和排序流程中。

Result: 该方法在大规模生产级广告系统中实现了显著的离线性能提升，并在在线业务指标中取得了可衡量的正向增长，证明了该方法能够有效赋能检索与后期排序的端到端优化。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在大规模工业广告系统中，通过将大语言模型作为专门的辅助预测器（而非传统的排序器或生成器），可以有效利用其世界知识和预测能力，从而为推荐系统的检索和排序环节提供关键先验信息，是实现大模型在工业级推荐系统中落地的一种实用且高效的路径。

Abstract: Recommendation systems power engagement and monetization across feeds, ads, and short-video platforms, but translating the latest advances in Large Language Models into Recommendation Systems (RecSys) gains remains rare, particularly in advertising and production-scale real-world industry setups. Prior real-world LLM successes typically fall into three buckets: (a) generative retrieval that directly predicts the next items for candidate generation, (b) late-stage re-ranking that uses LLMs, and (c) auxiliary signal enrichment with LLMs. We introduce a complementary paradigm for ads: a fine-tuned open-source LLM used not as a ranker, but as an ads-specific ancillary predictor, forecasting likely advertisers from user profiles and histories. This LLM-driven advertiser prediction augments conventional candidate generation and provides informative priors to downstream ranking. Developed in a large-scale production advertising system, our approach produces substantial offline improvements and measurable online business impact, demonstrating that LLM world knowledge and predictive capacity can be efficiently harnessed. Beyond validating LLMs for ads applications, our results show that targeted ancillary predictions can unlock end-to-end gains across both retrieval and late-stage ranking, offering a practical path to LLM-enhanced recommendation at scale.

</details>


### [324] [Whose Name Comes Up? III: Persona Prompting Effects in LLM-Based Scholar Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28187)
*Annabella Sánchez-Guzmán,Lukas Eberhard,Denis Helic,Lisette Espín-Noboa*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该研究通过对43个大模型进行多维度审计，发现提示词设计（如地理位置、角色设定）对学术推荐的质量和公平性有重大影响，提示词设计应与模型选择同等重视。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对大语言模型作为学者推荐工具的研究主要局限于英语环境、单一学科且忽视了提示词（persona）的影响，导致人们对于模型输出差异性的来源缺乏深入理解。为了填补这一空白，研究旨在揭示模型选择与提示词设计如何共同影响学术推荐结果。

Method: 构建了一个多维基准测试框架，审计了43个大语言模型；通过系统性地改变提示词中的角色（语言、地理位置、任务角色）和上下文（研究领域、资历、推荐数量k），对比Semantic Scholar的数据，从技术质量（事实准确性、覆盖率）和社会代表性（多样性、平权）两个维度进行量化评估。

Result: 研究发现：1. 基础技术质量主要取决于模型选择；2. 事实准确性和平权性受上下文影响较大；3. 多样性则主要受地理位置提示词影响；4. 实验显示不同地区背景（如南非或日本）的提示词会导致显著不同的推荐偏见（如事实性降低或推荐结果趋向同质化）。

Conclusion: 提示词设计（尤其是角色设定）是影响大模型学术推荐质量的关键因素，其重要性不亚于模型本身。研究强调，在开发和评估大模型推荐系统时，必须将提示词设计纳入系统性审计范围，以确保学术推荐的公正性与准确性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as scholar recommenders, shaping who is seen as an expert in academia. Existing audits remain English-centric, single discipline, and persona-agnostic, leaving the source of output variability poorly understood. To this end, we propose a benchmark that disentangles the effects of model choice and prompt design on recommendations. We audit 43 LLMs by varying persona prompts (language, location, role-and-task) and context (field, seniority, k). Recommended scholars are compared against Semantic Scholar over six scientific disciplines to measure technical quality (factuality, coverage) and social representativeness (diversity, parity). Basic technical quality is driven by model choice, factuality and parity by context, and diversity by location. South Africa prompts yield less factual lists, while Japan prompts yield highly factual but homogeneous lists skewed toward highly productive scholars. Prompt design is thus a non-trivial axis of LLM-based scholar discovery and should be systematically audited alongside model choice.

</details>
